# cs.LG [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [Pointwise Metrics Mislead: An Evaluation Protocol for Multimodal Inverse Problems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22891)
*Mads H. Baattrup,Jörn Bach,Laurids Jeppe,Finn Labe,Alexander Grohsjean,Christian Schwanenberger,Peer Stelldinger*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文指出，在科学重建（scientific reconstruction）任务中，以逐点度量（pointwise metrics，如RMSE、MAE）主导的评估隐式假设“误差越小重建越好”，但该假设在多模态后验（multimodal posteriors）的逆问题（inverse problem）中结构性失效。基于全方差律（law of total variance），逐点估计器会产生比真实分布更窄的边缘谱（marginal spectrum），且该偏差独立于架构与数据规模。作者提出一个三部分评估协议，分别针对逐事件分布准确性、总体边缘准确性及不确定性可信度，并证明评估协议本身而非模型决定了科学结论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前科学重建评估普遍依赖逐点度量（pointwise metrics，如RMSE、MAE），隐含假设“误差越小重建越好”。作者指出该假设在具有多模态后验（multimodal posteriors）的逆问题（inverse problem）中结构性失效，导致评估偏差，且该偏差会压缩下游科学测量依赖的谱特征（spectral features），因此需要更完善的评估协议。

Method: 通过全方差律（law of total variance）从理论上证明，最小化MSE或MAE的逐点估计器（point estimators）产生的边缘谱（marginal spectrum）严格窄于真实后验。提出三部分评估协议：(1) 逐事件分布准确性——CRPS（CRPS）；(2) 总体边缘准确性——谱保真度诊断（spectrum-fidelity diagnostic）；(3) 不确定性可信度——基于覆盖率的校准（coverage-based calibration）。

Result: 在具有解析后验的合成基准（synthetic benchmark）和粒子物理学（particle physics）的真实多对一逆问题（many-to-one inverse problem）上，逐点度量与分布度量（distributional metrics）之间的模型排名发生逆转；校准（calibration）进一步区分了CRPS无法区分的架构。

Conclusion: 评估协议（evaluation protocol）而非模型本身，决定了科学结论（scientific conclusion）。逐点度量的主导地位在多模态逆问题中会产生系统性偏差，所提出的三部分协议能够更全面地评估重建质量。

Abstract: Evaluation in scientific reconstruction is dominated by pointwise metrics - RMSE, MAE, per-event resolution - under the implicit assumption that lower error means better reconstruction. We show that this assumption fails structurally for inverse problems with multimodal posteriors. By the law of total variance, point estimators trained to minimize MSE or MAE produce a marginal spectrum strictly narrower than the truth whenever the posterior has nonzero width. The resulting bias is independent of architecture, training, and dataset size, and it compresses precisely the spectral features - tails, modes, shapes - that downstream scientific measurements rely on. We propose a three-part evaluation protocol where each step targets a failure mode the others miss: per-event distributional accuracy via CRPS, population-level marginal accuracy via a spectrum-fidelity diagnostic, and uncertainty trustworthiness via coverage-based calibration. On a synthetic benchmark with an analytic posterior and on a realistic many-to-one inverse problem from particle physics, model rankings reverse between pointwise and distributional metrics, and calibration further separates architectures indistinguishable under CRPS. The evaluation protocol, not the model, determines the scientific conclusion.

</details>


### [2] [Reinforcement Learning for Microcanonical Graph Ensemble with Assortativity Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23285)
*Hoyun Choi,Junghyo Jo,Deok-Sun Lee*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出深度微正则图生成器（Deep Microcanonical Graph Generator, DMGG），一种基于强化学习（reinforcement learning, RL）的框架，通过保度重连（degree-preserving rewiring）精确实现指定的同配性（assortativity），从而生成硬约束图（hard-constrained graphs），避免了传统指数随机图模型（exponential random graph models, ERGMs）的繁琐参数调优，并将生成速度提升至少一个数量级，同时保持构型多样性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 网络结构如何决定功能是一个基本问题，但现有的图生成方法存在局限：正则方法（canonical approaches）如指数随机图模型（ERGM）仅在期望意义上施加约束，允许个体实现围绕目标波动；而微正则系综（microcanonical ensembles）虽能施加硬约束，但除固定度序列（degree sequence）外，缺乏实用的采样方法。

Method: DMGG采用强化学习（RL）框架，通过保度重连（degree-preserving rewiring）对给定图进行变换，以精确达到预设的同配性（assortativity）；其策略导向搜索（policy-guided search）最大程度地改变联合度矩阵（joint-degree matrix），取代了ERGM中熵主导的Metropolis-Hastings动力学。

Result: DMGG消除了穷举的参数调优，将生成速度提升至少一个数量级，同时保留了构型多样性（configurational diversity）；该方法可泛化至不同图规模、稀疏度（sparsity）和拓扑结构（topology），提供精确零模型（exact null models），从而允许定量分离聚类系数（clustering coefficient）等二次可观测量（secondary observables）。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，强化学习（RL）是一种实用且强大的硬约束图生成范式，为在无系综伪影（ensemble artifacts）条件下研究结构-功能关系开辟了新途径。

Abstract: How network structure determines function is a fundamental question, and it can be investigated by graph ensembles with precisely controlled structural properties. Canonical approaches, formulated as exponential random graph models (ERGMs), enforce constraints only in expectation, allowing individual realizations to fluctuate around the target. Conversely, microcanonical ensembles impose hard constraints exactly, but practical sampling methods beyond fixing the degree sequence have remained out of reach. Here we introduce the Deep Microcanonical Graph Generator (DMGG), a reinforcement learning (RL) framework that transforms any given graph through degree-preserving rewirings to exactly reach a prescribed assortativity, which characterizes the degree--degree correlation of adjacent nodes. Instead of relying on the entropically dominated Metropolis--Hastings dynamics of the ERGM, DMGG employs a policy-guided search that maximally alters the joint-degree matrix. This eliminates exhaustive parameter tuning and accelerates generation by at least an order of magnitude while preserving configurational diversity. As DMGG generalizes across various graph sizes, sparsities, and topologies, it provides exact null models that allow for the quantitative isolation of secondary observables, such as the clustering coefficient. These results establish RL as a practical and powerful paradigm for generating hard-constrained graphs, opening avenues to investigate structure-function relationships free from ensemble artifacts.

</details>


### [3] [Non-normal spectral signatures of instability in neural network training dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23476)
*Souvik Ghosh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文建立非厄米算子理论（non-Hermitian operator theory）作为分析深度网络训练不稳定性（loss spikes, oscillatory convergence, gradient pathologies）的新框架。研究表明，Adam和带动量的SGD的线性化更新算子具有本质非正态性（generic non-normality），并通过伪谱前兆界（pseudospectral precursor bound）和条件数κ(V)作为瞬态放大的预警指标，为理解自适应优化稳定性提供了诊断语言和基准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深度网络中的训练不稳定性（损失尖峰、震荡收敛、梯度病理）在经验上普遍存在，但缺乏严格的算子理论（operator-theoretic）解释。现有理论工具无法充分刻画这些现象的深层机制，亟需建立更系统的数学框架。

Method: 对于Adam，非正态性由Hessian矩阵与对角自适应预条件子之间的对易子（commutator）[H, M]控制；对于带动量的SGD，非正态性源于更新映射的增广状态空间结构。应用非正态稳定性理论（non-normal stability theory）推导保守的伪谱前兆界，以κ(V)作为瞬态放大的早期预警指标，并将更新算子的异常点（exceptional points）视为κ(V)→∞的极限情形。

Result: 在两层网络上的数值实验表明，谱半径ρ(J)无法区分稳定与不稳定的训练阶段，而κ(V)能将其分离约一个数量级。该结果补充了经典的尖锐度准则（sharpness criterion），提供了非正态放大的连续严重性度量。

Conclusion: 非厄米算子理论是用于神经网络优化稳定性分析的一个有用且尚未被充分探索的框架，为理解和诊断自适应优化稳定性提供了诊断语言和概念验证基准（proof-of-concept benchmark）。

Abstract: Training instabilities in deep networks - loss spikes, oscillatory convergence, and gradient pathologies - are empirically prevalent but lack a rigorous operator-theoretic explanation. We show that the linearized update operators for practically used optimizers are generically non-normal: for Adam, non-normality is controlled by the commutator [H, M] between the Hessian and the diagonal adaptive preconditioner, while for SGD with momentum it arises from the augmented state-space structure of the update map. Applying non-normal stability theory to these operators, we derive a conservative pseudospectral precursor bound in which κ(V) serves as an early-warning indicator of transient amplification even when the spectral radius remains below one, and we establish that exceptional points of the update operator appear as the κ(V) -> \infty limiting case of this framework. Numerical experiments on two-layer networks confirm that the spectral radius ρ(J) provides no separation between stable and unstable training phases while κ(V) separates them by approximately one order of magnitude, complementing the classical sharpness criterion with a continuous severity measure of non-normal amplification. These results establish non-Hermitian operator theory as a useful and underexplored framework for neural network optimization stability, offering a diagnostic language and proof-of-concept benchmark for understanding adaptive optimization stability.

</details>


### [4] [Preisach Attention: A Hysteretic Model of Sequential Memory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23603)
*Piotr Frydrych*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出 Preisach 注意力层（Preisach Attention Layer, PAL），一种基于数学物理中经典 Preisach 磁滞算子的序列建模架构。PAL 用二元中继算子（binary relay operator）替换 softmax 注意力机制，通过 O(1) 深度实现图灵完备性，并在理论上证明了 PAL 与标准 Transformer 在可计算函数类上不可比较（incomparable），且 PAL 仅对局部极值序列（local extrema）响应，具有速率独立性（rate-independence），推理开销为 O(n log n)。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 Transformer 的 softmax 注意力机制在长序列任务中计算成本高（O(n²)），且标准硬注意力 Transformer 需要 O(log n) 深度才能达到图灵完备性。此外，某些任务（如历史极值范围统计）对 Transformer 而言效率低下。研究者希望设计一种更高效且具备不同计算特性的序列建模架构。

Method: PAL 以经典 Preisach 磁滞算子为核心，用二元中继算子替代 softmax 注意力，每个算子由可学习的激活阈值和去激活阈值参数化，并通过维护一个局部极值堆栈（stack of local extrema）作为内部状态来编码输入历史。

Result: 1）单层 PAL-Transformer（O(1) 深度）在任意精度算术下是图灵完备的，而标准硬注意力 Transformer 需要 O(log n) 深度；2）PAL 与 Transformer 可计算的函数类不可比较——PAL 能以 O(1) 层计算历史范围统计（Transformer 需 O(log n) 层），但 Transformer 支持随机访问检索（random-access retrieval），PAL 无辅助状态则无法实现；3）极值堆栈构成所有速率无关泛函（rate-independent functional）输入历史的极小充分统计量（minimal sufficient statistic）。

Conclusion: PAL 适用于具有长情节记忆（long episodic memory）且对位置依赖较弱（weak positional dependence）的任务，其推理代价为 O(n log n)，显著低于标准注意力的 O(n²)。该架构为磁滞理论与深度学习架起了一座新的桥梁。

Abstract: We introduce the Preisach Attention Layer (PAL), a novel sequence modelling architecture grounded in the classical Preisach hysteresis operator from mathematical physics. PAL replaces the softmax attention mechanism with a binary relay operator parameterised by learned activation and deactivation thresholds, maintaining a stack of local extrema as its internal state. A single-layer PAL-Transformer with O(1) depth is Turing-complete under arbitrary precision arithmetic, achievable through simulation of a two-stack pushdown automaton -- in contrast to the O(log n) depth required by standard hard-attention transformers. Second, we prove that the function classes computable by PAL and by the transformer are incomparable: PAL computes historical range statistics in O(1) layers that require O(log n) layers for transformers, while transformers support random-access retrieval that PAL cannot perform without auxiliary state. The separating property is rate-independence -- PAL responds only to the sequence of local extrema, not to absolute token positions or temporal spacing. Third, we show that the extremum stack constitutes a minimal sufficient statistic of the input history for all rate-independent functionals, providing a formal analogue of the wiping property in classical hysteresis theory. PAL is thus an efficient architecture for tasks with long episodic memory and weak positional dependence, with O(n log n) total inference cost versus O(n^2) for standard attention.

</details>

# cond-mat.quant-gas [[Back]](#toc)

### [5] [Weak wave turbulence as a precursor to universal coarsening in a homogeneous Bose gas](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22906)
*Simon M. Fischer,Martin Gazo,Sebastian J. Morris,Nikolai Maslov,Haoyu Zhang,Jiří Etrych,Gevorg Martirosyan,Christoph Eigen,Zoran Hadzibabic*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文通过均匀玻色气体实验，结合弱波湍流（WWT）理论，揭示了孤立低能玻色气体在弛豫和凝聚过程中，不仅长程有序的传播（粗化）具有普适性，而且局部相干性的形成同样服从普适描述——表现为逆湍流级联导致的幂律动量分布，指数 γ=2.4(1)，输运时间 ∝ (na)^{-2}。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 孤立低能玻色气体的弛豫与凝聚是研究远离平衡多体动力学（far-from-equilibrium many-body dynamics）和长程有序（long-range order）涌现普适特征的理想平台。尽管长程有序传播阶段的普适粗化（coarsening）动力学已有较好理解，但局部相干性（local coherence）形成阶段是否也具有普适描述尚不清楚。

Method: 在具有可调相互作用的均匀玻色气体中，实验测量动量分布的时间演化与输运时间尺度，并与弱波湍流（weak wave turbulence, WWT）理论框架进行定量比较。

Result: 初始粒子向低动量区域的输运对应逆湍流级联（inverse turbulent cascade），其动量分布服从幂律形式，指数 γ=2.4(1)；输运时间正比于 (na)^{-2}，其中 n 为气体密度，a 为 s 波散射长度（s-wave scattering length）。

Conclusion: 局部相干性形成阶段同样具有普适描述，从而补充了从微观相干到宏观长程有序涌现的完整普适图像。

Abstract: Relaxation and condensation of an isolated low-energy Bose gas provide an ideal setting for the study of the universal features of far-from-equilibrium many-body dynamics and the emergence of long-range order. Conceptually, the emergence of such order involves two steps: the formation of local coherence, on a system-specific microscopic lengthscale, and the spreading of coherence, over lengthscales much larger than any microscopic scale. The latter is understood in terms of universal phase-ordering kinetics, or coarsening, characterized by an algebraic growth of the coherence length. Here, for a homogeneous Bose gas with tunable interactions, we show that the former also has a universal description, within the framework of weak wave turbulence (WWT). Specifically, the initial transport of particles to low momenta corresponds to an inverse turbulent cascade that is, in agreement with the WWT theory, characterized by a power-law momentum distribution, with exponent $γ= 2.4(1)$, and transport times ${\propto} (na)^{-2}$, where $n$ is the gas density and $a$ the $s$-wave scattering length.

</details>


### [6] [Quantum fluctuations in quartet superfluid of two-dimensional Fermi mixture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23267)
*Wei Wang,Yupeng Wang,Xiaoling Cui*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文研究了二维质量不平衡费米子混合物中四重超流（QSF）的量子涨落，通过引入高斯涨落理论成功描述了深束缚区对数依赖的状态方程，揭示了四重团簇作为复合玻色子的物理图像。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的超导/超流理论主要关注双粒子配对（库珀对，Cooper pair），而对于涉及四个费米子（一个轻费米子与三个重费米子）的高阶四重超流（QSF）系统中量子涨落的行为尚缺乏研究，尤其是在二维（2D）质量不平衡体系中。

Method: 在描述四体关联主导的系统中引入高斯涨落（Gaussian fluctuations），将这一理论框架从常规的配对超流推广至四重超流体系。

Result: 理论成功再现了二维深束缚区域中状态方程（equation of state）的对数依赖关系，表明四重团簇（quartet clusters）的行为类似于复合玻色子（composite bosons）。

Conclusion: 将高斯涨落理论从配对超流推广至四重超流，为理解具有任意高阶关联的一般费米子超流体系中的量子涨落提供了新的理论视角。

Abstract: We study quantum fluctuations in quartet superfluid (QSF) of two-dimensional (2D) fermion mixtures with mass imbalance. Here QSF is a high-order superfluid that corresponds to the condensation of ($1+3$) clusters, each consisting of a light fermion and three heavy ones. By incorporating the Gaussian fluctuations respecting dominant four-body correlations in this system, our theory successfully produces the logarithmic dependence of the 2D equation of state in the deep binding regime, thereby offering a correct physical picture of quartet clusters behaving as composite bosons. By extending the Gaussian fluctuation theory from pairing to quartet superfluids, our results shed light on quantum fluctuations in general fermion superfluids with arbitrarily high-order correlations.

</details>


### [7] [Time crystals in cavity-BEC systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23881)
*Jayson G. Cosme,Ludwig Mathey*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文综述了在腔-玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚（cavity-BEC）系统中预测并实现的三种时间晶体态（time crystalline states），通过最小少模模型（minimal few-mode models）和关联函数（correlation functions）对它们进行表征与区分，为光致动力学现象的量子模拟提供了蓝图。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 光致动力学态（light-induced dynamical states）的理解是科学中富有挑战性的追求；超冷原子系统在动力学量子模拟中通常采用破坏性读出（destructive readout），限制了详细分析，因此需要一种非破坏性、实时读出方案来深入研究动力学现象。

Method: 采用原子-腔系统（atom-cavity systems），通过腔的光子发射实现光子态的实时读出（real-time readout）；基于最小少模模型分别给出三种时间晶体态的示例；利用腔模（cavity mode）和凝聚体特征动量模（characteristic momentum modes）的关联函数对时间晶体态进行表征。

Result: 三种不同的时间晶体态在腔-玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚系统中被预测并实现；通过关联函数实现了对这些时间晶体态的清晰区分（clear distinction）。

Conclusion: 该综述所展示的研究序列为建立动力学现象的最小模型及其表征提供了一套可复用的蓝图（blueprint）。

Abstract: The understanding of light-induced dynamical states continues to be a challenging and fruitful pursuit of science. This pursuit is supported by quantum simulation of dynamical phenomena, e.g., in ultracold atom systems. Typically, ultracold atom dynamics are read out destructively, via time-of-flight imaging, limiting a detailed analysis. However, atom-cavity systems provide a real-time readout of the photonic state via photon emission from the cavity, making the system ideally suited for the simulation of dynamical phenomena. Here, we review three distinct time crystalline states, predicted and realized in a cavity-BEC system. We give an example for each of them, based on minimal few-mode models. We characterize the time crystalline states via correlation functions of the cavity mode, and characteristic momentum modes of the condensate. This supports a clear distinction between these time crystals. More generally, the sequence of studies reviewed here, serves as a blueprint for setting up minimal models and their characterization, for dynamical phenomena.

</details>

# hep-ex [[Back]](#toc)

### [8] [Continuous coherent spin-frequency metrology in storage rings via resonant beam-driven detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23013)
*Younggeun Kim,Themis Bowcock,Dmitry Budker,Giovanni Cantatore,Hooman Davoudiasl,Dmitry Denisov,Abhay Deshbande,Wolfram Fischer,Selcuk Haciomeroglu,Haixin Huang,David Kawall,on Kim,Ivan Koop,Valeri Lebedev,Jonathan Lee,William M. Morse,Cenap Ozben,Vincent Schoefer,Yannis K. Semertzidis,Eleftherios Skordis,Edward Stephenson,Vladimir Tishchenko,Nicholaos Tsoupas,Graziano Venanzoni,Joost Vossebeld,Peter Winter*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于共振读出（resonant readout）的非破坏性、相位相干（phase-coherent）极化测量方法，将储存环中的束流极化视为连续动力学观测量，通过自旋依赖的电磁场信号、高Q谐振器相位调制及背景抑制技术，实现自旋相干时间接近10^5秒的可扩展测量，为储存环电偶极矩（EDM）实验提供接近标准模型预期的灵敏度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有储存环极化测量技术依赖破坏性散射过程，无法实现连续非拦截的自旋演化跟踪，限制了统计灵敏度和系统控制能力。随着储存环精密测量对长时间尺度上相干集体自旋动力学监测的需求日益增长，亟需一种非破坏性、相位相干的新型极化测量方法。

Method: 该方法将储存束流极化作为连续动力学观测量。极化相对论性束流产生的自旋依赖电磁场在拾取电极上建立对称性选择的差分信号；该信号被转换为高Q谐振器的窄带相位调制，通过相干探针读取；同时利用几何对称性、螺旋度反转和同步解调（synchronous demodulation）抑制电荷主导的背景。受控自旋进动（spin-wheel operation）提供稳定相位参考，实现慢速自旋演化的相位相干检测。

Result: 结合优化晶格对称性和束流冷却，该方法可在现有加速器技术下将可用自旋相干时间扩展到接近10^5秒。读出方案支持基于最优斜率的T^{-3/2}统计缩放估计，消除了基于散射的极化测量固有的效率损失。对于储存环EDM实验，该组合可实现接近标准模型预期水平的灵敏度。

Conclusion: 该方法建立了储存环中集体自旋测量的一般性相位相干架构，将轴子暗物质搜索中的共振传感概念适配到带电粒子精密实验中，为储存环精密测量提供了新的技术路径。

Abstract: Precision measurements in storage rings are increasingly limited by the ability to monitor collective spin dynamics coherently over long time scales. Existing polarimetry techniques rely on destructive scattering processes that preclude continuous, non-intercepting tracking of spin evolution and constrain both statistical sensitivity and systematic control. Here we introduce a non-destructive, phase-coherent polarimetry method in which the stored beam polarization is treated as a continuous dynamical observable rather than a quantity inferred from scattering events. Spin-dependent electromagnetic fields generated by a polarized relativistic beam establish a symmetry-selected differential signal on pickup electrodes. This signal is transduced into a narrowband phase modulation of a high-Q resonator interrogated with a coherent probe, while dominant charge-induced backgrounds are rejected through geometric symmetry, helicity reversal, and synchronous demodulation. Controlled spin precession (spin-wheel operation) provides a stable phase reference enabling phase-coherent detection of slow spin evolution. Combined with optimized lattice symmetry and beam cooling, this approach can substantially extend the usable spin coherence time, with values approaching 10^5 s appearing realistic within existing accelerator technology. The resulting readout supports optimal slope-based estimation with T^{-3/2} statistical scaling while eliminating the efficiency penalties inherent to scattering-based polarimetry. For storage-ring EDM experiments, this combination enables sensitivity approaching the level expected within the Standard Model. More broadly, the method establishes a general phase-coherent architecture for collective spin measurements in storage rings, adapting resonant sensing concepts from axion dark-matter searches to charged-particle precision experiments.

</details>


### [9] [A search for the dark photon in the OKA experiment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23533)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 寻找无质量暗光子（massless dark photon）这一超出标准模型（Standard Model）的假设粒子，通过K⁺→π⁺π⁰γ̅衰变过程进行实验探测，检验暗物质候选粒子存在的可能性。

Method: 利用OKA探测器，该探测器暴露于U70质子同步加速器（U70 Proton Synchrotron）的17.7 GeV/c射频分离次级束流（RF separated secondary beam）中。采用高统计量的K⁺衰变数据样本，对末态中的稳定无质量不可见暗光子（massless invisible dark photon, γ̅）进行缺失质量搜索（missing mass search）。

Result: 未观测到具有统计显著性的信号，因此基于该过程的实际矩阵元（matrix element），在90%置信水平（confidence level）上给出了分支比（branching ratio, Br）的上限：Br<2.0×10⁻⁶。

Conclusion: 该结果为当前对这一假设衰变通道（K⁺→π⁺π⁰γ̅）的最佳上限，为无质量暗光子的存在设定了更严格的实验约束。

Abstract: A search for the massless dark photon in the decay $K^{+}\to π^{+}π^{0}\overline{{} γ}$ is performed with the OKA detector exposed to 17.7 GeV/c RF separated secondary beam of the U70 Proton Synchrotron. A high-statistics data sample of the $K^{+}$ decays is used for a missing mass search of the stable massless invisible dark photon ($\overlineγ$) in the final state. In the absence of a statistically valuable signal the upper limit on the branching ratio of the decay $Br<2.0\times10^{-6}$ is obtained with a 90% confidence level based on a realistic matrix element of the process. Currently, it is the best upper limit for this hypothetical decay channel.

### [10] [FPGA Acceleration of Matrix-Element Calculations for Monte Carlo Event Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23785)
*H. Gutiérrez Arance,F. Carrió,L. Fiorini,S. Folgueras,F. Hervàs Álvarez,P. Leguina López,A. Oyanguren,A. Valero,C. Vico Villalba*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文基于FPGA加速蒙特卡洛事件生成中的矩阵元计算，以MadGraph5_aMC@NLO为基准框架，实现了全流程加速（e⁺e⁻ → μ⁺μ⁻）和选择性色代数核加速（gg → tt̄+X），相比CPU和GPU方案在速度和能效上均取得显著提升，数值精度与CPU参考结果高度一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 蒙特卡洛事件生成（Monte Carlo event generation）是高能物理模拟中的核心计算瓶颈，传统CPU和GPU架构在能效和可扩展性方面面临挑战，需要探索FPGA等新型计算架构来实现高效加速。

Method: 采用两种互补方案：一是针对简单过程e⁺e⁻ → μ⁺μ⁻在AMD Alveo U250加速器上实现完整矩阵元工作流（matrix-element workflow）；二是针对复杂过程gg → tt̄+X，聚焦于色代数核（color-algebra kernels）的选择性加速，使用高层次综合（High-Level Synthesis）开发。

Result: 与MG5aMC框架中的CPU和GPU实现相比，FPGA方案实现了显著加速比（speedups）和大幅提升的能效（energy efficiency）；数值结果与CPU参考计算高度一致；资源分析表明数值表示（numerical representation）对FPGA可扩展性至关重要。

Conclusion: FPGA可作为高能物理中选定蒙特卡洛事件生成工作负载的竞争性计算架构，兼具高性能和低能耗优势。

Abstract: We present an FPGA-based study of matrix-element acceleration for Monte Carlo event generation, using MadGraph5_aMC@NLO as a benchmark framework. Two complementary scenarios are considered. First, we implement the full matrix-element workflow on an AMD Alveo U250 accelerator for the benchmark process $e^+e^- \to μ^+μ^-$, enabling an end-to-end evaluation of FPGA acceleration for a simple process. Second, for the more complex $gg \to t\bar{t}+X$ processes with increasing jet multiplicity, we investigate FPGA acceleration of the color-algebra kernels as a structured and scalable entry point for selective acceleration. In this second case, the reported speedups correspond to the isolated color-reduction kernel operating on precomputed amplitudes, rather than to the full matrix-element evaluation or the complete event-generation workflow. The proposed implementations are developed using High-Level Synthesis and are evaluated in terms of numerical accuracy, performance, energy efficiency, resource utilization, and scalability. Compared with CPU and GPU implementations available within the MG5aMC framework, the FPGA solutions achieve substantial speedups and significantly improved energy efficiency. For the considered benchmarks, the numerical results remain in close agreement with the corresponding CPU reference calculations, while the resource analysis highlights the importance of numerical representation in determining scalability on FPGA devices. These results support the use of FPGAs as a competitive architecture for selected Monte Carlo event-generation workloads in high-energy physics.

</details>

### [11] [Magnetic field dynamics in isolated neutron stars with an external dipole field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22921)
*Aurora Capobianco,William Cook,Sebastiano Bernuzzi,Brynmor Haskell,Jacob Fields*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本研究通过数值相对论模拟发现，中子星的磁场会自发演化至一种角向磁场能量占比不超过10%的稳定混合极向-角向位形，该位形在泰勒不稳定性（Tayler instabilities）饱和后一个阿尔芬时间（Alfvén time）内形成，并受到引力波发射的辅助作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中子星可维持极强的磁场，但其磁场的具体位形结构与稳定性机制尚不清楚；观测仅能约束远场外部的偶极场（dipolar field），而内部磁场位形几乎不受约束，因此需要从动力学稳定性角度加以研究。

Method: 采用长时程数值相对论模拟（numerical-relativity simulations），研究一组初始具有外部偶极场（external dipole field）和内部混合极向-角向场（mixed poloidal-toroidal internal field）的中子星模型，其中角向分量（toroidal component）能量占磁能比例最高达80%。

Result: 内部磁场会松弛至一种动力学稳定的混合极向-角向位形（dynamically stable mixed poloidal-toroidal geometry），其中角向分量对总磁能的贡献在外部和内部均不超过约10%；该稳定位形在泰勒不稳定性（Tayler instabilities）饱和后的一个阿尔芬时间（Alfvén time）内形成，引力波发射（gravitational-wave emission）也起到辅助作用。

Conclusion: 长寿期中子星磁场受到强烈约束，倾向于演化至稳定的混合位形，这一发现对脉冲星辐射模型（pulsar emission models）、磁星演化（magnetar evolution）以及磁化致密天体引力波信号（gravitational-wave signals from magnetized remnants）的解读具有重要启示。

Abstract: Neutron stars can harbor extremely strong magnetic fields, yet the structure and stability of their magnetic field configuration remain poorly understood. Observations of pulsars indicate that the large-scale external field is predominantly dipolar far from the star, while the internal magnetic configurations are largely unconstrained. We investigate the dynamical stability of magnetized neutron stars through long-term numerical-relativity simulations. We explore a range of models with an initial external dipole field and mixed poloidal-toroidal internal field where the energy of the toroidal component varies up to $80\%$ of the magnetic energy. We find that the internal magnetic field relaxes toward a dynamically stable mixed poloidal-toroidal geometry, in which the toroidal component contributes to $\lesssim10\%$ of the total magnetic energy both in the exterior and in the interior. This configuration emerges within one Alfvén time following the saturation of the Tayler instabilities and also aided by gravitational-wave emission. These results suggest that long-lived neutron star magnetic fields are strongly constrained toward stable mixed configurations, with important implications for pulsar emission models, magnetar evolution, and the interpretation of gravitational-wave signals from magnetized remnants.

</details>


### [12] [Inferring the role of binary neutron star mergers in r-process nucleosynthesis with multi-messenger observations using Cosmic Explorer and Einstein Telescope](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23554)
*Aman Agarwal,Suvodip Mukherjee,Daniel M. Siegel*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文提出利用第三代引力波探测器（Cosmic Explorer 和 Einstein Telescope）测量双中子星并合对宇宙快中子俘获（r-process）核合成贡献的方法，通过红移依赖的GW事件数与平均r-process丰度之间的相关性，在两种观测场景（亮sirens和暗sirens）下均能达到≤5-6%的精度估计BNS的累积贡献分数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 快中子俘获（r-process）元素的宇宙起源尚未确定，双中子星并合（binary neutron-star mergers, BNS mergers）与稀有类核心坍缩超新星（core-collapse supernovae, CCSNe）是主要候选产生源。尽管BNS并合可能单独解释r-process核合成，但化学演化研究、引力波（gravitational-wave, GW）观测到的BNS事件率以及低质量晕中的保留问题表明情况并非如此，因此需要直接测量BNS并合对r-process的贡献。

Method: 该方法利用红移依赖的BNS引力波事件总数与红移z≤1处平均r-process丰度之间的相关性。将该相关技术应用于模拟的GW和丰度数据，考虑两种极限观测情景：具有电磁对应体的多信使"亮sirens"（bright-sirens）和无电磁对应体的"暗sirens"（dark-sirens）。使用Fisher预测（Fisher forecasts）评估估计精度。

Result: 在基准天体物理场景下（F_BNS,z0 ≥ 0.1-1），两种观测场景均能以1σ置信度将BNS并合对宇宙r-process的累积贡献分数F_BNS,z0估计到≤5-6%的精度水平。该方法还能给出BNS延迟时间分布参数，其估计精度可与其它方法相当。

Conclusion: 该方法为利用第三代引力波探测器识别超出本地宇宙范围的中子俘获元素特征提供了科学依据，尽管宇宙r-process丰度可以从低金属丰度下的本地观测中重建。

Abstract: Identifying the cosmic origin of rapid neutron-capture (r-process) elements remains an open problem. Binary neutron-star (BNS) mergers and rare classes of core-collapse supernovae (CCSNe) represent the main contenders as major r-process production sites. Although BNS mergers could exclusively account for r-process nucleosynthesis, results from chemical evolution studies taking into account their delays with respect to star formation, observed BNS rates by gravitational-wave (GW) detectors, as well as issues with retention in low-mass halos suggest otherwise. Here, we propose a method to measure the contribution of BNS mergers to cosmic r-process nucleosynthesis with the third-generation GW detectors Cosmic Explorer and Einstein Telescope. It exploits the redshift-dependent correlation between the total number of BNS GW events and the average r-process abundances at redshifts $z \lesssim 1$. We apply this correlation technique to mock GW and abundance data, accounting for expected observational uncertainties in two limiting scenarios: GW events with electromagnetic counterpart (multi-messenger 'bright-sirens') and without ('dark-sirens'). Using Fisher forecasts, we demonstrate that the fractional cumulative contribution of BNS mergers to the total cosmic r-process $F_{\rm{BNS,z0}}$ can be estimated to the $\lesssim 5-6\%$ precision level for both scenarios at $1σ$ for fiducial astrophysical scenarios with $F_{\rm{BNS,z0}} \gtrsim 0.1-1$. Furthermore, the method also yields estimates of the BNS delay-time distribution parameters comparable to other approaches. Although cosmic r-process abundances may be reconstructed from local observations at low metallicity, this method also provides a science case to identify signatures of neutron-capture elements beyond the local Universe.

</details>

### [13] [On Global Attraction for a Particle Coupled to a Scalar Field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23186)
*Valeriy Imaykin*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 研究经典粒子与标量波场耦合系统在能量范数下的全局吸引问题，论证了无论在有约束势或零势两种情况下，均不存在全局吸引现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索有限能量解在能量范数（energy norm）意义下是否会被吸引到平衡态集合或孤子流形（soliton manifold），以理解经典粒子-波场耦合系统的长期动力学行为。

Method: 采用能量守恒论证（energy conservation argument）进行分析，分别考察有约束势（confining potential）情形下的平稳解集合（stationary solutions）与零势情形下的孤子流形两种吸引目标。

Result: 在两种情形下均未观察到全局吸引现象：有约束势情况下解不会全局收敛到平稳解集合，零势情况下也不会全局收敛到孤子流形。

Conclusion: 对于经典粒子耦合标量波场系统，能量范数下的全局吸引不成立，该结论对两种势能情形均适用。

Abstract: We study the question of global attraction, in the energy norm, for finite energy solutions to classical particle coupled to a scalar wave field. The attraction could take place to either the set of the stationary solutions in the case of a confining potential or to the soliton manifold in the case of zero potential. By energy conservation argument we establish that in both cases there is no global attraction.

</details>


### [14] [The Floquet-Magnus expansion of unbounded operators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23734)
*Daniel Burgarth,Robin Hillier,Davide Lonigro,Leonhard Richter*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文将Floquet-Magnus展开（Floquet-Magnus expansion）从有界哈密顿量推广到一大类时间周期无界哈密顿量（time-periodic unbounded Hamiltonians），并基于一种非微扰框架（nonperturbative framework）证明了其在高频极限下可对原始时间演化传播子实现任意阶的近似，且无需展开级数收敛。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准的Floquet-Magnus展开严格限于有界哈密顿量（bounded Hamiltonians），而许多重要的量子系统（如量子拉比模型、受驱谐振子）涉及无界哈密顿量。因此，需要将该方法推广至无界情形。

Method: 采用一种与标准微扰方法有本质区别的非微扰框架（nonperturbative framework）来构造有效哈密顿量，并证明该框架能够重现Floquet-Magnus展开的结果。

Result: 证明了该非微扰框架在高频极限（high-frequency limit）下，无需Floquet-Magnus展开收敛，即可使有效动力学对原始时间演化传播子实现任意阶的近似。在量子拉比哈密顿量（quantum Rabi Hamiltonian）和周期驱动量子谐振子（periodically driven quantum harmonic oscillator）等代表性模型上验证了方法的适用性。

Conclusion: 成功将Floquet-Magnus展开的分析和定义扩展到了一类广泛的时间周期无界哈密顿量，提供了一种无需级数收敛即可保证高频近似精度的理论工具。

Abstract: The Floquet-Magnus expansion is a widely used tool to derive effective descriptions of time-periodic quantum systems by approximating their dynamics with a time-independent Hamiltonian. However, its standard formulation is, strictly speaking, restricted to bounded Hamiltonians. In this work, we extend its definition and analysis to a broad class of time-periodic unbounded Hamiltonians. Our approach is based on an a priori distinct nonperturbative framework for the construction of effective Hamiltonians, which we show to reproduce the Floquet-Magnus expansion. A particular strength of our framework is that it allows us to prove that the resulting effective dynamics approximates the original time evolution propagators to arbitrary order in the high-frequency limit without requiring convergence of the Floquet-Magnus expansion, a condition that is already highly restrictive even in the bounded setting. We illustrate the scope of the method on representative models: the quantum Rabi Hamiltonian in the interaction picture, and the periodically driven quantum harmonic oscillator.

</details>


### [15] [Haantjes Algebras, Zernike system and separation of variables](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23748)
*Ondrej Kubu,Danilo Latini*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文解决了广义Zernike家族中N=2情况（经典Zernike系统）的显式分离坐标构造问题，涵盖所有四种分离类型，并证明对于N≥3存在一个障碍，使得分离坐标的构造需要依赖于动量的正则变换。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Nozaleda、Tempesta与Tondo的定理保证了广义Zernike哈密顿量家族存在正则分离坐标（canonical separation coordinates），即Darboux–Haantjes坐标，但如何显式构造这些坐标仍是一个悬而未决的挑战。本文旨在解决N=2情形下的该构造问题。

Method: 本文利用Haantjes算子（Haantjes operators）的结构性质进行分析：发现与H_(2)的所有积分（integrals of motion）相关联的Haantjes算子具有“lift形式”，即不存在依赖于动量的非对角块。基于这一事实，证明分离坐标可通过扩展点变换（extended point transformation）达到，其中新坐标仅依赖于旧坐标，不涉及动量。

Result: 对于N=2的经典Zernike系统，显式构造了四种分离类型的坐标：极坐标（polar）、两种笛卡尔型（Cartesian-type）以及椭圆坐标（elliptic）。在极坐标和笛卡尔型情形下，新坐标最多涉及单变量有理函数的平方根；在椭圆情形下，新坐标由原始坐标中一个二次多项式的两个根给出，其分支结构在量子分离ODE中引入第四个正则奇点（regular singular point），使其属于Heun类（Heun class）。对于N≥3，证明了一个障碍：不存在lift形式的Haantjes算子可以产生独立于角动量（angular momentum）的积分。

Conclusion: 对于N=2情形，解决了广义Zernike家族中分离坐标的显式构造问题，并揭示了其与量子分离ODE的关联。对于N≥3，分离坐标的构造必须借助依赖于动量的正则变换，这留作未来的工作。

Abstract: The generalized Zernike family $H_{(N)} = p_1^2 + p_2^2 + \sum_{n=1}^N γ_n\,(q_1 p_1 + q_2 p_2)^n$ is a parametric family of two-dimensional superintegrable Hamiltonians, admitting $N$ integrals of motion of degree $N$ in the momenta. A theorem of Nozaleda, Tempesta, and Tondo guarantees that canonical separation coordinates (Darboux--Haantjes coordinates) exist for any such system; the challenge is to construct them explicitly. This paper solves the problem for $N = 2$ -- the classical Zernike system, which is canonically equivalent to the isotropic harmonic oscillator on flat space or on a space of constant curvature -- covering all four known separation types: polar, two Cartesian-type, and elliptic. The key structural fact is that the Haantjes operators associated with all integrals of $H_{(2)}$ have no momentum-dependent off-diagonal block (lift form). We prove that this implies the separation coordinates are reachable by an extended point transformation: the new positions depend only on the old positions, with no momentum entering the coordinate change. In the polar and Cartesian-type cases the new position coordinates involve at most a square root of a single-variable rational function; in the elliptic case they are given by the two roots of a quadratic polynomial in the original coordinates, and the resulting branch structure introduces a fourth regular singular point in the quantum separated ODE, placing it in the Heun class, in agreement with results of Atakishiyev, Pogosyan, Vicent, Wolf, and Yakhno. For $N \geq 3$ we prove an obstruction: no lift-form Haantjes operator can generate an integral independent of the angular momentum. The separation coordinates for higher Zernike Hamiltonians therefore require momentum-dependent canonical transformations, whose explicit construction is the subject of future work.

</details>


### [16] [Reconstruction methods for inverse scattering problems with phaseless data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23784)
*John C. Schotland,Shenwen Yu*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文针对薛定谔方程的无相位逆散射问题，提出了基于逆玻恩级数（inverse Born series, IBS）的三种重构方法，分别适用于远场总场、总场和远场散射场三类无相位数据，并通过数值实验验证了各方法的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 逆散射问题在成像、雷达等领域具有重要应用，但实际测量中常因无法获取相位信息而面临挑战。本文旨在解决薛定谔方程（Schrödinger equation）的无相位（phaseless）逆散射问题，发展无需相位信息即可重构散射势（scattering potential）的可行方法。

Method: 对于无相位总场数据，论文扩展了逆玻恩级数（inverse Born series, IBS）框架并分析了其收敛半径；对于远场总场数据，利用入射方向与观测方向之间的散射互易性（scattering reciprocity）提出了一种基于傅里叶（Fourier）的重构方法以恢复散射势的傅里叶系数；对于无相位散射场数据，采用基于偏振（polarization）的方法恢复相位信息，从而实现IBS重构。

Result: 通过数值实验验证了针对三类无相位数据所提出的重构方法的有效性。

Conclusion: 本文为薛定谔方程的无相位逆散射问题提供了三种可行的重构策略，拓展了IBS框架在无相位场景下的应用，为实际成像中缺乏相位信息的困难提供了理论和方法支持。

Abstract: We investigate phaseless inverse scattering problem for the Schrödinger equation and develop reconstruction methods based on the inverse Born series (IBS). We consider three types of phaseless data: the far-field total field, the total field and the far-field scattered field. For phaseless total-field data, we extend the IBS framework and analyze its radius of convergence. In the far-field setting, we propose a Fourier-based reconstruction method that exploits the scattering reciprocity between incident and observation directions to recover Fourier coefficients of the scattering potential. For phaseless scattered-field data, we employ a polarization-based approach to recover phase information and enable IBS reconstruction. Numerical experiments are conducted to validate the proposed methods.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于$z$依赖的超对称（supersymmetric, SUSY）变换推导出精确连续解，构建两个PT对称耦合波导在纵向调制下的理论模型，并将TB近似的结果与这一严格SUSY基准进行对比分析。

Result: 确定了TB近似的有效范围，表明其在重现空间强度分布方面表现良好，但无法准确捕捉该非厄米（non-Hermitian）演化中固有的复杂振荡相位动力学。

Abstract: The tight-binding (TB) model is a widely adopted approximation scheme for describing light propagation in waveguide arrays. In this work, we address this gap by performing a comparative analysis between exact continuous solutions derived from $z$-dependent supersymmetric (SUSY) transformations and their corresponding discrete TB approximations. To achieve this, we develop a theoretical model for two PT-symmetric coupled waveguides subject to longitudinal modulation. We then evaluate the performance of the TB framework against the exact SUSY benchmark. Our results delineate the specific validity range of the TB approximation, demonstrating its proficiency in reproducing spatial intensity distributions. However, we also identify its limitations in accurately capturing the complex oscillatory phase dynamics inherent to this non-Hermitian evolution.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 对16×16 LGAD阵列的完整行级电流-电压（I-V）扫描约需20分钟，逐像素扫描（0–300 V，步长1 V）约需340分钟；切换矩阵在最坏保守配置下引入的漏电流小于1 nA，远低于正常LGAD像素的漏电流水平。

Abstract: Low-Gain Avalanche Diode (LGAD) sensors, offering timing resolutions of the order of tens of picoseconds, are being widely adopted in particle physics experiments and related applications. As these applications scale to large numbers of sensors with varying pixel geometries, conventional manual characterization techniques become inadequate for large-scale quality control. We present a modular probe card system for automated electrical characterization of pixelated LGAD sensors, consisting of a probe card, a switching board, precision measurement instruments, and control software. The system supports arbitrary pixel selection and flexible measurement config16 urations, including single-pixel, grouped, row-wise, and inter-pixel measurements. Its performance is demonstrated through current-voltage (I-V) and capacitance-voltage (C-V) measurements of a $16 \times 16$ LGAD array. A rapid row-wise current-voltage (I-V) scan of the full array is completed in approximately 20 minutes, while a pixel-by-pixel current-voltage (I-V) scan from 0 to 300 V with a 1 V step requires about 340 minutes. The switching matrix introduces less than 1 nA of leakage current even in a conservative worst-case configuration, remaining small compared with the leakage current of a normal LGAD pixel. The modular architecture and automation capability make the system a practical and scalable solution for large-scale LGAD sensor quality control and distributed testing environments.

### [19] [Studies on photon-feedback and LaB$_6$ photocathode for the GasPM development](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23542)
*Simone Garnero,Kenji Inami,Kodai Matsuoka,Ryogo Okubo,Koichi Ueda*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文基于束流测试与宇宙线实验，发展了气体光电倍增管（GasPM）技术，重点研究了导致其时间分辨率从25 ps（2022年）退化至70 ps（2023年）的主要原因——气体分子退激产生的紫外光子反馈（photon-feedback）信号。通过采用10 GSPS高速数字化仪和改进的束流测试装置，成功分离了反馈信号与真实信号，并探索了LaB₆光电阴极的量子效率。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于束流测试和宇宙线实验，结合多种器件配置变更，采用10 GSPS（每秒十亿次采样）频率数字化仪分离光子反馈信号；同时使用LaB₆光电阴极（相比CsI具有更高的抗空气和抗反向漂移离子能力）进行量子效率研究。

Result: 2022年实验在3.3×10⁶增益下实现了25 ps的单光子时间分辨率；2023年采用MgF₂窗口与CsI光电阴极的配置导致时间分辨率退化至70 ps；通过改进装置和高速数字化仪成功分离了光子反馈信号。

Conclusion: 气体分子退激产生的紫外光子反馈信号是导致时间分辨率退化的主要原因，采用高速数字化仪可有效分离该干扰信号；LaB₆光电阴极因其更高的环境耐受性，在GasPM应用中具有潜力。

Abstract: We present new developments, based on beam tests and cosmic rays, on the gaseous photomultiplier (GasPM). The GasPM detects photons by combining a photocathode with a resistive-plate-chamber avalanche. It achieves $\mathcal{O}$(10) ps time resolution with affordable scalability. The GasPM provides precise and efficient Cherenkov-based charged-particle identification too when combined with a radiator. Our target application in a future Belle II upgrade aims at suppressing beam-induced background photons, which are typically detected off-collision time, that spoil the electromagnetic calorimeter performance. We reached 25 ps single-photon time-resolution at 3.3x10$^6$ gain in 2022, using a picosecond-pulse laser and a LaB$_6$ photocathode. However, electrons entering through a MgF$_2$ window upstream of a CsI photocathode showed a worsening to 70 ps in a 2023 test. Here we aim at addressing the chief causes of the observed degradation. We focus on ultraviolet-photon emission from the de-excitation of the gas molecules, which generates a secondary "photon-feedback" signal overlapping the primary one, and degrading time resolution. We conceive and operate an improved beam test that, along with multiple device-configuration changes, employes a new 10 GSPS frequency digitizer to separate the photon-feedback signal from the genuine signal. We also use cosmic-rays on a LaB$_6$ photocathode, which has higher than CsI's resistance to air and to ions drifting backwards onto the photocathode, to explore its quantum efficiency.

</details>

*L. Li,P. Behera,D. V. Berlea,D. Bortoletto,C. Buttar,T. Chembakan,V. Dao,G. Dash,Y. Enari,L. Fasselt,S. Haberl,T. Inada,F. K. Isik,C. Issever,X. Li,Y. Okazaki,H. Pernegger,P. Riedler,W. Snoeys,C. A Solans Sanchez,A. Swoboda,I. Turk Cakir,M. van Rijnbach,A. Vijay,S. Worm*

Result: 传感器性能（检测效率与簇尺寸）对表面N型覆盖层掺杂浓度表现出强烈依赖性。在优化掺杂浓度下，掠射角方法估算的活性深度与测量值在450电子阈值处偏差仅2%，实现了极好的一致性。

Conclusion: 该混合仿真框架无需专有信息即可准确模拟MALTA2传感器特性，为未来追踪探测器的传感器研究提供了一种通用且有效的工具包（toolkit）。

Abstract: In this work, a hybrid simulation framework combining TCAD and Allpi$\text{x}^2$ is presented to investigate the sensor properties of MALTA2, a depleted monolithic active pixel sensor designed for future tracking. The study starts from 3D modeling and transient simulations in TCAD, with generic doping profiles and simple well structures. The resulting doping profiles and electric field are extracted and fed into Allpi$\text{x}^2$ for high-statistics Monte Carlo simulations in both DUT-only and full-telescope mode.
  Simulations reveal a strong dependence of sensor performance, specifically the detection efficiency and cluster size, on the doping concentration of the N-type blanket at the sensor surface. The doping concentration is then optimized by comparing simulations with measurement data. The active depth of the depleted region of the MALTA2 sensor is estimated in both simulations and measurements using a grazing angle method, in which the sensor is positioned at various inclinations relative to the beam, covering angles from 0 to 60 degrees. Excellent agreement on active depth is obtained with the optimal doping concentration, showing a deviation of 2\% from the measured value at a threshold of 450\,$\text{e}^-$. Consequently, the framework offers a generic toolkit for sensor studies without requiring proprietary information.

### [22] [On almost periodicity in crystalline measures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23884)
*Jan Mazáč,Christoph Richard,Nicolae Strungaru*

Main category: math.FA

TL;DR: 本文通过构造反例，完整解决了Meyer关于晶体测度（crystalline measure）的猜想和Favorov的后续问题，表明晶体测度无需平移有界（translation bounded）即可成为几乎周期分布（almost periodic distribution），并揭示了晶体测度与傅里叶准晶（Fourier quasicrystal）之间清晰的类边界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Meyer猜想每个晶体测度作为缓增分布（tempered distribution）都是几乎周期的（almost periodic），但Favorov构造了反例并进一步追问：晶体测度作为一般分布（general distribution）是否至少是几乎周期的？该问题亟待解决。

Method: 首先证明，在Radon测度（Radon measures）、缓增分布或一般分布的任何一类中，晶体测度的几乎周期性均可通过其平移有界性（translation boundedness）来刻画。然后构造一个不具有平移有界性的晶体傅里叶本征测度（Fourier eigenmeasure）。最后构造一个不是傅里叶准晶（因而也非缓增的）但却是几乎周期缓增分布且其傅里叶变换甚至是范数几乎周期测度（norm almost periodic measure）的晶体测度。

Result: 构造了两个反例：其一为缺乏平移有界性的晶体傅里叶本征测度；其二为不满足傅里叶准晶条件、但仍是几乎周期缓增分布的晶体测度。这些例子完整回答了Meyer和Favorov的问题，并精确划定了平移有界性的类边界。

Conclusion: 晶体测度在平移有界性方面的表现超出先前认知，存在既非傅里叶准晶又非缓增但依然几乎周期的晶体测度。这些结果清晰界定了晶体测度与傅里叶准晶之间的类别界限，展示了晶体测度的异常行为。

Abstract: Meyer defined crystalline measures as tempered distributions $μ$ such that both $μ$ and its Fourier transform $\widehatμ$ are pure-point Radon measures of locally finite support. He conjectured that every crystalline measure is almost periodic as a tempered distribution. Favorov constructed a counterexample and asked whether crystalline measures are at least almost periodic as general distributions. To resolve Favorov's question, we first show that the almost periodicity of a crystalline measure is characterised in terms of its translation boundedness, in any class of Radon measures, tempered distributions, or general distributions. We then construct a crystalline Fourier eigenmeasure that fails to be translation bounded even as a distribution. We finally construct a crystalline measure that fails to be a~Fourier quasicrystal (in particular, it fails to be slowly increasing), but it is an almost periodic tempered distribution whose Fourier transform is even a norm almost periodic measure. Our examples fully resolve the questions of Meyer and Favorov and sharply delineate the class boundary of translation boundedness. They also demonstrate the unusual behaviour of crystalline measures beyond the class of Fourier quasicrystals.

</details>

### [23] [Convexity and non-Markovianity of Weyl Maps](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23852)
*Wen Xu,Vinayak Jagadish*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了由Weyl动力学映射及其凸组合支配的有限维开放量子系统中的非马尔可夫（non-Markovian）动力学。通过Hermite标准型对离散相空间子群进行了完全分类，揭示了各向异性Weyl映射无法具备半群性质，并发现非马尔可夫性在混合下不具可加性——凸组合可以产生或消除记忆效应。此外，还识别了无需混合机制即可展现永恒非马尔可夫性的不可约Weyl退相映射。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有非马尔可夫开放量子系统理论主要基于Pauli框架（如qubit系统），缺乏对更一般有限维系统中相空间代数结构与量子记忆效应之间关系的系统性理解。本文旨在利用Weyl动力学映射及其凸组合，建立有限相空间代数、凸结构和记忆效应之间的基本联系，从而将非马尔可夫动力学理论推广到Pauli框架之外。

Method: 运用Hermite标准型（Hermite normal form）对离散相空间 $\mathbb{Z}_d \times \mathbb{Z}_d$ 的子群进行完全分类，以此建立Weyl映射的代数基础。在此基础上，对各向同性与各向异性Weyl动力学映射的半群性质进行刻画，并通过凸组合分析非马尔可夫性的可加性与抑制机制。

Result: 各向同性（isotropic）Weyl动力学映射可生成马尔可夫半群（Markovian semigroup），而具有非均匀权重分布的各向异性（anisotropic）Weyl映射无法具备半群性质。凸组合可在永恒非马尔可夫Weyl退相映射之间生成马尔可夫半群，即非马尔可夫性在混合下不具可加性。反之，本文给出了 $N$ 个不同Weyl半群的凸混合物呈现永恒非马尔可夫性的一般条件。与qubit Pauli情形不同，存在不可约的永恒非马尔可夫Weyl退相映射，即无需混合即可展现永恒记忆效应的单个动力学映射。

Conclusion: 有限相空间代数、凸结构与量子记忆效应之间存在深层关联。本文通过Weyl动力学映射框架，将非马尔可夫动力学理论系统性地拓展到了Pauli框架之外的更一般有限维系统。qutrit实例展示了马尔可夫、非马尔可夫与永恒非马尔可夫（eternally non-Markovian）三种动力学区域之间的转换。

Abstract: We investigate the emergence of non-Markovian dynamics in finite-dimensional open quantum systems governed by Weyl dynamical maps and their convex combinations. Using the Hermite normal form, we provide a complete classification of the subgroups of the discrete phase space $\mathbb{Z}_d \times \mathbb{Z}_d$, establishing the algebraic framework underlying the Weyl maps. We characterize isotropic Weyl dynamical maps that generate Markovian semigroups and show that anisotropic Weyl maps with nonuniform weight distributions cannot possess the semigroup property. Furthermore, we analyze the role of convexity in the generation and suppression of memory effects. Remarkably, we prove that convex combinations of eternally non-Markovian Weyl dephasing maps can generate Markovian semigroups, demonstrating that non-Markovianity is not additive under mixing. Conversely, we establish a general condition under which convex mixtures of $N$ distinct Weyl semigroups exhibit eternal non-Markovianity. In contrast to the qubit Pauli setting, we further identify the existence of irreducible eternally non-Markovian Weyl dephasing maps, namely, individual dynamical maps that display eternal memory effects without requiring any mixing mechanism. Finally, explicit qutrit examples illustrate the transition among Markovian, non-Markovian and eternally non-Markovian regimes. Our results uncover a fundamental connection among finite phase-space algebra, convex structures, and quantum memory effects, thereby extending the theory of non-Markovian dynamics beyond the Pauli framework.

</details>


### [24] [Anomalous Decay of Quantum Resources: The Entanglement Sudden Death Mpemba Effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23197)
*Zhilong Liu,Zehua Tian,Jieci Wang*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文在量子系统中发现了一种与纠缠突然死亡（entanglement sudden death, ESD）相关联的新型量子姆潘巴效应：两个与振幅阻尼库（amplitude damping reservoirs）相互作用的量子比特（qubits）中，初始纠缠更强的态反而比纠缠更弱的态更快地坍缩为可分离态。研究提供了轨迹交叉动力学和ESD时间的精确解析推导，并绘制了初始态参数相图以界定该反常纠缠姆潘巴效应的发生区域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 分析两个与局域振幅阻尼库（local amplitude damping reservoirs）相互作用的量子比特（qubits），比较不同初始纠缠强度下系统演化的轨迹交叉动力学和纠缠突然死亡（ESD）时间。提供精确的解析推导以描述轨迹交叉行为。

Result: 初始纠缠更强的量子比特态比初始纠缠更弱的态更快地演变为可分离态，即存在纠缠姆潘巴效应（entanglement Mpemba effect）。得到了轨迹交叉动力学和ESD时间的解析表达式，并通过初始态参数相图（phase diagram）标定了该反常效应发生的参数区域。

Conclusion: 该发现揭示了耗散环境中量子资源寿命控制的新机制，为在耗散环境下调控量子资源（quantum resource）的寿命提供了理论依据和潜在路径。

Abstract: In classical thermodynamics, the Mpemba effect refers to the counterintuitive observation that hot water can freeze faster than cold water, manifesting as an anomalous crossing of dynamical trajectories. While analogues of this phenomenon have been explored in quantum radiative systems and spin-chain entanglement asymmetry, its connection to the finite-time decoupling of quantum correlations remains elusive. In this Letter, we uncover a distinct quantum Mpemba effect associated with entanglement sudden death (ESD). By analyzing two qubits interacting with local amplitude damping reservoirs, we demonstrate that a more strongly entangled initial state can experience a faster collapse into a separable state than a more weakly entangled one. We provide an exact analytical derivation of the trajectory crossover dynamics and the ESD time. Finally, we map the phase diagram of initial state parameters to delineate the regime where this anomalous entanglement Mpemba effect occurs, offering insights into the control of quantum resource lifetimes in dissipative environments.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索非对易时空（non-commutative spacetime）与量子群（quantum groups）在量子引力（quantum gravity）低能极限下所捕捉的非经典时空与对称性特征，并将其应用于自旋系统以揭示测量概率层面的量子结构。

Method: 利用 $SU_q(2)$ 量子群描述自旋-1/2系统与Stern-Gerlach装置的旋转对称性，将测量结果的概率表述为非对易算符（non-commuting operators），进而分析不同概率算符之间的不确定关系。

Result: 得到了不同概率算符之间的不确定性原理，实现了不定概率（indefinite probabilities）的概念；该不定概率进一步体现为连接两观测者参考系的旋转矩阵（rotation matrix）元素之间的非对易性（non-commutativity）。

Conclusion: 该结果从根本上阻止了观测者精确测量其相对取向，暗示了在量子群对称性框架下，参考系之间的相对方向本身具有量子不确定性。

Abstract: Non-commutative spacetime and quantum groups have been argued to capture non-classical features of spacetime and its symmetries in the low-energy limit of quantum gravity. In this letter, we show that employing the $SU_q(2)$ quantum group to describe rotational symmetry for spin-$\frac{1}{2}$ systems and Stern-Gerlach apparatuses leads to the description of probabilities of outcomes of spin measurements in terms of non-commuting operators. As a result, we obtain an uncertainty principle between different probability operators, realizing a notion of indefinite probabilities. This is then reflected in the non-commutativity of the entries of the rotation matrix relating the reference frames of two observers, hence fundamentally preventing them from sharply measuring their relative orientation.

### [26] [Quantum Fisher Information under decoherence with explicit wavefunctions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22917)
*Francesco Musso,Vittorio Vitale,Sara Murciano*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 提出了一种在退相干（decoherence）存在下估计多体量子态量子Fisher信息（quantum Fisher information, QFI）的方法，通过将QFI的下界映射到经典概率分布的期望值，利用马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（Markov-chain Monte Carlo, MCMC）采样实现高效计算，计算代价为慢指数增长，并分析了Jastrow-Gutzwiller波函数的计量学内容及噪声影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 直接计算多体量子态的QFI需要密度矩阵的完整谱分解（spectral resolution），这在退相干存在时计算代价极高，难以处理超出精确对角化（exact diagonalization）范围的系统尺寸。

Method: 对于在占据数基（occupation-number basis）上有解析形式的多体波函数，将QFI的系统性下界（lower bounds）映射为由波函数振幅定义的经典概率分布上的期望值，进而通过马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛采样进行高效估计。该框架具体应用于Jastrow-Gutzwiller波函数，并比较了多项式（polynomial）与Krylov两种下界方法。

Result: 计算代价以“慢”指数（$e^{b L}, b \lesssim 0.6$）增长，对远超精确对角化范围的系统尺寸仍然可控。在局域退相（local dephasing）、局域振幅阻尼（local amplitude damping）和全局退极化（global depolarizing）三种噪声通道下，分析了QFI的行为，并将下界方法与噪声密度矩阵的有效秩（effective rank）及参数编码生成算子的结构联系起来。

Conclusion: 该框架可自然推广到其他解析已知的波函数及QFI以外的更广泛信息论量（information-theoretic quantities）。

Abstract: We present a method to estimate the quantum Fisher information (QFI) of many-body quantum states in the presence of decoherence, where its direct evaluation requires the full spectral resolution of the density matrix. We show that, for many-body wave functions known analytically in the occupation-number basis, systematic lower bounds to the QFI can be mapped onto expectation values over a classical probability distribution defined by the wave function amplitudes. This mapping enables efficient estimation via Markov-chain Monte Carlo sampling, with a computational cost that scales as a `slow' exponential ($e^{b L}$ with $b \lesssim 0.6$) and remains manageable for system sizes well beyond exact diagonalization. We specify this framework to Jastrow-Gutzwiller wave functions. We characterize their metrological content by identifying the observables that maximize the QFI and the corresponding scaling with $L$. Then, we analyze the QFI under three physically motivated noise channels: local dephasing, local amplitude damping, and global depolarizing. We compare polynomial and Krylov-based lower bounds across these channels, relating their behavior to the effective rank of the noisy density matrix and to the structure of the operator generating the parameter encoding. The framework extends naturally to other analytically known wave functions and to a broader class of information-theoretic quantities beyond the QFI.

Abstract: Models of interacting complex systems provide the fundamental statistical physics reference frame for the study and the understanding of associative memories, machine learning, and the dynamics of neural networks. On the other hand, simulating complex multi-synaptic interactions on a classical hardware is computationally demanding due to the super-linear scaling of the system complexity. Photonic quantum technologies provide a promising solution to these limitations by leveraging on their inherent speed and parallel processing ability in order to simulate complex networks. Recently, a connection between multiphoton processes and generalized $p$-body Hopfield models has been theoretically established. Here, we design and demonstrate an experimental platform that exploits single photons distributed across a set of optical modes, in which controlled arrays of binary phase shifters act as Ising-like neurons. We focus specifically on a fully connected Hopfield Hamiltonian with four-body local interaction terms, realized via two-photon processes. Through quantum simulations on programmable photonic processors, the study identifies three distinct regimes: a memory retrieval phase, a spin-glass memory "black-out" phase, and a paramagnetic phase. Experimental results confirm successful memory retrieval at low storage capacities and temperatures, where the system consistently relaxes to fixed points with high memory overlap, effectively reconstructing the stored patterns. Future research will extend the platform design to investigate networks with local or dilute interactions, while advances in the realization of scalable photonic circuits will enable architectures that encompass very large numbers of interacting spins.

Abstract: We present a variant of the Dicke model, termed as the open coupled-top Dicke model, which enables the exploration of rich non-equilibrium phenomena, particularly the fate of quantum scars in an open environment. This model can effectively be realized by coupling a two-species Bose-Josephson junction to a lossy cavity. Photon loss induces spontaneous synchronization via projection onto a dissipation-free subspace, along with transient chaos followed by restoration of synchronization and coherence. We identify two distinct scarring phenomena in the presence of dissipation. One remains protected, exhibiting persistent revivals, while the scar associated with the superradiant phase displays a dissipation-induced slow decay of the survival probability. Abstract: We study transport across the Aubry-André-Harper localization transition in the presence of non-Markovian dissipation. For a single particle initially at the center of the chain, we show that bath memory (i.e., finite decay time of bath correlations) plays distinct roles in the two phases. In the extended phase, bath memory qualitatively reshapes the dynamical generator, thereby producing transport patterns that cannot be reduced to a simple rescaling of time. By contrast, in the localized phase, the bath activates motion between localized states and bath memory mainly renormalizes the dynamical timescales. Our results identify localization as a simple filter of non-Markovian effects: memory restructures transport in the extended regime, but survives mainly as a timescale renormalization in the deeply localized regime.

### [31] [Absorbing Many-Body Correlations into Core-Optimized Orbitals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22977)
*Hao Zhang,Matthew Otten*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出芯优化轨道（Core-Optimized Orbitals, COO）方法，将轨道基与稀疏组态相互作用（Configuration Interaction, CI）波函数联合优化，在强关联多中心体系（如铁硫簇）上实现了比最先进张量网络方法更为紧凑的波函数表示，将所需行列式数量降低多个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典或量子硬件上模拟量子多体系统的计算成本随变分参数数量增长，因此固定预算下取得进展需要更参数高效的拟设（ansatz）。组态相互作用（CI）被广泛认为参数过多，但本文指出这一判断是轨道基选择造成的人为假象。

Method: 本文提出芯优化轨道（Core-Optimized Orbitals, COO）方法，将轨道基与稀疏CI波函数联合优化，将大量动力学关联（dynamical correlation）直接吸收进单粒子基（single-particle basis）中，从而在已有紧凑TrimCI拟设的基础上将行列式数量再降低数个数量级。

Result: 在[Fe₄S₄]（54电子，36轨道）体系上，十亿行列式的TrimCI+COO波函数达到的精度在局域化基中需要3×10¹⁴个行列式。精度匹配时，其比最大无限制密度矩阵重整化群（unrestricted-DMRG）基准紧凑8倍（计入PT2后为25倍）。在铁硫系列（[Fe₂S₂]到P-cluster, 114e,73o）中，TrimCI+COO在匹配精度下比SU(2)自适应DMRG紧凑10-100倍。通过可调Hubbard-on-graph模型，该优势可分解为轨道基增益和拟设增益，后者捕获了阻碍矩阵乘积态（MPS）局域化的多中心纠缠。

Conclusion: COO方法改变了人们对CI效率的认知：具备优化轨道的稀疏CI能够在强关联多中心体系上超越最先进的张量网络方法。

Abstract: The cost of simulating quantum many-body systems - on classical or quantum hardware - scales with the number of variational parameters, so progress at fixed computational budget hinges on more parameter-efficient ansätze. Configuration Interaction (CI) is widely dismissed as parameter-heavy; we show this verdict is an artifact of the orbital basis. Co-optimizing the orbital basis with a sparse CI wavefunction - a method we call Core-Optimized Orbitals (COO) - absorbs a large fraction of the dynamical correlation directly into the single-particle basis, cutting the determinant count by several orders of magnitude beyond the already compact TrimCI ansatz on which it builds. On [Fe$_4$S$_4$] (54e, 36o), a billion-determinant TrimCI+COO wavefunction reaches accuracy that would require $3\!\times\!10^{14}$ determinants in a localized basis. At matched accuracy, it is $8\times$ more compact than the largest unrestricted-DMRG benchmark ($25\times$ with PT2). Across the iron-sulfur series - from [Fe$_2$S$_2$] (30e,20o) to the P-cluster (114e,73o) - TrimCI+COO is $10$-$100\times$ more compact than SU(2)-adapted DMRG with entanglement-minimized orbitals at matched accuracy. A tunable Hubbard-on-graph model factorizes the advantage into an orbital-basis gain and an ansatz gain, the latter capturing multi-center entanglement that resists MPS localization. COO therefore changes the picture of CI efficiency: sparse CI with optimized orbitals can outperform state-of-the-art tensor networks on strongly correlated multi-center systems.

</details>


### [32] [Transition-state lattice modes and the breakdown of adiabatic tunneling for hydrogen and deuterium in bcc Nb](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23212)
*P. Graham Pritchard,James M. Rondinelli*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过五维晶格重整化玻恩-奥本海默（5D LRBO）框架，证明体心立方金属中氢和氘的隧穿是一个集体非绝热过程，仅在正μ子质量极限下绝热近似成立，从而推翻了传统绝热分离假设的普适性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 氢同位素在体心立方（bcc）金属中的量子隧穿是典型的量子隧穿系统，其重要性因铌中氢隧穿与超导量子比特中缺陷诱导退相干之间的关联而重新凸显，亟需建立具有预测能力的微观理论。然而，现有理论基于轻间隙原子与宿主晶格间的绝热分离（adiabatic separation）假设，其有效性从未被严格验证。

Method: 提出五维晶格重整化玻恩-奥本海默（5D Lattice-Renormalized Born-Oppenheimer, LRBO）框架，将三个间隙模式和两个精挑的晶格模式（含一个过渡态模式）置于同等的量子基点上。通过在该形式中重构嵌套的玻恩-奥本海默层次结构，并基于现代从头算（ab initio）势能面进行基准测试。

Result: 实验测量的O陷阱捕获的H和D在bcc Nb中的隧穿劈裂（tunnel splittings）仅在5D LRBO框架下被定量再现。绝热分离仅在正μ子（μ⁺）质量极限下成立；对H和D而言，隧穿本质上是集体非绝热（nonadiabatic）过程，由非谐晶格耦合（anharmonic lattice couplings）介导。绝热性失效可通过少量固定晶格构型下的基态轻粒子能量简单估计来预判。

Conclusion: 传统绝热分离假设不适用于H和D的隧穿过程，需采用包含晶格-间隙子集体耦合的非绝热理论。所提出的能量估计方法为评估其他系统绝热隧穿理论的有效性提供了实用判据。

Abstract: Interstitial hydrogen and deuterium in body-centered-cubic metals constitute archetypal quantum tunneling systems. Their relevance has been renewed by the connection between hydrogenic tunneling in Nb and defect-induced decoherence in superconducting qubits, motivating a predictive microscopic theory. Existing theoretical treatments invoke an adiabatic separation between the light interstitial and the host lattice, an assumption whose validity has not been rigorously established for hydrogenic species. Here, we show that the experimentally measured tunnel splittings of O-trapped H and D in bcc Nb are quantitatively reproduced only within a five-dimensional (5D) Lattice-Renormalized Born-Oppenheimer (LRBO) framework. This approach treats three interstitial modes and two judiciously selected lattice modes, which includes a transition-state mode, on equal quantum footing. By recasting nested Born-Oppenheimer hierarchies within this same formalism and benchmarking against modern \textit{ab initio} potential energy surfaces, we show that adiabatic separation of the light particle from lattice dynamics is satisfied only in the positive-muon ($μ^{+}$) mass limit. In contrast, tunneling for H and D is fundamentally a collective, nonadiabatic process mediated by anharmonic lattice couplings. Finally, we show that the breakdown of adiabaticity can be anticipated from simple energy estimates involving the ground-state light-particle energy evaluated at a small number of fixed lattice configurations, providing a practical criterion for assessing the validity of adiabatic tunneling theories in other systems.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子系统的演化包含连续幺正动力学（unitary dynamics）和随机测量诱导的跳跃（measurement-induced jumps）两个基本过程，后者通常被视为退相干（decoherence）的来源。本文的核心问题在于：由局域测量构成的两种演化历史是否能够相互干涉？

Method: 作者设计了一个协议（protocol），其中两种交替的局域测量过程（alternative local measurement processes）作用在一对量子比特（qubits）上。通过相干控制（coherent control）实现不同测量历史之间的干涉，从而产生纠缠。

Result: 干涉的测量历史可以在两个与不同探测器耦合的量子比特部分之间产生纠缠。即使对探测器的读出结果取平均，系统仍然处于纠缠态（尽管不是最大纠缠态）。

Conclusion: 本文的结果将量子干涉（quantum interference）的概念从幺正演化扩展到纯测量驱动的动力学（measurement-driven dynamics），并指出了利用测量历史干涉产生量子关联（quantum correlations）时所受的限制。

Abstract: The evolution of a quantum system comprises two fundamental processes--continuous unitary dynamics and stochastic measurement-induced jumps. The latter are often viewed as a source of decoherence. Can two histories of such an evolution, made up of local measurements, interfere with each other? Here, we answer this question in the affirmative. A manifestation of this interference is the generation of entanglement between two parts of the system that are individually coupled to distinct detectors. Specifically, we develop a protocol in which two alternative local measurement processes act on a pair of qubits, and show how interference of histories is generated under coherent control, leading to entanglement. Furthermore, we find that averaging over the detectors' readouts still results in an entangled (albeit not maximally entangled) state. Our results extend the notion of quantum interference beyond unitary evolution to genuinely measurement-driven dynamics, and identify limits on the generation of quantum correlations using interference of measurement histories.

### [34] [Quantum viscosity mechanism of the dissipative dynamics in the Dicke model expressed via Lindblad equation of motion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23322)
*M. E. S. Beck,S. S. Seidov,S. I. Muhkin*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过量子力学方法解析推导扩展Dicke模型在超辐射相中与Caldeira-Leggett热浴耦合的Lindblad方程，分析半经典运动方程中的有效粘度项。

Result: 有效粘度在零温极限T→0下不为零，其贡献包含与玻色-爱因斯坦分布函数（Bose-Einstein function）nB(ω, T)相关的prefactor nB+1，表明该粘度来源于热浴中谐振子的虚激发。正确构建超辐射相的Lindbladian需使用凝聚位移后的光子产生湮灭算符以及Holstein-Primakoff表象中的赝自旋算符。

Abstract: Quantum dissipation is studied in the superradiant phase of the Extended Dicke model. It is demonstrated analytically by quantum mechanical derivation of the Lindblad equation for the Dicke model in the superradiant state coupled to Caldeira-Leggett thermal bath, that the effective viscosity appearing in the semiclassical equations of motion of polaritonic condensate survives in the zero temperature limit T -> 0. The nonzero contribution to viscosity contains prefactor nB (ω, T ) + 1 with the Bose-Einstein function nB of harmonic oscillators in the thermal bath, indicating that virtual excitations of harmonic oscillators in the thermal bath coupled to the polaritons of Dicke model give rise to effective viscosity in the T -> 0 limit. Besides, it is demonstrated analytically, that correct expression for Lindbladian in the superradiant phase should be built using condensate-shifted creation and annihilation operators of the photons and pseudospin operators in Holstein-Primakoff representation of the coupled to photons two-level systems in order the system could relax to its minimum energy in T -> 0 limit due to thermal bath provided effective viscosity.

Method: 采用大$N$极限下的量子$\mathcal{O}(N)$模型，使用无限平板二分几何（infinite-slab bipartition geometry）和精确数值关联函数，对淬火后动力学过程中的纠缠熵和纠缠本征模进行标度分析。

Abstract: We demonstrate that the dynamical phase transition of the quantum $\mathcal{O}(N)$ model at large $N$ leaves universal fingerprints in the infrared structure of the entanglement spectrum. While the leading contribution to the entanglement entropy at long time follows the conventional volume law associated with ballistic entanglement spreading, its subleading behavior sharply distinguishes the different dynamical regimes. Specifically, quenches at and below the critical point generate gapless low-energy entanglement modes together with logarithmic corrections to the long-time entanglement entropy, whose scaling is governed by the dynamical exponent of the transition. Using an infinite-slab bipartition geometry and exact numerical correlation functions in the large-$N$ limit, we characterize these scaling laws across the dynamical phase diagram and relate them to the emergence of long-range correlations during the post-quench dynamics. Abstract: We study atom-photon bound states seeded by two-level emitters coupled to self-similar photonic lattices. By expressing the photonic Green's function through the heat kernel, we show that the far-field localization length obeys $ξ\sim Δ^{-1/d_w}$, with the detuning $Δ$ from the lower spectral edge and the walk dimension $d_w$ of the underlying fractal. This scaling is controlled by anomalous diffusion and does not rely on translational invariance or a band-edge effective-mass approximation. Exact diagonalization on Sierpiński gaskets, pyramids, Vicsek graphs, and Sierpiński carpets confirms the far-field prediction once the bath Hamiltonian is rendered Laplacian-like by compensating the local inhomogeneity in the connectivities with on-site potentials. Our results extend structured-bath waveguide QED to self-similar non-periodic geometries and connect bound-state profiles to transport exponents of the underlying fractal lattice.

Abstract: Generic quantum many-body systems are expected to thermalize, scrambling initial coherence while local observables relax to equilibrium values. We introduce a family of local spin-1/2 chains with a structured subspace that hosts a much broader range of nonthermal phenomena, such as scars, chirally propagating quasiparticles or approximate topological edge modes. These nonthermal phenomena happening at high energy densities can be understood via structured subspaces that are protected by destructive interference. ### [39] [Quantum Quenches that Resemble Operator Growth](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23874)
*Xiangyu Cao*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究“生长淬火”（growth quenches）——一类通过局部淬火（local quenches）渐进失稳假真空（false vacuum）的动力学过程——在East-West模型等动力学约束量子格点模型中的表现。通过与海森堡绘景（Heisenberg picture）下局域算符动力学的形式类比，作者将算符动力学方法（如Krylov方法）移植到生长淬火问题，得到了Lanczos系数的线性增长猜想、Krylov空间与Fock空间中的局域化条件、Lyapunov指数上界，并在大N可解模型和1D East-West模型中验证了相关现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索“生长淬火”这一新兴非平衡动力学过程的基本性质，特别是其与算符动力学之间的深层联系，并利用该类比揭示假真空渐进失稳过程中的局域化、混沌与输运行为。

Method: 采用Krylov方法（递归方法，recursion method）分析Lanczos系数的渐近行为；构造大N可解生长淬火模型（借鉴Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev模型）；利用半经典方法分析非随机全连接生长淬火；通过保守荷与平带机制分析一维East-West模型中的Fock空间笼态（cage states）及其局域化。

Result: （1）在一般生长淬火中，Lanczos系数的对角元a_m ~ νm、非对角元b_m ~ αm呈线性增长；（2）当|ν| > 2α时，动力学在Krylov空间和Fock空间均局域化；（3）当|ν| < 2α时，Lyapunov指数λ_L ≤ √(4α² - ν²)，且该上界在大q SYK生长淬火中被饱和；（4）非随机全连接生长淬火几乎总是Fock局域化；（5）在一维East-West模型中，Fock空间笼态对应于一个守恒荷，该荷因流守恒而呈弹道输运，且微调跃迁项可因平带（flat band）诱导部分局域化。

Conclusion: 生长淬火是一种有前景的实现多体系统中非平衡相干现象的工具，其动力学可由算符增长假设（operator growth hypothesis）的推广来刻画，并在多种模型（SYK类、East-West模型）中展现出丰富的局域化与输运行为。

Abstract: We study growth quenches, which are local quenches that may gradually destabilize a false vacuum in certain kinetic constrained quantum lattice models, such as the East-West model. We point out a formal analogy with the dynamics of a local operator in the Heisenberg picture. Exploiting this analogy, we obtain several results on growth quenches by adapting operator-dynamics concepts and methods. First, applying the Krylov approach (recursion method), we conjecture the linear growth of Lanzcos coefficients in generic quenches, $a_m \sim νm$ (diagonal), and $b_m \sim αm$ (off-diagonal), extending an operator growth hypothesis. We show that the growth quench dynamics is localized in both Krylov and Fock spaces when $|ν| > 2 α$, and derive a bound for the growth quench analogue of Lyapunov exponent $λ_L \le \sqrt{4 α^2 - ν^2}$ when $|ν| < 2 α$. Second, we realize the Fock localization in large $N$ solvable growth quenches inspired by Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev (SYK) models. The bound on Lyapunov exponent is saturated in large-$q$ SYK grow quench. By contrast, the growth quench is almost always Fock localized in a nonrandom all-to-all growth quench amenable to semiclassics. Finally, in the 1D East-West model, we interpret Fock space cage states as the existence of a conserved charge. We show that the latter has ballistic transport due to current conservation. Moreover, adding hopping with a fine-tuned amplitude induces a partial localization due to a flat band. Our work suggest growth quenches as a promising approach to realize non-equilibrium coherent phenomena in many-body systems.

</details>

### [40] [Beyond descendants: integrable observables for cohomological field theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22236)
*Xavier Blot,Danilo Lewański,Sergey Shadrin*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文提出“可积可观测量（integrable observables）”概念，作为标准Witten psi类（2D量子引力中的descendants）的替代，用于耦合上同调场论（cohomological field theories）及其推广。通过三个实例（包括一个新的Π-类例子）展示其保持可积性的核心性质，并证明新Π-层次（hierarchies）与Dubrovin-Zhang层次及双分岔层次（double ramification hierarchies）之间存在Miura等价性，同时给出Witten猜想的一个极短新证明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准Witten psi类在耦合上同调场论时缺乏可积结构保持能力；本文旨在引入一种新型可观测量，使其在保留可积性（integrability）的同时，为可积系统理论提供统一框架，并揭示已有层次之间的深层联系。

Method: 定义可积可观测量（integrable observables）作为概念框架，替代Witten psi类与上同调场论耦合。通过三个具体实例进行验证：前两个分别恢复Dubrovin-Zhang层次和双分岔层次（double ramification hierarchies），第三个基于Π-类（Π-class）的近期性质进行推广。

Result: 新Π-层次（Π-hierarchies）与Dubrovin-Zhang层次及双分岔层次（double ramification hierarchies）之间存在Miura等价性（Miura equivalence）。此外，得到一个Witten猜想（Witten's conjecture）的极短新证明。

Conclusion: 可积可观测量框架不仅统一了已有的可积层次，还自然地将Π-类纳入可积系统理论中，并为Witten猜想提供了简洁的新证明途径，展示了该方法在理论物理和数学物理交叉领域的潜在价值。

Abstract: We introduce the concept of integrable observables and propose them as alternatives to the standard Witten's psi classes (a.k.a. descendants in $2D$ quantum gravity) to be coupled with cohomological field theories and their generalisations. The main property of integrable observables is that they retain the integrability properties.
  We present three examples of integrable observables. The first two recover the Dubrovin-Zhang and double ramification hierarchies, while revealing new structural features in this framework. The third, a new example, builds on recently established properties of the so-called $\mathbbΠ$-class, extending them and placing this class naturally within the theory of integrable systems.
  Notably, our integrable observables framework yields a proof that the new $\mathbbΠ$-hierarchies are Miura equivalent both to the Dubrovin-Zhang hierarchies and to the double ramification hierarchies. A new very short proof of Witten's conjecture is also provided.

</details>

### [41] [Flows on Graded Manifolds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22910)
*Rudolf Smolka,Jan Vysoky*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文在ℤ-分次几何（ℤ-graded geometry）中定义了向量场的流（flow），证明了每个向量场（在奇情形下需满足同调性条件）存在唯一最大流，并研究了流的交换性及与相关向量场对应的流之间的相互作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 向量场的流是微分几何中的基本工具，在理论和应用中均有大量用途。尽管该概念已在普通流形和超流形（supermanifold）上得到充分研究，但在ℤ-分次几何中尚无相关处理。ℤ-分次流形（ℤ-graded manifold）作为超流形的自然推广，允许坐标函数具有任意整数度，因此有必要填补这一空白。

Method: 论文首先在ℤ-分次流形上定义了向量场的流，然后证明了每个向量场（在奇度情形下假设该向量场是同调的（homological））均存在唯一最大流。接着考察了在流下保持不变的向量场，研究了两个向量场的流可交换的条件，并分析了与相关向量场对应的流之间的相互作用。

Result: 每个向量场在ℤ-分次流形上都存在唯一最大流，其中奇度情形需附加同调性条件。给出了流不变向量场的刻画，确定了流交换的条件，以及相关向量场之间的对应关系。

Conclusion: 本文首次系统建立了ℤ-分次几何中向量场流的理论框架，且主体部分保持简短，旨在让仅有最少ℤ-分次几何知识的读者也能理解。

Abstract: Flows of vector fields are an essential tool in differential geometry, with countless applications in both theory and practice. While they have been extensively studied for ordinary manifolds and supermanifolds, a treatment of flows in $\mathbb{Z}$-graded geometry is currently missing. $\mathbb{Z}$-graded manifolds constitute a natural generalization of supermanifolds, allowing functions in coordinates of arbitrary integer degree.
  In this paper, flows of vector fields on $\mathbb{Z}$-graded manifolds are defined, and it is proved that every vector field admits a unique maximal flow (in the odd case, under the assumption that the vector field is homological). Vector fields invariant under flows are examined. Conditions under which the flows of two vector fields commute are investigated, and the interaction between flows corresponding to related vector fields is studied.
  The main body of the paper is intentionally kept short, and we hope it is accessible to readers with only minimal prior knowledge of $\mathbb{Z}$-graded geometry.

</details>

### [42] [Asymmetric Scaling Laws from Sparse Features](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23591)
*John Sous,Michael Winer*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个稀疏激活（sparse activation）下的神经缩放定律（neural scaling laws）模型，揭示了由稀有坐标（rare coordinates）导致的独特瓶颈，推导了欠参数化和过参数化下的渐近损失及双下降（double-descent）行为，并分析了计算最优边界与梯度下降动力学。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有神经缩放定律主要针对稠密模型（dense models），而实际大规模模型中广泛存在稀疏激活现象，其带来的缩放行为尚不明确。本文旨在建立稀疏激活条件下的理论模型，揭示其与稠密模型不同的缩放机制。

Method: 通过构建一个包含稀疏激活的抽象模型，分析训练输入中从未观测到的稀有坐标对测试损失的主导作用。分别在欠参数化和过参数化两种机制下推导渐近总体损失（asymptotic population loss），并分析固定步长梯度下降（fixed-step gradient descent）的稳定性概率缩放律。

Result: 损失在插值阈值（interpolation threshold）附近出现双下降峰值，由两个不同的缩放指数（scaling exponent）控制——一个对应于过参数化区域，另一个对应于欠参数化区域，其间差距由稀疏度决定。计算最优边界（compute-optimal frontier）倾向于在固定计算预算下优先增加数据集规模而非模型容量。此外，稀疏诱导的效应在非线性激活函数下依然存在。

Conclusion: 稀疏激活引入了一种与稠密模型本质不同的缩放瓶颈，说明稀疏性对神经缩放定律具有深远影响，为设计更具计算效率的模型提供了理论指导。

Abstract: We introduce a model for neural scaling laws under sparse activations. In the model, test loss is often dominated by rare coordinates that are never observed in the training input. This mechanism induces a novel bottleneck absent from dense models. We derive the asymptotic population loss in both the underparameterized and overparameterized regimes, and show that the loss exhibits a double-descent peak near the interpolation threshold -- where the number of parameters is just sufficient to fit the training data -- resulting in a loss curve governed by two distinct scaling exponents -- one for the overparameterized regime and one for the underparameterized regime -- with a gap determined by the degree of sparsity. Additionally, we derive a compute-optimal frontier that favors increasing dataset size over model capacity under fixed compute budgets. We also analyze gradient-descent dynamics and identify a scaling law for the probability that fixed-step gradient descent becomes unstable. We further show that the sparsity-induced effect persists under nonlinear activations.

</details>

### [43] [Analysis of spin avalanches due to interplay of disorder and temperature](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23436)
*Niharika Bhuyan,Diana Thongjaomayum*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文通过在三角晶格上研究非平衡零温随机场伊辛模型（RFIM）的温度效应，发现幂律行为仅存在于低温或小到中等无序区域，且温度与无序对雪崩尺寸分布具有类似的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非平衡零温RFIM已被广泛用于理解无序驱动系统中的临界响应与雪崩现象，但以往研究局限于零温动力学。实际实验中温度不可避免，因此需要系统研究温度对幂律行为的影响。

Method: 在三角晶格上构建RFIM，通过改变温度、随机场强度和弛豫时间三个参数，考察它们对晶格上幂律行为普遍性的影响。

Result: 幂律行为仅存在于低温或小到中等无序参数的区域；温度与无序对雪崩尺寸分布（avalanche-size distribution）的影响具有相似性，且增加温度或无序会导致幂律行为逐渐模糊（blurring out）。

Conclusion: 温度与无序在破坏幂律行为上表现出强对应关系，这一发现有助于理解真实实验中温度不可避免时的临界行为。

Abstract: The nonequilibrium zero-temperature Random Field Ising Model (RFIM) has been extensively studied to understand critical response and avalanches in disordered driven systems. The emergence of power-law behaviour is observed over a wide region around the critical point. These studies however, are confined to zero-temperature dynamics. We study the role of temperature, which is inevitable in real experiments, in the context of RFIM on triangular lattices. We explore the interplay of different parameters: temperature, random field strength, and relaxation time which affect the prevalence of power-law behaviour on the lattice. The results indicate that power-law survives only in the regime of low temperature or small and intermediate disorder. Variations in temperature and disorder have similar affects on the avalanche-size distribution, indicating their strong correspondence. We also discuss the process of blurring out of the power law on increasing temperature or disorder.
