### [44] [Amorphous Radial Frustration and Water-Like Anomalies in a Ramp-Shoulder Fluid](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22951)
*Murilo S. Marques,Lucas Axel R. Santana,Gabriel San R. R. Câmara,José Rafael Bordin*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 通过分子动力学模拟，研究了由聚合物接枝纳米粒子有效相互作用衍生的三维粗粒化斜坡肩状流体的热力学、结构和动力学行为，发现密度、扩散和结构异常，以及这些异常部分解耦的层级关系，并揭示了无定形径向阻挫与异常扩散之间的关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在理解聚合物接枝纳米粒子粗粒化有效相互作用所衍生的斜坡肩状流体（ramp-shoulder fluid）的热力学、结构和动力学行为，特别是其异常现象（anomalies）的起源与层级关系。

Method: 采用粗粒化分子动力学（molecular dynamics）模拟，分析了径向分布函数（radial distribution function）、过量熵（excess entropy）、平移序（translational order）、取向序（orientational order）以及配位壳层（coordination-shell）组织等微观结构量。

Result: 该流体表现出密度、扩散和结构异常，但与各向同性核软化流体不同，其异常层级部分解耦：密度异常范围超出结构异常，扩散异常与无定形化（amorphization）和壳层迁移过程紧密相关。异常并非仅由壳层竞争控制，而是在径向关联增加但未形成晶态取向序的条件下，由协同径向重构（cooperative radial restructuring）涌现。

Conclusion: 软化相互作用区域的详细形状强烈影响压缩下的结构路径，导致一种无定形径向阻挫（amorphous radial frustration）状态，该状态与异常扩散和受阻碍的壳层重组相关联。

Abstract: We investigate the thermodynamic, structural, and dynamic behavior of a three-dimensional coarse-grained ramp-shoulder fluid derived from effective interactions between polymer-grafted nanoparticles. The interaction combines a softened repulsive ramp with a shallow attractive shoulder, stabilizing competing local organizations over a broad pressure interval. Molecular dynamics simulations reveal density, diffusion, and structural anomalies together with crystalline, amorphous, and fluid regions in the phase diagram. Unlike conventional isotropic core-softened fluids, the anomalous hierarchy becomes partially decoupled: the density anomaly extends beyond the structural anomaly, while the diffusion anomaly becomes closely connected to amorphization and shell migration processes. Analysis of radial distribution functions, excess entropy, translational and orientational order, and coordination-shell organization shows that the anomalies are not controlled solely by shell competition. Instead, they emerge from cooperative radial restructuring in a regime where radial correlations increase without the development of crystalline orientational order. The results indicate that the detailed shape of the softened interaction region strongly influences the structural pathways explored under compression, leading to a regime of amorphous radial frustration associated with anomalous diffusion and frustrated shell reorganization.

### [45] [Nonlinear Wave Propagation in 1D Polycatenated Ring Chains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23001)
*Xiaoxiao Xiong,Reo Yanagi,Tingtao Zhou,Chiara Daraio*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文研究了一维多环链（polycatenated ring chains）中的非线性波动力学，通过实验、有限元建模和离散粒子模拟，揭示了由拉伸激活和内部弯曲模量驱动的非线性波传播现象，并展示了通过几何参数调节波速与非线性特性的可调控性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统颗粒晶体（granular crystals）中非线性波的传播特性受限于固定材料常数，而多环链这类互锁结构因其内部结构柔性（structural flexibility）和拉伸激活机制（tensile activation）可能提供更丰富的调控手段，目前该体系中的非线性波动行为尚未被系统研究。

Method: 采用动态冲击实验（dynamic impact experiments）、有限元建模（finite-element modeling）和离散粒子模拟（discrete-particle simulations），对受重力预拉伸的垂直多环链进行系统研究。

Result: 观察并解释了以紧凑波前（compact leading wavefront）伴随持续尾部振荡（persistent trailing oscillations）为特征的非线性波，该振荡源于能量分配到环的内部弯曲模态（internal bending modes）。进一步发现系统非线性可通过改变环的几何长径比（aspect ratio）和接触角（contact angles）进行调节，从而调控有效接触指数（effective contact exponent）和波速的振幅标度（amplitude scaling）。

Conclusion: 本文在经典颗粒晶体非线性波传播研究的基础上，建立了多环链系统作为一种高度可调控、可设计的平台，用于研究和控制非线性动力学。

Abstract: We study the nonlinear wave dynamics of one-dimensional chains of polycatenated rings. These interlocked structures support amplitude-dependent nonlinear wave propagation driven by tensile activation and internal structural flexibility, unlike traditional granular crystals. Through dynamic impact experiments, finite-element modeling, and discrete-particle simulations of vertical chains pretensioned by gravity, we observe and explain nonlinear waves characterized by a compact leading wavefront followed by persistent trailing oscillations, which arise from energy partitioning into the rings' internal bending modes. Further, we demonstrate that the system's nonlinearity is not a fixed material constant. By altering the rings' geometric aspect ratio and contact angles, we can tune the effective contact exponent and the amplitude scaling of the wave speed. This work builds upon nonlinear wave propagation in classical granular crystals and establishes polycatenated systems as a highly tunable and designable platform to study and control nonlinear dynamics.

</details>


### [46] [Mean first passage time of chiral active Brownian particles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23095)
*Sarafa A. Iyaniwura,Mingfeng Qiu,Zhiwei Peng*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文研究了手性活性布朗粒子（chiral active Brownian particles, CABPs）在一维和二维受限区域中的逃逸动力学，推导了高手性（high-chirality）情形下的闭合渐近解，并通过数值求解偏微分方程计算了平均首次通过时间（mean first passage time, MFPT）。结果表明，MFPT 随手性（chirality）变化呈现非单调行为，存在一个最优手性值使逃逸时间最小化，揭示了手性可作为受限系统中输运和搜索的关键控制参数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手性活性布朗粒子（CABPs）具有内在旋转动力学，其圆形轨迹常见于生物和合成微游动体（microswimmers）。理解CABPs在受限环境中的探索和目标定位行为，对于表征物理和生物系统中的输运、搜索效率及反应过程至关重要。

Method: 在一维情形下，研究具有两个吸收边界（absorbing boundaries）或一侧为反射边界（reflecting boundary）另一侧为吸收边界的区间，推导高手性（high-chirality）区域的闭合渐近解。在二维情形下，分析包含单个吸收弧（absorbing arc）或两个对称吸收弧的圆盘逃逸问题，通过数值求解偏微分方程（partial differential equations）计算MFPT。

Result: 推导出一维情形下MFPT随粒子旋转速度（手性）变化的定量标度关系。在二维情形下，MFPT随粒子初始取向、自推进速度、角速度和域几何形状变化，且表现出非单调行为：存在一个中间最优手性值，使逃逸时间最小化。

Conclusion: 该工作为CABPs在典型受限区域中的逃逸动力学提供了全面表征，并指出手性（chirality）可作为受限物理和生物系统中输运与搜索的关键控制参数。

Abstract: Chiral active Brownian particles (CABPs) are self-propelled agents with intrinsic rotational dynamics, giving rise to circular trajectories commonly observed in biological and synthetic microswimmers. Understanding how CABPs explore confined environments and locate targets is crucial for characterizing transport, search efficiency, and reaction processes in physical and biological systems. We study the escape dynamics of CABPs from one- and two-dimensional confined domains. In one dimension, we consider intervals with either two absorbing boundaries or a reflecting boundary on one side and an absorbing boundary on the other, and derive closed-form asymptotic solutions in the high-chirality regime, revealing the quantitative scaling of the mean first passage time (MFPT) as a function of particle rotation speed (chirality). In two dimensions, we analyze escape from a disk containing one absorbing arc or two symmetric absorbing arcs. By numerically solving the governing partial differential equations, we compute the MFPT for CABPs to escape the domains as a function of the particle's initial orientation, self-propulsion speed, angular velocity, and domain geometry. Our results show that, depending on the parameters and geometry, the MFPT can exhibit non-monotonic behavior as a function of chirality. There exists an optimal chirality at an intermediate value that minimizes the escape time. Our work offers a comprehensive characterization of CABP escape dynamics in canonical confinements and identifies chirality as a key control parameter for transport and search in confined physical and biological systems.

</details>


### [47] [Memory-driven topological ordering during the transition from dormant to migrating epithelia](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23339)
*Richard Ho,Anna Lång,Emma Lång,Stig Ove Bøe,Luiza Angheluta*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文揭示静止上皮单层（quiescent epithelial monolayers）中储存的空间收缩应力充当一种力学记忆（mechanical memory）；血清诱导再激活后，这些预应力区域成核生成伸展星形结构并发射传播的极性畴界（polarity domain walls），沿界面发生拓扑缺陷（topological defects）的产生、平流和湮灭，导致缺陷粗化（defect coarsening）的动力学快于弹性相互作用。活性弹性模型（active elastic model）定量再现了观测动力学，并将储存应力确定为快速拓扑重组的起源。该机制与传统的去堵塞（unjamming）和群集（flocking）转变截然不同。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 上皮从静止到集体迁移（collective migration）的转变在伤口愈合和癌症侵袭中至关重要，但其物理起源尚不清楚（poorly understood）。

Method: 结合实验观测与活性弹性模型（active elastic model），通过血清诱导静止上皮单层再激活，追踪其应力释放与拓扑缺陷动力学。

Result: 静止上皮单层储存空间收缩应力作为力学记忆；再激活后预应力区域成核伸展星形（extensile asters）并发射传播的极性畴界；沿畴界产生、平流和湮灭拓扑缺陷，缺陷粗化动力学快于弹性相互作用。活性弹性模型定量再现了观测结果。

Conclusion: 建立了一种基于力学记忆触发活性应力释放的机制，通过快速拓扑有序化驱动集体迁移，该机制区别于传统的去堵塞转变和群集转变。

Abstract: Transitions from quiescence to collective migration in epithelia underlie wound healing and cancer invasion, yet their physical origin remains poorly understood. Here we show that quiescent epithelial monolayers store spatially contractile stresses that function as a form of mechanical memory. Upon serum-induced reactivation, these pre-stressed regions nucleate extensile asters that emit propagating polarity domain walls. Along these interfaces, topological defects are created, advected and annihilated, leading to defect coarsening with faster kinetics than by elastic interactions. An active elastic model quantitatively reproduces the observed dynamics and identifies stored stress as the origin of rapid topological reorganization. Our results establish a mechanism in which mechanical memory in quiescent epithelia triggers active stress release, driving collective migration via rapid topological ordering, distinct from conventional unjamming and flocking transitions.

### [48] [Orientational frustration drives enhanced diffusion of anisotropic particles in a liquid labyrinth](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23340)
*Rohit Mangalwedhekar,Limeng Ruan,Somen Nandi,Quentin Gresil,Marc Tondusson,Stephane Bancelin,Lea-Laetitia Pontani,Laurent Cognet*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过三维单粒子追踪技术，研究了一维碳纳米管在由互联腔室和收缩通道构成的软物质网络中的扩散行为，发现了一种对齐介导的输运机制：长纳米管通过与收缩通道动态对齐实现高效逃逸，从而将束缚强度与逃逸动力学解耦，这与传统的孔隙介导输运机制截然不同。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 复杂结构环境中纳米尺度物体的输运对诸多过程至关重要，如细胞外空间中的生物分子动力学以及多孔材料（如过滤器和催化剂）中的输运。虽然反常扩散（anomalous diffusion）已被充分认识，但粒子各向异性（particle anisotropy）如何在几何约束下主导输运仍不清楚。

Method: 采用三维单粒子追踪（3D single-particle tracking）技术，研究刚性一维碳纳米管在连续软物质网络（由互联腔室和收缩通道组成）中的扩散行为。

Result: 输运表现为反常且反持续（antipersistent），具有强烈的长度依赖的束缚和俘获效应，符合受阻扩散的特征。然而，逃逸束缚对纳米管长度不敏感：尽管长度增加十倍、俘获显著增强，逃逸时间仅增加约1.4倍。长纳米管（长度与腔室尺寸相当）会动态对齐于收缩通道，实现几何辅助的逃逸；而短纳米管则需要扫描整个体积以寻找逃逸路径。

Conclusion: 研究发现了一种对齐介导的输运机制（alignment-mediated transport mechanism），该机制将束缚强度与逃逸动力学解耦，区别于传统的孔隙介导输运（pore-mediated transport）机制，为复杂环境中各向异性扩散建立了定量框架。

Abstract: Transport of nanoscale objects in complex, structured environments plays a key role in a wide range of processes, from biomolecular dynamics in extracellular spaces to transport in porous materials such as filters and catalysts. While anomalous diffusion is well established, how particle anisotropy governs transport under geometric constraints remains unclear. Here we use 3D single-particle tracking to investigate the diffusion of stiff one-dimensional carbon nanotubes in a continuous soft matter network of interconnected chambers and constrictions. Transport is anomalous and antipersistent, with strong length dependent confinement and trapping, consistent with obstructed diffusion. Unexpectedly, however, escape from confinement is poorly sensitive to nanotube length as opposed to what would be expected of pore mediated transport. Despite a tenfold length increase and significantly enhanced trapping, escape time increased by only ~1.4. Single-particle orientational tracking reveals the origin of this weak scaling. Indeed, long nanotube, i.e. those with length comparable to the chamber dimensions, dynamically align with constrictions enabling efficient, geometry-assisted escape that offsets increased confinement while shorter nanotubes need to screen the volume to find their escape path. These results uncover an alignment-mediated transport mechanism that decouples confinement strength from escape kinetics, distinct from pore-mediated transport mechanisms, establishing a quantitative framework for anisotropic diffusion in complex environments.

</details>


### [49] [Nonreciprocal surface tension: anisotropy-induced defect motility and organization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23425)
*Laya Parkavousi,Suropriya Saha*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文在非互易Cahn-Hilliard（Nonreciprocal Cahn-Hilliard）模型框架下，研究了界面非互易性（interfacial nonreciprocity）如何改变守恒标量场（conserved scalar fields）中的缺陷动力学。非互易表面张力单独即可产生间歇性稳定缺陷，导致系统尺度靶向图案（target patterns）的形成、失稳、自毁与重新成核。当体效应与界面效应以特定方式耦合时，系统形成一种独特的马赛克波态（mosaic-wave state），其中行波在由运动位错（motile dislocations）线性排列划定的有限域内保持相干性。马赛克波在远大于行波平均波长的尺度上表现出无标度涨落（scale-free fluctuations）。作者通过构建Goldstone模（Goldstone-mode）动力学来解释涌现动力学，其大尺度涨落的非线性属于各向异性Kardar-Parisi-Zhang（Kardar-Parisi-Zhang, KPZ）普适类，非线性各向异性（anisotropic nonlinearity）的符号控制着非平衡动力学的性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解界面非互易性（即界面相互作用不满足作用-反作用对称性）对非平衡系统中缺陷动力学和图案形成的影响，揭示超越传统互易系统的涌现现象。

Method: 采用非互易Cahn-Hilliard模型（Nonreciprocal Cahn-Hilliard model）作为理论框架，通过构建Goldstone模（Goldstone-mode）动力学来解析系统的大尺度涨落行为，并将非线性动力学归类到各向异性Kardar-Parisi-Zhang（anisotropic KPZ）普适类。

Result: 发现了两种由非互易性诱导的新奇动力学态：间歇性靶向图案和由运动位错（motile dislocations）作为相滑移线（lines of phase slip）界定的马赛克波态（mosaic-wave state）。马赛克波在远超平均波长的尺度上呈现无标度涨落（scale-free fluctuations）。

Conclusion: 界面非互易性是产生丰富非平衡缺陷动力学的关键机制，所建立的Goldstone模动力学揭示了其与各向异性KPZ普适类（anisotropic KPZ universality class）的深层联系，非线性各向异性的符号（sign of the anisotropic nonlinearity）可作为调控非平衡动力学性质的控制参数。

Abstract: We show that interfacial nonreciprocity transforms defect dynamics in conserved scalar fields within the framework of the Nonreciprocal Cahn-Hilliard model. Nonreciprocal surface tension alone produces intermittently stable defects: system-spanning target patterns form, lose stability, self-destruct, and nucleate again from a defect-chaotic state. When bulk and interfacial contributions interplay in a particular way, the system forms a distinct mosaic-wave state: traveling waves remain coherent within finite domains demarcated by linear arrangements of motile dislocations, which act as lines of phase slip. Mosaic-waves exhibit scale-free fluctuations at length scales much larger than the average wavelength of the traveling patterns. To explain the wide range of emergent dynamics, we construct the dynamics of the Goldstone-mode. The nonlinearities governing its large-scale fluctuations belong to the anisotropic Kardar-Parisi-Zhang universality class, with the sign of the nonlinear anisotropy controlling the nature of the out-of-equilibrium dynamics.

</details>

### [50] [Correlated $b \to s$ and $s \to d$ Rare Semileptonic Transitions in the Standard Model Effective Field Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23759)
*Nilakshi Das,Rusa Mandal,Praveen S Patil*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在标准模型有效场论（SMEFT）框架下对半轻子味改变中性流过程进行了综合分析，涵盖b→s和s→d跃迁。通过联合拟合允许复数值的Wilson系数，发现左手四费米子算符主导b→s数据解释，而味普遍性耦合会增强稀有轻子衰变分支比从而与实验冲突，因此需要引入最小味破坏（MFV）或U(3)^5/U(2)^5对称性框架。同时分析了中微子对不变质量平方和CP破坏的敏感性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: B介子衰变中的反常现象（anomalies）尚未完全消除，为探索标准模型（Standard Model, SM）之外的新物理提供了持续动力。本文旨在系统性地研究半轻子味改变中性流过程，以解释当前实验数据并对未来实验提出可检验预言。

Method: 在标准模型有效场论（Standard Model Effective Field Theory, SMEFT）框架下，对b→s和s→d跃迁进行联合拟合，允许相关维度-6 Wilson系数（Wilson coefficients）取复数值。同时分析了双中微子不变质量平方的微分分布，以及重构变量q²_rec在B→K^(*)νν衰变中的新物理算符区分能力。

Result: 左手四费米子算符（four-fermion operators involving left-handed quark and lepton doublets）为当前b→s数据提供了最优描述，同时修正Z玻色子耦合的电弱算符也对拟合改进起重要作用。味普遍性（flavor-universal）SMEFT耦合会导致稀有半轻子Kaon衰变分支比大幅增强，与实验上限冲突；而基于U(3)^5和U(2)^5的味对称框架能自然恢复CKM层级结构并使预言符合数据。复Wilson系数可在特定q²区域产生百分之几量级的CP不对称性（CP asymmetry）效应。

Conclusion: 当前b→s反常数据可用左手四费米子算符和修正Z耦合的电弱算符共同描述。味普遍性耦合因与Kaon衰变实验抵触而需要最小味破坏（Minimal Flavor Violation, MFV）机制，U(3)^5和U(2)^5对称性框架是有效的实现方式。中微子衰变和CP不对称性测量对区分不同新物理算符具有重要敏感性。

Abstract: The persistent anomalies observed in $b \to s\,(\ell^+\ell^-,\,ν\barν)$ transitions continue to provide strong motivation for exploring possible extensions of the Standard Model (SM). Motivated by these discrepancies, we present a comprehensive analysis of semileptonic flavor changing neutral current processes within the Standard Model Effective Field Theory (SMEFT), encompassing both $b \to s\,(μ^+μ^-,\,ν\barν)$ and $s \to d\,(μ^+μ^-,\,ν\barν)$ transitions. We perform a combined fit to $b \to s\,(μ^+μ^-,\,ν\barν)$ observables, allowing the relevant dimension-six Wilson coefficients to be complex. We find that the four-fermion operators involving left-handed quark and lepton doublets provide the preferred description of the current $b \to s$ data, while the electroweak operator modifying the $Z$-boson couplings also plays an important role in improving the fit. We show that flavor-universal SMEFT couplings lead to strongly enhanced rare semileptonic kaon decay branching ratios, in conflict with current experimental bounds and thus motivating the implementation of Minimal Flavor Violation. In particular, we demonstrate that flavor-symmetric frameworks based on $U(3)^5$ and $U(2)^5$ naturally restore the required CKM hierarchies and bring the predicted kaon observables into agreement with present data. We further analyze the differential distributions with respect to the dineutrino invariant mass squared $q^2$, as well as the reconstructed variable $q^2_{\mathrm{rec}}$, in $B \to K^{(*)}ν\barν$ decays, demonstrating their sensitivity to different new physics operators. In addition, we investigate the impact of complex Wilson coefficients on $\mathcal{CP}$ asymmetries in $B \to K^{(*)}μ^+μ^-$ decays and find that percent-level effects can arise in specific $q^2$ regions.

### [52] [Scale-Invariant Open Quantum Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22919)
*Carlos Argüelles,Gabriela Barenboim,Gonzalo Herrera,Tanvi Krishnan,Héctor Sanchis*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文为与尺度不变环境（scale-invariant environments）耦合的开放量子系统建立了完整理论框架，证明此类环境由具有单一标度维度（scaling dimension）$d_{\mathcal{U}}$ 的unparticle库（unparticle baths）普适描述，推导了非马尔可夫记忆核（non-Markovian memory kernels）与分数阶Caldeira-Leggett主方程（fractional Caldeira-Leggett master equation），并在量子伊辛模型、暴涨宇宙学和高能中微子三个物理系统中展示了其丰富的相结构与可观测效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开放量子系统（open quantum systems）与尺度不变环境的耦合缺乏统一的理论描述。现有框架（如Caldeira-Leggett和Lindblad方法）无法处理此类环境中由标度维度导致的非马尔可夫（non-Markovian）动力学与普适相结构。本文旨在填补这一空白，提供严格的唯一性定理证明及完整的动力学形式。

Method: 通过唯一性定理（uniqueness theorem）证明尺度不变环境必然由unparticle bath描述，其特征参数为单一标度维度 $d_{\mathcal{U}}$。在此基础上推导非马尔可夫记忆核、包含真空与热贡献的精确噪声核（exact noise kernel），以及任意 $d_{\mathcal{U}}$ 下的分数阶Caldeira-Leggett主方程。并将该框架应用于三个物理系统：临界量子伊辛模型（quantum Ising model at criticality）、暴涨宇宙学中的德西特时空（de Sitter spacetime）以及高能天体物理中微子（high-energy astrophysical neutrinos）。

Result: 标度维度 $d_{\mathcal{U}}$ 决定了丰富的相结构：$d_{\mathcal{U}}=3/2$ 处存在热化相变（thermalization transition），$d_{\mathcal{U}}=2$ 为欧姆边界（Ohmic boundary），$d_{\mathcal{U}}=5/2$ 为热区退相干相变（decoherence transition），超越此界限后长时间量子相干性（long-time quantum coherence）得到保护。在 $(1+1)$ 维临界伊辛模型中 $d_{\mathcal{U}}=3/2$ 产生 $1/f$ 噪声；$(2+1)$ 维情形通过共形自举（conformal bootstrap）给出 $d_{\mathcal{U}}\approx 1.413$。德西特时空中无质量标量场与引力子库对应 $d_{\mathcal{U}}=2$，预测与量子-经典过渡一致的线性退相干增长。中微子的退相干率 $\Gamma_{\mathrm{decoh}}\propto \mathcal{B}(E,T_{\mathcal{U}})L^{5-2d_{\mathcal{U}}}$ 为标度维度提供了可观测特征。

Conclusion: 本文建立的框架提供了尺度不变环境中开放量子系统的普适描述，其相结构超越传统Caldeira-Leggett和Lindblad方法的适用范围。该理论在囚禁离子模拟器（trapped-ion simulators）、中微子望远镜（neutrino telescopes）和超导量子比特（superconducting qubits）等实验平台上具有可验证的预测能力，为量子退相干与标度不变环境的交叉研究奠定了基础。

Abstract: We develop a complete theoretical framework for open quantum systems coupled to scale-invariant environments. We show that such environments are universally described by unparticle baths characterized by a single scaling dimension $d_{\mathcal{U}}$. This work provides the proof of the uniqueness theorem, the formalism of the resulting non-Markovian dynamics, and applications to several physical systems.
  From the uniqueness theorem, we derive the non-Markovian memory kernels, the exact noise kernel including vacuum and thermal contributions, and a fractional generalization of the Caldeira-Leggett master equation for arbitrary $d_{\mathcal{U}}$. The scaling dimension governs a rich phase structure, including a thermalization transition at $d_{\mathcal{U}}=3/2$, the Ohmic boundary at $d_{\mathcal{U}}=2$, and a decoherence transition at $d_{\mathcal{U}}=5/2$ in the thermal regime, beyond which long-time quantum coherence is protected.
  Three realizations are studied. For the quantum Ising model at criticality, coupling to the energy operator in $(1+1)$ dimensions gives $d_{\mathcal{U}}=3/2$, producing $1/f$ noise, while the $(2+1)$D case yields $d_{\mathcal{U}}\approx1.413$ from the conformal bootstrap. In inflationary cosmology, massless scalar and graviton baths in de Sitter spacetime give $d_{\mathcal{U}}=2$, predicting linear decoherence growth consistent with the quantum-to-classical transition. For high-energy astrophysical neutrinos, the decoherence rate $Γ_{\mathrm{decoh}}\propto \mathcal{B}(E,T_{\mathcal{U}})L^{5-2d_{\mathcal{U}}}$ provides an observable signature of the scaling dimension.
  We also compare the framework with Caldeira-Leggett and Lindblad approaches, analyze the validity regimes, and discuss experimental implications for trapped-ion simulators, neutrino telescopes, and superconducting qubits.

</details>

This scenario provides a promising avenue for exploring extensions beyond the Standard Model and motivates further experimental and theoretical studies.

### [54] [Yukawa-Screened Bose-Star Condensation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23206)
*Jiajun Chen*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究 Yukawa-Schrödinger-Poisson (YSP) 系统中的玻色星形成过程。有限相互作用范围抑制了导致玻色星凝聚的红外动力学弛豫，从而改变了平衡态玻色星结构与凝聚时间尺度。通过推导屏蔽动力学凝聚公式、分析静态解以及全动力学数值模拟，发现 Yukawa 屏蔽效应会拓宽玻色星密度轮廓并系统性地延迟凝聚过程，与理论预测在拟合单一归一化参数后吻合良好。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在 Yukawa 相互作用（有限力程）下，玻色星（Bose-star）的凝聚行为如何受到屏蔽效应的影响，特别是与牛顿引力情形（无限力程）的差异。

Method: 推导了屏蔽动力学凝聚公式（screened kinetic condensation formula），将普通的引力库仑对数（gravitational Coulomb logarithm）替换为有限 Yukawa 输运对数（finite Yukawa transport logarithm）。求解了静态 YSP 方程以获得平衡态解。并采用全动力学赝谱模拟（fully dynamical pseudospectral simulations）对均匀各向同性初始条件进行了时间演化。

Result: Yukawa 屏蔽效应使玻色星的密度轮廓比牛顿孤子（Newtonian soliton）更宽。动力学模拟表明，Yukawa 屏蔽会系统性地延迟玻色星的凝聚过程。在拟合单一整体归一化参数后，模拟结果与屏蔽动力学预测吻合良好。

Conclusion: 有限相互作用范围通过削弱红外动力学弛豫（infrared kinetic relaxation）同时影响平衡态结构与动力学过程；屏蔽效应是调控玻色星形成时间与空间分布的关键因素。

Abstract: We study Bose-star formation in a Yukawa-Schrödinger-Poisson (YSP) system. A finite interaction range suppresses the infrared kinetic relaxation responsible for Bose-star condensation, modifying both the equilibrium Bose-star structure and the condensation timescale. We derive a screened kinetic condensation formula in which the ordinary gravitational Coulomb logarithm is replaced by a finite Yukawa transport logarithm. Static YSP solutions show that Yukawa screening broadens the Bose-star density profile relative to the ordinary Newtonian soliton. Fully dynamical pseudospectral simulations with homogeneous and isotropic initial conditions demonstrate that Yukawa screening systematically delays Bose-star condensation, in good agreement with the screened kinetic prediction after fitting a single overall normalization parameter.

</details>

### [55] [Fractionalization, emergent SU($N$) symmetries, and fragmentation in layered quantum spin-orbital models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22908)
*Pedro M. Cônsoli,Aayush Vijayvargia,Onur Erten*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出了一族分层量子自旋-轨道模型，通过堆叠具有Kitaev型相互作用的平方晶格层并引入Ising自旋层间耦合，研究分数化（fractionalization）、非常规对称性破缺序及其共存。利用部分子构造（parton construction）将低能哈密顿量映射到半填充π-流平方晶格上的N分量费米-哈伯德模型（Fermi Hubbard model），发现等强度全连接层间耦合极限下系统涌现出SU(N)对称性。对N=3情况的平均场计算揭示了交织序与味道选择性局域化（flavor-selective localization）等丰富现象，其基态实现不同形式的磁分裂（magnetic fragmentation），其中轨道保持量子液体态而自旋呈现常规长程序或由非平庸弦序参量（string order parameter）表征的非局域序。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 提出一类可解析处理的分层量子自旋-轨道模型平台，用以研究分数化激发、非常规对称性破缺序以及两者可能共存的物理机制。

Method: 通过堆叠N层具有Kitaev型相互作用的平方晶格系统构建模型，层间以Ising自旋相互作用耦合；利用部分子构造将低能哈密顿量映射到半填充π-流平方晶格上的N分量费米-哈伯德模型；对N=3有效模型采用平均场理论计算零温相图。

Result: 发现等强度全连接层间耦合极限下系统涌现SU(N)对称性；N=3平均场相图呈现交织序和味道选择性局域化；基态实现不同形式的磁分裂，轨道保持量子液体态，自旋呈现常规长程序或由非平庸弦序参量表征的非局域序。

Conclusion: 该构造方案可扩展，并为不同分数化量子临界点（fractionalized quantum critical point）提供具体的微观模型。

Abstract: We propose a family of layered quantum spin-orbital models as a platform to study fractionalization, unconventional forms of symmetry-breaking order, and their possible coexistence. The models are built by stacking $N$ layers of a square-lattice system in which Kitaev-type interactions promote the formation of a $\mathbb{Z}_2$ quantum spin-orbital liquid and coupling the different layers via Ising spin interactions. Using a parton construction, we show how, at low energies, these Hamiltonians can be mapped to $N$-component Fermi Hubbard models on a $π$-flux square lattice at half filling. We also demonstrate that the models acquire an emergent SU($N$) symmetry in the limit of equal all-to-all interlayer couplings and argue that, for $N>2$, the proximity to this limit offers the potential to realize an array of competing phases. To illustrate this point, we compute the zero-temperature phase diagram of the effective $N=3$ Hubbard model within mean-field theory and uncover rich phenomena, including intertwined orders and flavor-selective localization. Mapping back to the original degrees of freedom reveals that the ground states realize distinct forms of magnetic fragmentation, wherein the orbitals remain in a quantum liquid state whereas the spins can present conventional long-range order or nonlocal order characterized by a nontrivial string order parameters. We highlight possible extensions of our construction as well as its potential to provide concrete microscopic models for different fractionalized quantum critical points.

### [56] [Tuning J$_1$-J$_2$ in Quasi-2D Triangular Lattice Antiferromagnet $α$-SrCr$_2$O$_4$ via Uniaxial Pressure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23133)
*Jazzmin Victorin,Shreenanda Ghosh,Seyed Koohpayeh,Chris Lygouras,Natalia Drichko*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过拉曼散射（Raman scattering）研究准二维反铁磁体α-SrCr₂O₄在单轴压力下的自旋动力学，发现单轴压力可有效调控该材料的磁各向异性（magnetic anisotropy），从而为在三角晶格反铁磁体中实现量子自旋液体（quantum spin liquid）态提供实验途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 三角晶格反铁磁体（triangular lattice antiferromagnet）作为阻挫磁晶格（frustrated magnetic lattice），被认为是实现共振价键态（resonating valence bond state）的候选平台。理论相图表明，在特定参数范围内可能存在量子自旋液体态，而通过施加单轴压力（uniaxial pressure）改变磁各向异性是一种潜在的调控途径。

Method: 对准二维反铁磁体α-SrCr₂O₄施加单轴压力，进行拉曼散射实验；结合自旋波（spin wave）和双磁振子态密度（two-magnon density of states）计算，对实验结果进行比较验证。

Result: 在常压下，α-SrCr₂O₄在奈尔温度T_N = 43 K以下形成长程螺旋磁序（long-range helical magnetic order），并在15.5 meV和40 meV处观察到与反铁磁有序相关的双磁振子激发（two-magnon excitation）。施加拉伸（compressive）压力使两个双磁振子特征峰相互远离（靠近），表明各向异性减小（增大）。拉曼活性声子（Raman active phonon）在压缩（拉伸）压力下向高频（低频）移动，表明压力有效传递并调控晶格。

Conclusion: 单轴压力可有效调控α-SrCr₂O₄的磁各向异性，实验结果与自旋波及双磁振子态密度的理论计算一致，为通过压力调控实现三角晶格反铁磁体中的量子自旋液体态提供了实验依据。

Abstract: Triangular lattice antiferromagnets first attracted attention as a frustrated magnetic lattice which can serve as a platform to realize the resonating valence bond state. While the triangular lattice itself was shown to support classical 120 degree order, many theoretical phase diagrams suggest a quantum spin liquid state within a small range of parameters. One possible avenue to achieve such a state is to tune the anisotropy of the triangular lattice antiferromagnet by applying uniaxial pressure. This motivated our Raman scattering study of quasi-two-dimensional antiferromagnet $α$-SrCr$_2$O$_4$ under applied uniaxial pressure. Under ambient conditions, $α$-SrCr$_2$O$_4$ develops long-range helical magnetic order below T$_N$ = 43 K. We identify two-magnon excitations associated with this long-range antiferromagnetic order below T$_N$ at 15.5 meV and 40 meV by comparison with spin wave calculations. We observe the two features from the two-magnon excitation shift away from (towards) each other under applied tensile (compressive) pressure, indicating a decrease (increase) in anisotropy. Raman active phonons show a shift to higher (lower) frequencies under applied compressive (tensile) pressure, indicating efficient transmission of pressure and tuning of the lattice. We show spin wave and two-magnon density of states calculations under uniaxial pressure are consistent with our experimental results.

Conclusion: 该工作为Cs₂RuO₄中由强阻挫驱动的量子临界行为提供了定量实验验证，并建立了确定其自旋哈密顿量完整参数集的可行方案。

Abstract: We report neutron diffraction under applied magnetic fields and complementary zero-field neutron spectroscopy measurements on Cs$_2$RuO$_4$. Previous work [Phys. Rev. B. 112, 134436 (2025)] identified a spin-flop-like transition accompanied by a quantum critical point within the ordered phase, attributed to strong frustration between alternating single-ion anisotropy planes. Here, we quantitatively confirm the predicted field evolution of the magnetic structure using neutron diffraction. Furthermore, analysis of the excitation spectrum within an SU(3) spin-wave framework resolves previously undetermined parameters of the minimal spin Hamiltonian and lifts the associated degeneracies.

### [58] [Kondo singlet from ferromagnetic coupling: an analog of Anderson-Morel superconductivity in the magnetic channel](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23755)
*Ewan Scott,Yaqi Chen,Michael Turaev,Tarkan Yzeiri,Chris Hooley,Krzysztof P. Wójcik,Michał P. Kwasigroch*

TL;DR: 本文研究磁杂质与传导电子海通过全向同性铁磁自旋交换耦合的系统，发现单杂质情况下存在参数区间使传统近藤效应（Kondo effect）在低温下发展并形成单重态基态；杂质晶格情形下则产生重费米液体（heavy Fermi liquid）态，其在广泛参数范围内能量上优于磁有序。这些效应被视为安德森-莫雷尔超导（Anderson-Morel superconductivity）的类比，并讨论了实验实现路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究铁磁自旋交换耦合系统中，当耦合强度依赖传导电子模式时，是否会出现与常规反铁磁近藤系统不同的强关联物理行为，特别是非磁有序的基态可能性。

Method: 采用解析与数值相结合的方法，分别针对单杂质和杂质晶格两种情形进行分析；通过类比安德森-莫雷尔超导机制进行理论论证。

Result: 在单杂质情形下，存在特定参数区间使传统近藤效应在低温下出现并形成单重态基态；在杂质晶格情形下，系统形成重费米液体态，且在广泛参数范围内该态的能量低于磁有序态。

Conclusion: 铁磁自旋交换耦合系统中可产生类似安德森-莫雷尔超导的效应，为重费米液体态的实现提供了新途径，并指出了实验验证的可行方向。

Abstract: We consider magnetic impurities coupled to a conduction sea via a fully isotropic ferromagnetic spin-exchange term, the strength of which depends on the conduction-electron modes involved in the scattering. In the single-impurity case we show both analytically and numerically that there exists a parameter regime in which the conventional Kondo effect develops at low temperatures, leading to a singlet ground state. In the case of a lattice of impurities, we show that this leads to a heavy Fermi liquid state that is energetically favored over magnetic ordering in a broad parameter range. We argue that these effects are analogs of Anderson-Morel superconductivity, and discuss routes to their experimental realization.

### [59] [Interaction-Split Edge Spectral Flow and Neutral Triplet Boundary Modes in a C = 2 Hubbard Pump](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23769)
*Yong-Feng Yang,Zhao-Rui Tian,Chen Cheng,Hong-Gang Luo*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过在哈伯德（Hubbard）模型中引入滑动空间调制，实现了一种多体休斯泵（many-body Thouless pump），其边界谱流（boundary spectral flow）被关联效应重构。密度矩阵重整化群（DMRG）计算表明，在填充数ρ=2/3的周期三哈伯德链上，出现了一个多体陈数C=+2的关联绝缘体，每个周期泵浦两个电荷。开边界条件下，自旋简并的参考泵在两个自旋通道中同时出现边缘流，而完整的调制哈伯德模型抑制了边界双占据通道，将谱流分裂为两个不同的边缘事件。全局μ-U相图揭示了填充依赖的拓扑性质：ρ=2/3区域保持C=+2，而ρ=4/3区域经历自旋能隙关闭，从C=-2泵转变为C=+1的拓扑莫特泵（topological Mott pump）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在强关联体系中，空间调制的哈伯德相互作用能否实现多体休斯泵，并研究关联效应对边界谱流和拓扑特性的重构作用。

Method: 采用密度矩阵重整化群（density-matrix renormalization group, DMRG）方法，对周期三哈伯德链（period-three Hubbard chain）进行数值计算，分析其填充数ρ=2/3和ρ=4/3下的多体陈数（many-body Chern number）、能隙结构以及开边界条件下的谱流行为。

Result: 在ρ=2/3时，系统为多体陈数C=+2的关联绝缘体，电荷能隙与中性自旋能隙分离；开边界下，完整调制模型抑制双占据通道，谱流分裂为两个边缘事件，其间边界电荷被中和并出现局域的自旋三重态激发。ρ=4/3时，系统从C=-2泵浦转变为C=+1的拓扑莫特泵。

Conclusion: 空间调制的哈伯德相互作用能够实现关联效应重构的拓扑泵浦，其边界流和拓扑相图具有填充依赖性，揭示了强关联系统中拓扑莫特泵浦的新机制。

Abstract: We show that a sliding spatial modulation of the on-site Hubbard interaction realizes a many-body Thouless pump whose boundary spectral flow is reconstructed by correlations. For a period-three Hubbard chain at filling $ρ=2/3$, density-matrix renormalization group (DMRG) calculations identify a correlated insulator with many-body Chern number $C=+2$, corresponding to two units of charge pumped per cycle. Its excitation spectrum separates the charge gap from the lowest neutral spin gap, revealing an interacting bulk response beyond a simple spin-degenerate band pump. Under open boundary conditions, this contrast becomes even more pronounced. A spin-degenerate Hartree/Aubry-André-Harper reference pump exhibits simultaneous edge flow in the two spin channels, whereas the full modulated Hubbard model suppresses the boundary doublon channel and splits the spectral flow into two distinct edge events. Between these events, the boundary charge is neutralized while a neutral, spinful triplet-like excitation is localized at the edge. The global $μ-U$ phase diagram reveals filling-dependent topology: the $ρ=2/3$ regime remains in the $C=+2$ sector, while $ρ=4/3$ regime undergoes a spin-gap-closing transition from a $C=-2$ pump to a distinct $C=+1$ topological Mott pump.

</details>

### [60] [Non-reciprocal Coulomb drag in a ballistic quantum wire](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22945)
*Suyang Cai,Mingyang Zheng,Nathan Rao,Glen Gillia,Rebika Makaju,Sadhvikas J. Addamane,Dominique Laroche*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文实验测量了弹道拖拽线（ballistic drag wire）构成的库仑拖拽（Coulomb drag）器件，发现在近乎纯净的量子线中，尽管拖拽线是弹道的，非互易（non-reciprocal）库仑拖拽信号仍然显著存在，其强度与互易分量相当，且温度依赖关系与扩散模型（diffusive model）吻合，而现有理论框架无法完全自洽地解释所有实验数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 一维库仑拖拽是探测一维系统中电子-电子相互作用的平台。在电荷涨落（charge fluctuation）形式下，介观器件中库仑拖拽信号的非互易分量被预测依赖于由内在无序（intrinsic disorder）导致的平移对称性破缺。实验旨在通过构建弹道拖拽线器件，研究近完美量子线（nearly pristine quantum wires）中的拖拽信号，以检验上述理论预测。

Method: 实验构建了一个包含弹道拖拽线的库仑拖拽器件，测量了拖拽信号在弹道条件下的行为。通过分析低偏压和低温下拖拽线电导的演化，以及温度依赖关系，研究了非互易分量的来源。同时，将拖拽线电导的偏压依赖关系拟合至三种理论模型，以提取相互作用参数（interaction parameter）和电导线的无序程度（disorder level）。

Result: 非互易分量的强度与互易分量（reciprocal component）相当，在弹道拖拽线中仍可被探测到；非互易信号的温度依赖关系呈现幂律行为（power-law temperature dependence），与扩散模型预测一致；互易分量的温度依赖关系无法用现有框架解释；三种模型均不能完全自洽地解释偏压依赖的实验数据。

Conclusion: 非互易信号可能来源于器件中的低能无序（low energy disorder），这与拖拽线在低偏压和低温下的电导演化一致。然而，现有理论模型尚无法对全部实验观测提供自洽的定量解释，表明目前对弹道一维系统中非互易库仑拖拽的机制理解仍不完善。

Abstract: 1D-Coulomb drag serves as a platform for probing electron-electron interactions in 1D systems. Under the charge fluctuation formalism, the non-reciprocal component of Coulomb drag signal in mesoscopic devices is predicted to rely on the breaking of translational invariance due to intrinsic disorder. In this work, we report the measurement of a Coulomb drag device with a ballistic drag wire, allowing us to study the drag signal in nearly pristine quantum wires. Surprisingly, a non-reciprocal component with strength comparable to that of the reciprocal component is still detected across the measured regime, despite the drag wire being ballistic. We suggest that the non-reciprocal signal arises from low energy disorder in the device, which is consistent with the evolution of the drag wire's conductance at low biases voltages and temperatures. Additionally, the non-reciprocal component of the drag signal shows a power-law temperature dependence that coincides with a diffusive model, while the reciprocal component's temperature dependence cannot be explained under the existing framework. The bias voltage dependence of the drag wire conductance is fitted into three models to extract the interaction parameter and disorder level within the wire, but none of the models provides a fully self-consistent explanation for the data.

</details>


### [61] [Surface States in Strain-Induced Nodal-Line Topological Semiconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23000)
*Vitaly N. Golovach,Alexander Khaetskii*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文基于简化的 Luttinger 哈密顿量模型，系统研究了在应变和自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）作用下反带半导体（inverted-band-gap semiconductors）的拓扑相图，分析了三维拓扑绝缘体、狄拉克半金属、节线半金属和外尔半金属之间的相变，并推导了表面态的解析解，揭示了表面态色散在投影节线处的非解析性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有文献对反带半导体中多种拓扑相的描述较为分散，缺乏统一的图像来理解不同拓扑相（如拓扑绝缘体、狄拉克半金属、节线半金属、外尔半金属）之间的连续演化关系。

Method: 采用最小化 Luttinger 哈密顿量模型（minimalistic Luttinger Hamiltonian model），沿高对称方向及若干极限情形下推导表面态（surface states）的解析解与精确解，并分析相边界处表面态的连续演化。

Result: 建立了从狄拉克半金属到节线半金属再到外尔半金属的连续演化路径；确定了实现各相的能量尺度层级（hierarchy of energy scales）；揭示了表面态色散在投影节线（projected nodal line）处的非解析性（non-analyticity），该行为源于动量空间中具有独特自旋织构（spin textures）的不同表面态斑块（terminating patches）的分离。

Conclusion: 该工作为反带半导体中拓扑相变提供了统一的描述框架，阐明了表面态在相边界处的连续演化机制，并对未来实验识别和调控这些拓扑相提供了理论依据。

Abstract: This work explores the topological phase diagram of inverted-band-gap semiconductors under strain and spin-orbit coupling. Using a minimalistic Luttinger Hamiltonian model, we follow the transitions between a 3D topological insulator, a Dirac semimetal, a nodal-line semimetal, and a Weyl semimetal. Analytical and exact solutions for surface states are derived for high-symmetry directions as well as in several limiting cases. We demonstrate the continuous evolution of these surface states across phase boundaries, providing a unified picture that synthesizes previous literature. Specifically, we detail the progression from a Dirac to a nodal-line and then to a Weyl semimetal as spin-orbit coupling originating from bulk inversion asymmetry is introduced. A hierarchy of energy scales is established, defining the criteria for realizing these phases. Finally, we reveal a non-analyticity in the surface-state dispersion at the projected nodal line, originating from distinct, terminating patches of surface states with unique spin textures in momentum space.

</details>

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文研究了量子反常霍尔效应（quantum anomalous Hall effect）作用下带隙二维材料的光学性质，发现低温下透射、反射和吸收系数仅依赖于光子能量与能隙能量之比，并呈现普适行为；当两者相等时出现全反射奇异行为。无带隙极限下可恢复石墨烯（graphene）结果，光学系数仅取决于精细结构常数（fine-structure constant）。这些光学性质可用于精确测量带隙。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过理论分析计算低温度下有带隙二维材料的透射、反射和吸收系数，重点关注光子能量与能隙能量之比对光学行为的影响，并通过无带隙极限情形与石墨烯已知结果进行对比验证。

Result: 发现光学系数在低温下具有仅依赖于光子能量与能隙能量之比的普适行为（universal behavior），且在二者相等时出现全反射奇异行为（singular behavior）。无带隙极限下恢复石墨烯结果，光学系数仅由精细结构常数决定。

Conclusion: 所观测的光学性质（optical properties）可用于精确测量带隙（bandgap），为二维材料能带结构的实验表征提供了新途径。

Abstract: We study the optical properties of gapped two-dimensional materials which are subject to the quantum anomalous Hall effect. At sufficiently low temperatures the transmission, reflection and absorption coefficients are found to have a universal behavior that depends only on the ratio of the photonic energy and the gap energy. There is a singular behavior with total reflection when these energies are equal. In the limit of a vanishing gap we recover results for graphene, where the optical coefficients depend only on the fine-structure constant. The observed optical properties provide an accurate measurement of the bandgap.

Abstract: Molecular rectifiers are key functional components of molecular-scale integrated circuits, yet achieving high rectification ratios remains a longstanding challenge due to the intrinsic symmetry of resonant tunneling and the complexity of interfacial energy-level alignment. Here, we propose a rectifier design strategy based on selective Fermi-level pinning that breaks transport symmetry via pinning interactions between molecular frontier orbitals and electrodes. The resulting cyclo[n]carbon-based molecular junctions exhibit giant rectification ratios exceeding 103, while retaining exceptional structural robustness against variations in both donor chain length and carbon ring size. Abstract: Wafer-scale growth of two-dimensional semiconductors remains a key challenge for their integration into photonic technologies. Here, we report wafer-scale growth of gallium selenide (GaSe) by metal-organic chemical vapor deposition (MOCVD) and investigate its structural and optical properties for visible-range classical and quantum light emission. ### [65] [Generalized Shift Vector as the Intrinsic Dipole of Many-Body Correlated Electronic States](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23431)
*Jiaming Hu,Sudipta Kundu,Zhichao Guo,Joshua J. P. Thompson,Wenbin Li,Hua Wang,Bartomeu Monserrat*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文证明，在非线性光学和输运现象中广泛使用的 shift vector（位移矢量）可更基本地理解为单个关联态（correlated state）的本征电偶极矩（intrinsic dipole moment）。通过将 shift vector 重新定义为单个关联态的内禀属性，统一了先前分散于不同物理场景（如光学诱导关联、电子-声子介导过程、激子态）中的位移矢量概念，并为位移电流（shift current）建立了共同的物理基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Shift vector 在非线性光学和输运现象中扮演核心角色，但传统上被理解为量子态之间跃迁所伴随的电荷中心偏移，缺乏更基本的单态层面解释。作者旨在揭示 shift vector 本质上是单个关联态的内在偶极性质，从而澄清规范不变性（gauge invariance）的局域与全局方面、相位梯度项（phase-gradient term）的起源及其与多体关联内部相干结构的关系。

Method: 作者从几何结构（geometric structure）角度出发，将 shift vector 重新推导为单个关联态的本征偶极矩。推导过程考虑了规范不变性的局域与全局方面，并建立了实空间联合概率密度（joint probability density）的位移与能量空间中线性电场修正之间的对应关系。随后将该框架应用于光学诱导关联、电子-声子介导过程和激子电子-空穴态等具体物理场景。

Result: 在新的单态框架下，作者恢复了先前已提出的各种 shift vector 表达式，并推导出位移电流的标准表达式作为特例。这些结果统一了原本来自不同物理过程（非线性光学、电子-声子耦合、激子态）中的 shift vector 定义。

Conclusion: Shift vector 的物理本质是关联电子态（correlated electronic states）的本征偶极属性（intrinsic dipolar properties），而非仅由态间跃迁决定。该发现为 shift vector 和相关物理现象（如位移电流）建立了统一的物理基础。

Abstract: Shift vectors play a central role in nonlinear optics and transport phenomena, where they are usually understood as charge-center shifts associated with transitions between quantum states. Here we show that the same geometric structure can be more fundamentally understood as the intrinsic dipole moment of a single correlated state. Our derivation clarifies the local and global aspects of gauge invariance, the origin of the phase-gradient term, and its connection to the internal coherence structure of many-body correlations. The single-state shift character appears both as a displacement of the real-space joint probability density and as a linear electric-field modification in energy space. Applying this framework to optically induced correlations, electron-phonon-mediated processes, and excitonic electron-hole states, we recover previously proposed shift vectors and the standard expression for the shift current as special cases. Our results establish a common physical foundation for shift vectors as intrinsic dipolar properties of correlated electronic states.

### [66] [Commensuration torques in double-moiré twisted trilayer hexagonal boron nitride and graphene heterostructures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23492)
*Youngju Park,Nicolas Leconte,Prathap Kumar Jharapla,Md Shaifullah,E. H. Hwang,Jeil Jung*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索双莫尔公度性（double-moiré commensuration）在扭转多层范德华（van der Waals）异质结构中对扭转角稳定性的影响，并理解其在不同材料体系中的系统依赖性。

Method: 采用大规模原子松弛（large-scale atomistic relaxations）方法，对双莫尔三层六方氮化硼（hBN）同质结构与石墨烯/hBN异质层结构进行模拟计算。

Result: 在扭转三层hBN中，双莫尔公度条件（θ₁₂ = -θ₂₃）对应局部能量极小值，伴随扭矩符号反转，结合能约0.2–0.3 meV/原子；在石墨烯/hBN异质层中，全局能量最低点可与双莫尔公度角重合（如约0.6°）；非公度结构因低能堆叠域重叠减少而稳定性降低，超润滑性增强；库仑静电相互作用可进一步增强稳定化能量。

Conclusion: 双莫尔公度性是一种普遍但系统依赖的扭转角稳定机制，其角度稳定性可通过扭矩大小与结合能定量表征。

Abstract: We study commensuration-driven torques and angle locking in double-moiré trilayer hexagonal boron nitride (hBN) and graphene heterostructures using large-scale atomistic relaxations. In twisted trilayer hBN (t3BN) homostructures, double-moiré commensuration ($θ_{12} = -θ_{23}$) give rise to local energy minima accompanied by torque sign reversals, signaling a restoring tendency toward the commensurate configuration. The corresponding binding energies are $\sim$0.2-0.3 meV/atom, originating from enhanced overlap of low-energy stacking domains, although the system is globally stable at zero twist. In contrast, in graphene/hBN heterolayers systems the global energy minimum can coincide with the double-moiré commensuration angle, particularly near $\sim$0.6$^{\circ}$, reflecting competition between lattice mismatch and interfacial relaxation. Incommensurate atomic structures have reduced stabilization due to suppressed overlap of low-energy stacking and have enhanced superlubricity due to spatial averaging of interfacial energies. These results establish double-moiré commensuration as a general, system-dependent mechanism for twist-angle stabilization, whose angular stability is characterized by the torque magnitude and binding energy. Coulomb electrostatic interactions further enhance the stabilization energy without changing the underlying physics.

### [67] [Momentum-Resolved Tunneling Modulation Induced Giant Multistate Resistance in Antiferroelectric Multiferroic Junction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23577)
*Wei Yang,Yibo Xu,Shen Li,Jiangchao Han,Jiayou Chen,Juan-Carlos Rojas-Sánchez,Stéphane Mangin,Xiaoyang Lin,Weisheng Zhao*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出一种双机制（dual mechanism）策略，基于Fe₃GaTe₂/双层In₂Se₃/Fe₃GaTe₂异质结构：(1) 反铁电（antiferroelectric, AFE）相变调制布洛赫波矢空间中衰逝衰减率（evanescent decay rate）的动量分辨分布；(2) 在Fe₃GaTe₂/α-In₂Se₃界面实现完美自旋过滤（spin filtering）。头部型与尾部型AFE态之间的转变保留了中心对称势能分布，但改变了衰逝态的动量分布。

Result: 该机制产生巨大的TER（约7.6×10³%），是传统铁电基MFTJ的4倍以上；TMR超过6.8×10⁵%，比典型MFTJ提高两个数量级。在室温下实现了六种不同的非易失电阻态（six distinct non-volatile resistance states）。

Conclusion: 该双机制成功解决了MFTJ中读写性能的权衡问题（resolve the performance trade-off），为多态非易失存储器和新型计算范式提供了一种可行的器件架构。

Abstract: Multiferroic tunnel junctions (MFTJs), integrating ferroelectric and ferromagnetic functionalities within a single nanoscale device, hold significant promise for non-volatile, multi-state memory and innovative computing paradigms. In conventional MFTJs, tunneling resistance modulation relies primarily on ferroelectric (FE) polarization switching, which alters interfacial electric fields and shifts the Fermi level of adjacent ferromagnetic electrodes. However, achieving high tunnelelectroresistance (TER) through this approach demands strong built-in electric fields, which simultaneously hinder FE polarization switching, creating an intrinsic trade-off between reliable data reading and efficient writing. Here, we propose a dual mechanism that combines antiferroelectric (AFE) phase-transition modulation of the evanescent decay states with interfacial spin filtering based on $Fe_3GaTe_2$/bilayer-$In_2Se_3$/$Fe_3GaTe_2$ heterostructure. Beyond altering the electrostatic potential as in AFE-FE switching, the transitions between head-type and tail-type AFE states preserve the centrosymmetric potential profile yet fundamentally modulate the momentum-resolved distribution of evanescent decay rates across the Brillouin zone. When integrated with perfect spin filtering at the $Fe_3GaTe_2$/$α$-$In_2Se_3$ interface, this mechanism yields a giant TER (~$7.6\times10^3\%$), over 4 times that of conventional FE-based MFTJs, and a TMR exceeding $6.8\times10^5\%$, enhanced by two orders of magnitude over typical MFTJs. These mechanisms resolve the performance trade-off in MFTJs, enabling six distinct non-volatile resistance states at room temperature.

### [68] [Graphene-based Photodetector with Engineered Hot Carrier Cooling Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23646)

Result: 实验结果显示，邻近屏蔽将热载流子冷却时间（cooling time）延长至原来的四倍，同时内禀光响应度提升了约50%。

Abstract: Graphene has emerged as a promising material for integration into silicon photonics, owing to its ultrafast and broadband photoresponse without the need for an external bias voltage. This photoresponse relies on the photo-thermoelectric effect created by hot carriers. A key factor underlying the performance of graphene photodetectors is the cooling dynamics of these hot carriers. In this work, we engineer these dynamics in a WSe2-graphene-WSe2 waveguide-integrated photodetector. In particular, by introducing proximity screening by a nearby graphite layer to this structure, we prolong the hot-carrier cooling time, leading to an enhanced photoresponse. We characterize the cooling dynamics under continuous-wave laser excitation by employing a photomixing technique, revealing an increase in the cooling time by up to a factor of four. Direct photoresponse measurements show that the internal photoresponsivity improves by approximately 50%. Together, these results demonstrate the potential of proximity screening to enhance the performance of graphene-based photodetectors on an integrated photonics platform.

### [69] [Nonreciprocal conductance in uniformly dissipative devices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23725)
*Oliver Solow,Emil J. Bergholtz,Karsten Flensberg*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究表明，均匀耗散电路（uniformly dissipative circuits）可以表现出非互易电导（nonreciprocal conductance），即两个非局域电导值不同。该现象通过左移电子与右移电子之间传输时间（transmission times）的差异得以解释，并以耗散Rashba纳米线（dissipative Rashba nanowire）与偏斜磁场（skewed magnetic field）构型为例，展示了这种传输时间差异如何通过电路内部的干涉产生，以及随耗散强度变化而改变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在非厄米电子系统（non-Hermitian electronic systems）的研究中，一个自然的问题是各种非厄米效应如何影响可测量的物理量（如电导）。本文旨在探究均匀耗散电路能否及如何产生非互易电导现象。

Method: 通过分析左移电子与右移电子之间传输时间的差异，来建立耗散与非互易电导之间的联系。以耗散Rashba纳米线与偏斜磁场构成的特定电路为例，考察干涉效应如何导致传输时间差异，以及该差异如何随耗散强度变化。

Result: 均匀耗散电路能够产生非互易电导；非互易性源于左、右移动电子传输时间的不同；在耗散Rashba纳米线加偏斜磁场的具体构型中，这种传输时间差异由电路内部的干涉效应引起，并受到耗散强度的调控。

Conclusion: 均匀耗散本身即可打破电导的互易性，为非厄米系统中可观测电学行为的研究提供了新的理论视角，暗示非互易电导可能是耗散系统中普遍存在的现象。

Abstract: When studying non-Hermitian electronic systems, an obvious question is how various non-Hermitian effects affect measurable quantities like the conductance. Here, we show that uniformly dissipative circuits can exhibit nonreciprocal conductance, meaning that the two nonlocal conductances are different. We describe how this happens through a difference in transmission times between left-moving and right-moving electrons. We consider a specific case of a dissipative Rashba nanowire with a skewed magnetic field, and show how this difference in transmission times comes about through interference inside the circuit, and how this is modified as the dissipation strength changes.

</details>


### [70] [Orbital Selective Dirac-like States in EuAgAs Revealed by Polarization Dependent ARPES and DFT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23836)
*Mohit Mudgal,Suman Nandi,Mohamed El Gazzah,Masashi Arita,Shin-ichiro Ideta,Nirmal J. Ghimire,Kenya Shimada,Anup Pradhan Sakhya*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本研究结合密度泛函理论（DFT）和角分辨光电子能谱（ARPES），系统分析了磁性拓扑狄拉克半金属候选材料EuAgAs的电子结构及轨道特性，揭示了准线性狄拉克色散、范霍夫奇点（van Hove singularity）以及激发能量与偏振对光电发射矩阵元的选择性调控作用，并发现其狄拉克态在9 K至30 K温度范围内几乎不受磁有序影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 磁性拓扑半金属（magnetic topological semimetals）因磁性与相对论性费米子（relativistic fermions）的耦合，有望实现反常输运效应和可调拓扑相。本研究旨在深入理解候选材料EuAgAs的电子结构及其轨道特征，以揭示其作为磁性拓扑狄拉克半金属的物理机制。

Method: 采用密度泛函理论（DFT）进行理论计算，并结合偏振依赖的角分辨光电子能谱（ARPES）进行实验测量；在9 eV光子能量下测量了费米面映射（Fermi surface mapping）和等能轮廓（constant energy contours），并在s和p偏振几何下开展偏振依赖的ARPES测量，以分析光电发射矩阵元（photoemission matrix elements）对激发能量和偏振的敏感性。

Result: 实验观察到环状费米面特征随结合能增大而系统性扩展，符合近线性狄拉克色散；不同光子能量的ARPES测量暗示了DFT预测的范霍夫奇点（van Hove singularity）的存在；s和p偏振下的ARPES表现出显著的光谱强度差异，表明对称选择性的轨道贡献；DFT计算成功复现了矩阵元驱动的强度调制；狄拉克态在9 K至30 K范围内几乎保持不变，表明磁有序对电子结构影响极小。

Conclusion: 研究结果提供了EuAgAs轨道选择性电子结构的详细理解，并讨论了其对磁性拓扑量子态（magnetic topological quantum states）的潜在意义。

Abstract: Magnetic topological semimetals provide a promising platform for emergent quantum phenomena driven by the interplay between magnetism and relativistic fermions, including anomalous transport effects and tunable topological phases. Here, we investigate the electronic structure and orbital character of EuAgAs, a magnetic topological Dirac semimetal candidate, using density functional theory (DFT) and polarization dependent angle resolved photoemission spectroscopy (ARPES). Fermi surface mapping and constant energy contours measured at 9 eV reveal ring like features that systematically expand with increasing binding energy, consistent with nearly linear low energy Dirac like dispersion. ARPES measurements at different photon energies hint at the presence of a van Hove singularity predicted by DFT calculations. Furthermore, this indicates that the photoemission matrix elements are highly sensitive to the excitation energy, allowing different photon energies to selectively probe distinct orbital characters. Polarization dependent ARPES measurements performed in s- and p-polarized geometries exhibit pronounced variations in spectral intensity, indicating symmetry selective orbital contributions to electronic states. These matrix element driven intensity modulations are well reproduced by DFT calculations. Furthermore, the observed Dirac like states remain nearly unchanged over the temperature range from 9 K to 30 K, suggesting that the magnetic ordering has minimal influence on the electronic structure. Our combined experimental and theoretical results provide detailed insight into the orbital selective electronic structure of EuAgAs and its implications for magnetic topological quantum states.

</details>

### [71] [Emergent heavy-tailed distributions from a Markovian random walk](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22933)
*Henrique S. Lima,Evaldo M. F. Curado*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出一种严格局域、离散时间马尔可夫的一维随机游走模型，通过位置依赖的步长正反馈机制产生幂律尾部统计，并解析得到稳态分布为对称类洛伦兹形式 $\rho_{\text{st}}(x) \propto (|x|/l+r\Delta x)^{-2}$，指数为-2的幂律衰减跨越六个数量级。利用Onsager-Machlup路径积分形式证明，非零初始加速度是驱动行走者远离原点、实现无标度统计与稳态分布可归一化的根本机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 复杂系统中重尾统计（heavy-tailed statistics）的传统解释依赖于非局域随机跳跃或非马尔可夫记忆（non-Markovian memory），本文旨在探索是否可以从严格局域、无记忆的马尔可夫机制（Markovian mechanism）中自然涌现出幂律行为（power-law behavior），为跨学科普遍存在的-2幂律提供新的微观基础。

Method: 构建一维离散时间马尔可夫随机游走（random walk），步长由行走者位置的确定性函数决定，从而形成正反馈循环（positive feedback loop）并沿轨迹产生强有效关联。在连续极限（continuum limit）下进行解析推导，并结合大规模数值模拟验证。采用Onsager-Machlup路径积分形式论（path-integral formalism）分析最短涨落轨迹上有效速度与加速度的物理意义。

Result: 该规则产生稳健的非高斯稳态，解析解为对称类洛伦兹分布 $\rho_{\text{st}}(x) \propto (|x|/l+r\Delta x)^{-2}$，确认渐近幂律尾部以 $|x|^{-2}$ 衰减且跨越六个数量级。Onsager-Machlup路径积分表明，有效速度与加速度在最短涨落轨迹上获得物理意义；非零初始加速度是驱动行走者远离原点、同时确保无标度统计（scale-free statistics）涌现与稳态分布可归一化（normalizability）的根本机制。

Conclusion: 该最小化路径（minimal pathway）为跨学科复杂系统中广泛观测到的-2幂律提供了全新的微观基础，表明局域马尔可夫机制本身足以产生重尾统计，无需依赖非局域性或记忆效应。

Abstract: The emergence of heavy-tailed statistics in complex systems is conventionally attributed to non-local stochastic jumps or non-Markovian memory. Here, we present a one-dimensional random walk where power-law behaviors arise instead from a strictly local, discrete-time Markovian mechanism. The step length is governed by a deterministic function of the walker's position, establishing a positive feedback loop that induces strong effective correlations along the trajectories. Through analytical derivations in the continuum limit and extensive numerical simulations, we show that this rule yields a robust, non-Gaussian stationary state. The exact analytical solution is obtained in the closed form of a symmetric, Lorentz-like distribution, $ρ_{\text{st}}(x) \propto (|x|/l+rΔx)^{-2}$, confirming asymptotic power-law tails that decay as $|x|^{-2}$ over six decades. Furthermore, by employing the Onsager-Machlup path-integral formalism, we demonstrate that effective velocity and acceleration acquire physical meaning along the shortest fluctuation trajectories. Crucially, we find that a non-zero initial acceleration acts as the fundamental mechanism driving the walker away from the origin, ensuring both the emergence of scale-free statistics and the normalizability of the stationary distribution. This minimal pathway provides a new microscopic foundation for the widespread $-2$ power law observed across multidisciplinary complex systems.

</details>


### [72] [Chirality-sensitive mobility and dissipation of Brownian motion on a helical landscape](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23803)
*Debankur Bhattacharyya,Abraham Nitzan*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了在圆柱表面二维螺旋势场（helical landscape）中惯性粒子的布朗动力学（Brownian dynamics）与线性响应（linear response），揭示了各向异性阻尼（anisotropic damping）导致运动耦合、零模（zero mode）的出现，并通过投影到稳定子空间构建了线性响应理论，导出了动力学迁移率张量（dynamical mobility tensor）的解析表达式，发现了螺旋几何诱导的交叉响应与能量耗散不对称性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解螺旋几何约束下惯性粒子在噪声环境中的输运行为，特别是各向异性阻尼对随机动力学可分离性（separability）的破坏，以及如何构建相应的线性响应理论来描述轴向与角向之间的交叉输运效应。

Method: 采用谐波阱近似（harmonic well approximation）分析确定性运动；引入朗之万描述（Langevin description）处理随机动力学；将各向异性阻尼系统表述为相空间中的线性奥恩斯坦-乌伦贝克过程（Ornstein-Uhlenbeck process）；通过投影掉零模，在稳定子空间中构造平稳动力学（stationary dynamics）；利用线性响应理论推导时间关联函数与动力学迁移率张量的解析表达式。

Result: 各向同性阻尼下随机运动保持可分离性，而各向异性阻尼沿轴向和角向耦合随机动力学并破坏可分离性。在无限系统中，相空间动力学因零模的存在不趋于平稳分布。投影后得到稳定子空间的平稳动力学，导出了时域和频域中迁移率张量的闭式解析解。迁移率张量的非对角元描述了轴向力与角运动、力矩与轴向输运之间的交叉响应，且二者相等，体现了时间反演对称性（time reversal symmetry）和螺旋几何特征。同时施加轴向和角向驱动时，螺旋势场导致能量耗散率出现不对称性。

Conclusion: 螺旋几何结构在随机动力学中产生独特的交叉输运效应，其非对角迁移率相等是时间反演对称性的直接体现，且螺旋势场可导致能量耗散的不对称分布，这些结果对理解螺旋微结构中的输运现象具有理论意义。

Abstract: We study the Brownian dynamics and linear response of a particle with inertia moving in a 2-dimensional helical landscape imprinted on a cylindrical surface. In the harmonic well approximation, the deterministic motion separates into free propagation along the screw direction and harmonic motion in the transverse screw-normal direction. We show that for isotropic damping this simplification survives in the Langevin description, whereas anisotropic damping along the axial and angular directions couples the stochastic dynamics and destroys separability. The resulting anisotropic model is formulated as a linear Ornstein-Uhlenbeck process in phase space with a zero mode associated with diffusion along the screw coordinate, so that in an infinite system the full phase-space dynamics does not relax to a stationary distribution. To treat transport in this setting, we construct the stationary dynamics in the stable subspace obtained after projecting out the zero mode. This leads to a linear response theory for this system and yields closed analytical expressions for stationary time-correlation functions and the dynamical mobility tensor in both the time and frequency domains. The off-diagonal elements of the mobility tensor describe cross-response between axial forcing and angular motion, and between applied torque and axial transport. Consistent with time reversal symmetry, these cross mobilities are equal and provide a direct dynamical signature of the helical geometry. In addition, a simultaneous application of driving in both the axial and angular direction reveals asymmetry in energy dissipation rate due the helical landscape.

</details>


### [73] [Exact solution of generalized gauge-invariant Ising chains with multi-spin interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23228)
*Pavel Khrapov,Stepan Shchurenkov*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文对一类具有任意多自旋相互作用的广义规范不变 n-链伊辛模型（n=1,2,3,4），在有限长条格点上的精确解进行了系统性推导，给出了配分函数、规范不变关联函数和威尔逊圈的显式公式，并基于威尔逊圈的标度行为识别了禁闭相与非禁闭相的相图。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有经典工作已对规范不变伊辛模型（gauge-invariant Ising model）进行了研究，但缺乏对具有任意多自旋相互作用（multi-spin interactions）的广义模型的精确解分析，尤其是在有限条带格点上的系统理论处理。

Method: 采用转移矩阵方法（transfer-matrix method），在有限长度 L、宽度 n 的条带晶格上，通过两步变换——消除规范冗余（elimination of gauge redundancy）和将原始模型约化为有效 n-链伊辛模型——推导配分函数和关联函数。对转移矩阵进行谱分解（spectral decomposition），针对 n≤3 的情况给出特征值和特征向量的显式表达式。

Result: 获得了配分函数和任意宽度威尔逊圈（Wilson loop）的通用公式；识别出威尔逊圈的面积律（area-law，类似禁闭 confinement）和周长律（perimeter-law，类似退禁闭 deconfinement）两种标度行为；计算了特定哈密顿量下的弦张力（string tension）并构建了相图（phase diagrams）。

Conclusion: 该工作将经典规范不变伊辛模型的结果进行了推广和实质性扩展，为理解多自旋相互作用下的规范理论与统计力学（statistical mechanics）提供了精确可解的理论框架。

Abstract: In this work, exact solutions are obtained for a class of generalized gauge-invariant $n$-chain Ising models ($n=1,2,3,4$) with arbitrary multi-spin interactions that are invariant under the local $\mathbb{Z}_2$ gauge group. On a strip lattice of finite length $L$ and width $n$ with periodic or free boundary conditions, an explicit expression for the partition function is derived using the transfer-matrix method. Two successive transformations are developed: elimination of gauge redundancy and reduction of the original model to an effective $n$-chain Ising model with all possible interactions between neighboring vertical layers. On the basis of the spectral decomposition of the $2^n\times 2^n$ transfer matrix, general formulas are obtained for gauge-invariant correlation functions and Wilson loops of arbitrary width. For $n \le 3$, explicit expressions are derived in terms of eigenvalues and eigenvectors. A detailed analysis of the behavior of the Wilson loop is performed, which allows us to identify regimes exhibiting area-law (confinement-like) and perimeter-law (deconfinement-like) dependence. For specific Hamiltonians, the string tension is computed and the corresponding phase diagrams are constructed. The results generalize and substantially extend the classical works on the gauge-invariant Ising model.

</details>


### [74] [Inviscid scaling in the Kuramoto-Sivashinsky equation from functional renormalization group and direct numerical simulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23364)
*Liubov Gosteva,Dipankar Roy,Nicolás Wschebor,Léonie Canet*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文发现一维Kuramoto-Sivashinsky方程在中间尺度存在一个动力学指数z=1的标度区，介于大尺度的Kardar-Parisi-Zhang标度（z=3/2）与小尺度的非普适行为之间。该标度行为源于有效粘滞性从微观负值向宏观正值过渡时的消失，属于无粘Burgers普适类，并通过泛函重整化群和直接数值模拟进行了验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前对Kuramoto-Sivashinsky (KS)方程标度行为的理解主要集中于大尺度的Kardar-Parisi-Zhang (KPZ)普适类（z=3/2）与小尺度的非普适行为，中间尺度是否存在其他标度区尚未被充分认识。本文旨在揭示并表征这一被忽视的中间标度区。

Method: 采用泛函重整化群（functional renormalization group）分析KS方程的有效粘滞性随尺度的流动，同时结合直接数值模拟（direct numerical simulations）验证相关预言。

Result: 发现了介于大尺度KPZ标度（z=3/2）与小尺度非普适行为之间的中间标度区，其动力学指数z=1。该标度行为源于有效粘滞性从微观负KS值向宏观有效正KPZ值演化过程中的消失，并对应于无粘Burgers普适类（inviscid-Burgers universality class），即KPZ方程的零粘滞性不动点。

Conclusion: 一维KS方程在中间尺度存在一个普适的z=1标度区，该标度行为对系统的关联函数有深刻影响，其物理起源是有效粘滞性的零穿越。这一发现丰富了KS方程和KPZ方程标度行为的理解，并为连接微观非普适行为和宏观普适行为提供了中间桥梁。

Abstract: We show that the one-dimensional Kuramoto-Sivashinsky (KS) equation features a scaling regime characterized by the dynamical exponent $z=1$ at intermediate scales between the large-scale Kardar-Parisi-Zhang (KPZ) scaling with $z=3/2$ and the small-scale non-universal behavior. This scaling regime is intrinsic to the KS dynamics since it arises from the vanishing of the effective viscosity when evolving from its microscopic negative KS value, to its macroscopic effective positive KPZ value. This vanishing of the viscosity deeply imprints the behavior of correlations at intermediate scales, which exhibit a universal $z=1$ scaling. This behavior pertains to the inviscid-Burgers universality class, which corresponds to the zero-viscosity fixed point of the KPZ equation. We evidence and characterize this so-far-overlooked scaling regime using both functional renormalization group and direct numerical simulations.

</details>


### [75] [Order-Disorder Tricriticality in $\mathrm{A}_n \mathrm{B}_n$ Star Polymer Melts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23758)
*Minhoon Kim,Wonjun Kang,Daeseong Yong,Junhan Cho,Jaeup U. Kim*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文发现对称型 AₙBₙ 星形聚合物熔体中，臂数 n 本身可作为调节三临界点（tricritical point）的热力学参数，驱动有序-无序转变（order–disorder transition, ODT）从二级连续转变为一级不连续转变。通过随机相位近似（random phase approximation）展开至六阶自由能，并与自洽场理论（self-consistent field theory, SCFT）对比，解析得到三临界臂数 n_tc ≈ 5.4475。该行为源于臂间共接合点（common junction）产生的关联效应，且非整数三临界臂数可通过星形聚合物二元混合物有效实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 三临界现象通常需要额外调节一个热力学参数，本文旨在探索在对称 AₙBₙ 星形聚合物熔体中，臂数 n 是否能自然扮演这一角色，从而在无需外部参数调谐的情况下实现三临界行为。

Method: 采用随机相位近似（random phase approximation）构建六阶自由能展开，解析识别三临界臂数；同时结合自洽场理论（self-consistent field theory, SCFT）的数值计算进行验证和对比。

Result: 解析得到三临界臂数 n_tc ≈ 5.4475；当 n < n_tc 时，层状有序转变（lamellar ordering transition）为连续转变，发生在旋节线点（spinodal point）(χN)ₛ ≈ 10.495；当 n > n_tc 时，转变变为一级不连续，有序-无序转变点 (χN)_ODT 低于 (χN)ₛ，并具有近三临界点的二次依赖关系。SCFT 计算确认了转变类型和相边界移动。

Conclusion: 星形聚合物臂数可诱导三临界性，其微观机制是共接合点导致的臂间关联效应。非整数三临界臂数可通过二元混合物实现，为微相分离聚合物体系中由拓扑结构驱动的三临界现象提供了一个稀有的可解析处理的范例。

Abstract: Tricriticality usually requires tuning an additional thermodynamic parameter. Here we show that, in symmetric $\mathrm{A}_n\mathrm{B}_n$ star-polymer melts, the arm number $n$ itself plays this role and drives the order--disorder transition (ODT) from second order to first order. By developing a sixth-order free-energy expansion within the random phase approximation and comparing it with self-consistent field theory (SCFT) calculations, we analytically identify a tricritical arm number, $n_{\mathrm{tc}}\approx 5.4475$. For $n<n_{\mathrm{tc}}$, the lamellar ordering transition remains continuous and occurs at the spinodal point, $(χN)_{\mathrm{s}}\approx 10.495$. For $n>n_{\mathrm{tc}}$, the transition becomes first order, and $(χN)_{\mathrm{ODT}}$ shifts below $(χN)_{\mathrm{s}}$ with a quadratic dependence near the tricritical point. SCFT calculations confirm the predicted transition character and phase-boundary shift. The origin of this behavior is traced to inter-arm correlations generated by the common junction. We further show that the noninteger tricritical arm number can be effectively realized in binary mixtures of star polymers. This provides a rare analytically tractable example of architecture-induced tricriticality in a microphase-separating polymer system.

</details>


### [76] [Multi-field Return Point Memory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23781)
*Nathaniel Croce,Hossein Salahshoor,D. Zeb Rocklin*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过零温伊辛模型（zero-temperature Ising model）证明，多控制场下的部分有序化（partial ordering）概念可导致回点记忆（return-point memory）现象，使系统不仅能恢复到先前的磁化强度（magnetization），还能恢复到确切的微观态（microstate），从而对非平衡系统中的记忆、学习与训练提供新见解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非平衡系统（non-equilibrium systems）表现出对历史施加场的记忆，而多稳态系统（multistable systems）如自旋玻璃（spin glasses）、马氏体（martensites）和颗粒物质（granular matter）拥有指数级多的微观态，导致其丰富动力学难以控制。现有控制方法不足以实现对这些系统微观状态的精确操控。

Method: 将部分有序化（partial ordering）概念推广至受多个控制场（multiple control fields）的系统，并使用零温伊辛模型（zero-temperature Ising model）作为模型系统进行理论演示。

Result: 多控制场的引入使系统表现出回点记忆（return-point memory）：施加的场序列不仅可将滞后系统（hysteretic system）恢复到先前的磁化强度，还能恢复到先前的精确微观态。不同类别的操作展现出可交换（commutative）与不可交换（noncommutative）行为，且场的多重性赋予系统更精确和复杂的控制能力。

Conclusion: 该研究为物理系统如何记忆、学习和被训练提供了新的理论视角，表明通过多控制场可实现对外场驱动非平衡系统的精细微观控制。

Abstract: Non-equilibrium systems display memory, a dependence not merely on their present environment but on previously applied fields. Multistable systems such as spin glasses, martensites and granular matter have exponentially many microstates consistent with an applied field, making their rich dynamics difficult to control. Control and order can be achieved through the concept of partial ordering, which we here generalize to systems subject to multiple control fields. We demonstrate, within the model system of the zero-temperature Ising model, that this leads to return-point memory, in which an applied sequence of fields restores the hysteretic system not only to a previous magnetization, but to a previous exact microstate. The multiplicity of fields grants more precise and complex control of the system, with different classes of operations displaying commutative and noncommutative behavior. This grants new insight into how physical systems can remember, learn, and be trained.

### [77] [Orientable Surfactants on Thin Liquid Films: A Dynamic Density-Functional Theory Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23789)
*Toby Kay,Serafim Kalliadasis*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 基于密度泛函理论（density-functional theory, DFT）及其动态扩展（DDFT），推导了考虑表面活性剂（surfactant）极性的新型薄膜方程，揭示了一种依赖于表面活性剂极化和浓度的广义表面张力（generalised surface tension）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典薄膜模型将表面活性剂视为对称点状粒子，忽略了其两亲性（amphiphilic）极性头-尾结构（polar head-tail structure），可能导致对马拉戈尼效应（Marangoni effect）和薄膜动力学的严重误判。需要引入更精确的统计力学方法修正这一缺陷。

Method: 从经典流体的统计力学（statistical mechanics）出发，采用密度泛函理论（DFT）及其动态扩展（DDFT），结合长波近似（long-wave approximation），将表面活性剂处理为极性单轴粒子（polar uniaxial particles），推导控制薄膜高度、表面活性剂浓度和极化场（polarisation field）的方程。

Result: 推导出的薄膜方程保持了梯度动力学（gradient dynamics）形式，其中自由能包含通常的界面贡献以及来自极化场的额外贡献。发现了一种新型广义表面张力，它同时依赖于表面活性剂的极化和浓度，并且以热力学一致的方式出现。

Conclusion: 所提出的模型更真实地描述了表面活性剂形状对薄膜稳定性和动力学的影响，为研究含极性表面活性剂的薄液膜提供了热力学自洽的理论框架。

Abstract: Thin liquid films are ubiquitous across many natural and engineering systems, including films which are laden with surface active molecules, i.e. surfactants. The presence of surfactants may have a destabilising effect on the film owing to their influence on surface tension, the so-called Marangoni effect, which in turn can induce flows in the film. Classical thin-film models for surfactant-laden films lead to paradigmatic gradient dynamics equations governing the film height and surfactant concentration and have been widely studied. However, in all these works, which are based on fluid dynamics or nonequilibrium thermodynamics, the shape of surfactants is neglected, and they have been treated as symmetric point-like particles. In general, this is a drastic oversimplification, as surfactants are amphiphilic with a polar head-tail structure. To account for this effect we use elements from the statistical mechanics of classical fluids, namely density-functional theory (DFT), and its dynamic extension (DDFT). Starting from DDFT and under the long-wave approximation, we derive the pertinent thin-film equations with the surfactants treated as polar uniaxial particles. These are equations which govern the film height, as well as the surfactant concentration and polarisation field. They preserve the gradient dynamics form by appropriately defining the free energy, which contains the usual interfacial contributions, as well as further contributions from the polarisation field. In doing so, we uncover a novel form of a generalised surface tension that is dependent on the surfactant polarisation as well as concentration, and show that it arises in a thermodynamically consistent way.

</details>

### [78] [Scalable Dark Siren Cosmology with gwcosmo: GPU Acceleration, Validation and Systematics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23538)

Method: 作者提出了gwcosmo管线的升级版本，通过在图形处理器（graphics processing unit, GPU）上利用向量化（vectorisation）技术，将整个引力波目录并行处理于每次迭代中，从而大幅提升计算速度。

Result: 新实现相较于先前版本实现了1000倍的加速，能够在以小时计的挂钟时间（wall-clock time）尺度上完成约第五次观测运行（O5）级别数量的引力波事件分析。

Conclusion: 结果表明gwcosmo管线具有良好的可扩展性（scalability），能够有效应对不断扩大的引力波事件目录所带来的计算负载增长，为未来暗汽笛宇宙学（dark-siren cosmology）的进展提供了关键工具。

Abstract: As the number of confident gravitational-wave detections grows, population-level hierarchical analyses face increasing computational costs. Dark-siren cosmological inference integrates over the localisation volume of each gravitational-wave source. To remain feasible without discarding information from the quieter but more numerous sources in the catalogue, significant efficiency improvements are vital for analysis pipelines. In this work, we present an upgraded version of the cosmological inference pipeline gwcosmo, which leverages vectorisation on graphics processing units to process the entire gravitational-wave catalogue in parallel with each iteration. This new implementation achieves a speed-up of 1000 times over the previous version, facilitating analyses of O5-like numbers of GW events on wall-clock timescales of hours. Our results demonstrate the scalability of the gwcosmo pipeline, specifically its ability to handle the increasing computational load of expanding event catalogues, positioning it as a vital tool for future advances in dark-siren cosmology.

### [79] [A No-Go Theorem for the Mass-Radius Relation of Solitons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22901)
*Mohammad Hossein Namjoo*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该论文证明了一个关于孤子（soliton）质量-半径关系的不可能定理（no-go theorem）：在d维空间中的实标量场理论里，典型的非拓扑、非相对论性、球对称孤子的质量-半径指数Γ无法落在区间[0, d]内。该定理适用于任意自相互作用形式，并排除了超轻暗物质或流体状暗物质模型作为星系晕核自然解释的可能性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 暗物质晕（dark matter halos）的中心核区域观测到的质量-半径指数Γ≈1.7（d=3时）恰好位于被排除区间中部，这促使作者检验现有暗物质模型（如超轻或流体状暗物质）在自然性（naturalness）意义上是否仍可成立。

Method: 通过定义质量-半径指数Γ ≡ d ln M / d ln R，作者从一般性假设出发，基于梯度能（gradient energy）、自相互作用（self-interaction）和引力（gravitation）三种力的相对强度，排除了参数空间中三者可比肩的精细调节（fine-tuned）区域，从而证明Γ无法位于[0, d]区间内。该推导不依赖孤子密度剖面的具体形式或Γ作为R函数的显式行为。

Result: 该定理适用于实标量场理论中典型的非拓扑、非相对论性、球对称孤子，以及由自引力非相对论性正压流体（barotropic fluids）构成的致密天体（compact objects），且对任意非线性自相互作用（包括非幂律、非解析或含导数耦合）普遍成立。

Conclusion: 超轻暗物质（ultra-light dark matter）或流体状暗物质（fluid-like dark matter）模型作为暗物质晕核的自然解释（在其他天体物理效应可忽略时）被该不可能定理排除。

Abstract: We prove a no-go theorem for the mass-radius relation of localized and stable field configurations, known as solitons. Defining the mass-radius index by $Γ\equiv \frac{\rm{d}\ln M}{\rm{d}\ln R}$, for real scalar field theories in $d$ spatial dimensions, we show that typical non-topological, non-relativistic, and spherically symmetric solitons cannot have $Γ$ in the range $[0, d]$. The forces considered originate from gradient energy, self-interaction, and gravitation, with the typicality assumption excluding the fine-tuned region of the parameter space where all three forces have comparable strength. Importantly, the theorem works for an arbitrary self-interaction that, in the relativistic theory, is allowed to be non-power-law in the field, be non-analytic around the classical vacuum (where the field amplitude vanishes), or to include derivative couplings. Additionally, the theorem makes no assumptions about the explicit form of the soliton's density profile or the behavior of $Γ$ as a function of $R$. We also argue that the same exclusion applies to compact objects formed from self-gravitating, non-relativistic, barotropic fluids with arbitrary equations of state. As a consequence for cosmology, it is worth noting that observations favor a core in the centers of dark matter halos with $Γ\simeq 1.7$, which (for $d=3$) lies approximately in the middle of the excluded range. Therefore, proposals such as ultra-light or fluid-like dark matter models are essentially ruled out as natural explanations for halo cores, provided other astrophysical effects are negligible.

</details>


### [80] [Gravitational waves from cosmic strings with friction: analytical approximations and parameter space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22944)
*Sergei Mukovnikov,Lara Sousa*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 宇宙弦（cosmic strings）在摩擦主导时期（friction-dominated era）产生的环会激发随机引力波背景（stochastic gravitational wave background）的特高频次级峰（ultra-high-frequency secondary peak），但此前缺乏对该特征的快速且准确的解析描述。

Method: 推导了描述宇宙弦摩擦主导时期环贡献的解析近似（analytical approximations），并在相关频率范围和广泛的宇宙弦参数（cosmic string parameters）下验证了其准确性。

Result: 解析近似对摩擦主导时期环的贡献给出了良好的描述；利用这些近似，揭示了该特高频峰在随机引力波背景谱上可区分的完整参数范围，并发现其存在于比文献Mukovnikov:2024zed最初报道的更广泛的高能物理场景中。

Conclusion: 所推导的解析近似为快速且准确地表征宇宙弦特高频引力波次级峰提供了有效工具，并拓展了该可观测特征所适用的高能物理模型范围。

Abstract: We derive analytical approximations to describe the ultra-high-frequency secondary peak of the stochastic gravitational wave background generated by cosmic strings that is sourced by loops created in the friction-dominated era. We show that these approximations provide a very good description of the contribution of the friction-era loops over the relevant frequency range and for a broad range of cosmic string parameters, thus enabling a fast and accurate characterization of this signature. We also use these approximations to uncover the full parameter range in which this ultra-high-frequency peak should be distinguishable on the stochastic gravitational wave background spectrum and show that it should be present in a broader range of high-energy physics scenarios than originally reported in~\cite{Mukovnikov:2024zed}.

### [81] [Effects of compocasting process parameters on microstructural characteristics and tensile properties of A356-SiCp composites](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22881)
*Hamed Khosravi,Hamed Bakhshi,Erfan Salahinejad*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 研究了复合铸造工艺参数（搅拌温度、速度和时间）对A356-10% SiCp（体积分数）复合材料的结构和拉伸性能的影响，发现均匀分布对拉伸性能的贡献优于孔隙率水平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究半固态搅拌复合铸造（compocasting）工艺参数（温度、搅拌速度、时间）对A356铝基复合材料中SiC颗粒分布均匀性、孔隙率及拉伸性能的影响，以确定最优工艺条件。

Method: 在590、600、610°C三个温度下，以200、400、600 r/min的搅拌速度分别进行10、20、30分钟的半固态搅拌（semisolid stirring）；随后对样品进行结构评估（颗粒分布均匀性、孔隙率）和拉伸性能测试。

Result: 延长搅拌时间和降低搅拌温度可改善颗粒分布均匀性；搅拌速度增加时均匀性先升后降。所有工艺参数增加均导致孔隙率提高。最优工艺参数为：搅拌速度400 r/min、温度590°C、时间30分钟。颗粒分布均匀性对拉伸性能的贡献大于孔隙率水平。

Conclusion: 复合铸造工艺参数显著影响A356-10% SiCp复合材料的微观结构和拉伸性能，其中颗粒分布均匀性是决定拉伸性能的主导因素。

Abstract: The effects of compocasting process parameters on some structural and tensile characteristics of the A356-10% SiCp (volume fraction) composites were studied. Semisolid stirring was carried out at temperatures of 590, 600 and 610 C with stirring speeds of 200, 400 and 600 r/min for 10, 20 and 30 min. The distribution of the SiC particles within the matrix, porosity content and tensile properties of the obtained samples were examined. The structural evaluations show that by increasing the stirring time and decreasing the stirring temperature, the uniformity in the particle distribution is improved; however, by increasing the stirring speed the homogeneity firstly increases and then declines. It is also found that by increasing all of the processing parameters, the porosity content is enhanced. From the tensile characteristics viewpoint, the optimum values of the speed, temperature and time are found to be 400 r/min, 590 C and 30 min, respectively. The contribution of the reinforcement distribution uniformity prevails over that of the porosity level to the tensile properties.
