### [82] [Genome-Guided Interpretable Screening of Phase-Stable, Lead-Free Double Perovskite Absorbers for All-Inorganic Semiconductors, Sensors, and Photovoltaics with DFT-Validated Design Rules](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22887)
*Nafis Ahtasu,Sohanur Rahman Sohan,Md. Mostaq Ahmed Himel,Md. Zahid Hassan,Muhammad Harussani Moklis,Masud Rana Rashel,Hasan Jamil,AKM Kamrul Islam,Mouhaydine Tlemcani*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 提出了一种基因组引导、物理信息驱动的框架，通过四个可解释的描述符家族（堆积、键合、极化和电子身份）解码无铅卤化物双钙钛矿的热力学稳定性和光电行为。结合机器学习代理模型与逆向设计约束堆栈，从13,088种候选材料中筛选出五种位于凸包上、相稳定且具有强光吸收的无铅双钙钛矿半导体。基因型-表型耦合分析揭示了从结构到光电响应的层级调控机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 寻找稳定且无铅的卤化物钙钛矿用于光电应用面临巨大的组分空间和传统筛选方法可解释性有限的挑战。现有方法难以高效地从海量组合中识别出符合热力学稳定性和光电性能要求的候选材料，亟需一种兼具预测准确性与物理可解释性的设计范式。

Method: 构建了由四个物理可解释的描述符家族（堆积、键合、极化和电子身份）组成的框架。基于1,221个DFT计算的A2BB'X6化合物数据训练机器学习代理模型：一个面向稳定性的分类器（ROC-AUC=0.92）和一个用于带隙预测的XGBoost回归器（R²=0.93）。采用分阶段逆向设计约束堆栈对13,088种电荷平衡的无铅组分进行筛选，最终经DFT验证确认候选材料。

Result: 筛选出五种DFT验证的相稳定半导体：Rb2SnMnBr6、Cs2CdSnBr6、Cs2CdSnI6、Cs2KGaI6和Cs2AgAlBr6，它们均位于凸包上（E_hull ≤ 0 meV/atom），保持有序双钙钛矿结构，并表现出强光吸收（吸收峰约1e5 cm⁻¹）。基因型-表型耦合分析揭示了层级控制机制：堆积基因决定结构可成形性，键合基因控制近边光学跃迁和电导率，光电响应基因调控介电响应和激子屏蔽（ε₀ = 4.6–8.2）。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了一种可推广的可解释逆向设计范式，将描述符层面的基因组学与实验相关的光电表型相连接，为光伏、传感和透明电子应用中发现稳定的无铅双钙钛矿提供了设计规则。

Abstract: The discovery of stable, lead-free halide perovskites for optoelectronic applications is constrained by vast compositional space and limited interpretability of conventional screening approaches. We present a genome-guided, physics-informed framework that decodes thermodynamic stability and optoelectronic behavior through four physically interpretable descriptor families: packing, bonding, polarization, and electronic identity. Trained on 1,221 DFT-calculated A2BB'X6 compounds, machine-learning surrogates achieve robust predictive performance, with a recall-optimized stability classifier (ROC-AUC = 0.92) and an XGBoost regressor for band-gap prediction (R2 = 0.93 on held-out data). Applying a staged inverse-design constraint stack to 13,088 charge-balanced, lead-free compositions reduces the search space to five DFT-validated, phase-stable semiconductors: Rb2SnMnBr6, Cs2CdSnBr6, Cs2CdSnI6, Cs2KGaI6, and Cs2AgAlBr6. These candidates lie on the convex hull (E_hull <= 0 meV/atom), preserve ordered double-perovskite structures, and exhibit strong optical absorption (alpha peak ~1e5 cm^-1). Genotype-phenotype coupling analysis reveals a hierarchical control mechanism: packing genes define structural formability, bonding genes govern near-edge optical transitions and conductivity, and optoelectronic response genes regulate dielectric response and exciton screening (epsilon0 = 4.6-8.2). This work establishes a generalizable paradigm for interpretable inverse design, linking descriptor-level genomics to experimentally relevant optoelectronic phenotypes and providing design rules for discovering stable, lead-free double perovskites for photovoltaics, sensing, and transparent electronic applications.

</details>


### [83] [Thickness-Dependent Spintronic Terahertz Emission in MBE-Grown PtTe$_2$: From Semiconductor to Type-II Dirac Semimetal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22932)
*Rahul Sharma,Sylvain Massabeau,Armando Pezo,Ekta Yadav,Viliam Vretenár,Ravi K. Biroju,Fatima Ibrahim,Sukhdeep Dhillon,Alain Marty,Isabelle Gomes de Moraes,Adrien Michon,Jing Li,Mairbek Chshiev,Henri Jaffrès,Jean-Marie George,Matthieu Jamet*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文发现PtTe₂（第二类狄拉克半金属）作为自旋电子太赫兹发射器时，通过原子级厚度调控可以突破传统自旋霍尔电导率的限制。利用分子束外延生长1至20个单层的PtTe₂薄膜，实验显示太赫兹发射强度随厚度非单调变化：在单层半导体相中无信号，在约2层处发生半金属转变后急剧增强，10层时达到铂参考样品的6倍峰值，之后因太赫兹再吸收而下降。这一行为源于多通道自旋-电荷转换过程，包括拓扑表面态和厚度依赖的界面Rashba劈裂。第一性原理计算定量复现了实验趋势，证明该物理图像的正确性。厚度工程化范德华半金属为优化自旋电子太赫兹发射器和自旋轨道转矩磁存储器（SOT-MRAM）提供了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统自旋电子太赫兹发射器（spintronic THz emitter）的性能受限于非磁性转换层的自旋霍尔电导率（spin Hall conductivity），该物理量一旦材料选定即固定不变，缺乏调控自由度。本文旨在探索能否利用材料本身随厚度演变的电子相变来突破这一固有限制。

Method: 采用分子束外延（molecular beam epitaxy, MBE）生长PtTe₂薄膜，以单分子层（monolayer, ML）精度控制厚度从1到20 ML。通过测量不同厚度下的自旋电子太赫兹发射强度，并结合第一性原理（first-principles）计算分析界面自旋积累（interfacial spin accumulation），系统研究发射行为与电子相图的关系。

Result: 太赫兹发射强度随厚度非单调变化：单层半导体相中无信号，约2 ML处发生半金属转变后发射急剧增强，10 ML时达到峰值——为同等厚度铂参考样品的6倍；之后因太赫兹再吸收（THz reabsorption）而在更厚薄膜中下降。第一性原理计算定量复现了该实验趋势。

Conclusion: 该非单调行为不能用体反自旋霍尔（bulk inverse spin Hall）机制解释，而是反映了多通道自旋-电荷转换（multi-channel spin-to-charge conversion）过程：自旋动量锁定的拓扑表面态（spin-momentum-locked topological surface states）与厚度依赖的界面Rashba劈裂（interfacial Rashba splitting）在第二类狄拉克能带结构形成过程中共同增强。厚度工程化（thickness engineering）范德华半金属为优化自旋电子太赫兹发射器和自旋轨道转矩磁存储器（SOT-MRAM）提供了新的可行路径。

Abstract: Spintronic terahertz (THz) emitters have established themselves as among the most practical broadband THz sources available, yet their performance remains fundamentally limited by the spin Hall conductivity of the nonmagnetic conversion layer - a quantity that is fixed once the material is chosen. Here, we demonstrate that in PtTe$_2$, a type-II Dirac semimetal within the transition metal dichalcogenide family, this limitation can be circumvented by exploiting the dramatic thickness-driven electronic phase evolution of the material itself. Using molecular beam epitaxy to grow PtTe$_2$ films with single-monolayer precision from 1 to 20 ML, we show that the spintronic THz emission tracks the underlying electronic phase diagram directly: it is absent in the single-layer semiconducting phase, turns on sharply at the semimetal transition near 2 ML, and reaches a peak amplitude six times that of an equivalent Pt reference at 10 ML, before declining at larger thicknesses due to THz reabsorption in the increasingly metallic film. This non-monotonic behavior is inconsistent with a bulk inverse spin Hall mechanism and instead reflects a multi-channel spin-to-charge conversion process in which spin-momentum-locked topological surface states and a thickness-dependent interfacial Rashba splitting both contribute and strengthen as the type-II Dirac band structure develops. First-principles calculations of the interfacial spin accumulation reproduce the experimental trend quantitatively, confirming this physical picture. These findings introduce thickness engineering of van der Waals semimetals as a new and accessible route to optimizing spintronic THz emitters and spin-orbit torques in magnetic memories (SOT-MRAMs), with direct implications for the broader class of dimensionally tunable topological materials.

</details>


### [84] [A new method to probe conducting filaments in MoS$_2$-based memristors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22943)
*Pierre Trousset,Lucie Le Van-Jodin,Bruno Reig,Clotilde Ligaud,Thomas Jalabert,Hanako Okuno,Le Van-Hoan,Paul Brunet,Stéphane Cadot,Matthieu Jamet*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过开发一种新型机械剥离技术，选择性地去除基于二硫化钼（MoS₂）忆阻器（memristor）的顶部金属电极，结合开尔文探针力显微镜（KPFM）、拉曼光谱映射和透射电子显微镜（TEM）等多尺度表征手段，揭示了导电细丝（conducting filament）的形成机制——顶部电极金属原子迁移进入MoS₂层，并证明了电极材料（金 vs. 镍）的选择通过吸附能与扩散能的差异显著影响开关行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维过渡金属硫族化物（transition metal dichalcogenides, TMDs）在忆阻器（memristor）中具有应用潜力，但其电阻开关（resistive switching）背后的物理机制，特别是导电细丝（conducting filament）的形成与消散过程，仍不明确。

Method: 提出一种新型机械剥离技术，利用MoS₂与顶部金属电极之间较弱的范德华相互作用（van der Waals interaction），选择性去除顶部电极；进而使用开尔文探针力显微镜（Kelvin Probe Force Microscopy, KPFM）和拉曼光谱映射（Raman spectroscopy mapping）对初始态、开态（ON）和关态（OFF）下的MoS₂表面进行直接、多尺度表征，并结合截面透射电子显微镜（Transmission Electron Microscopy, TEM）分析不同导电状态。

Result: 实验结果表明，导电细丝的形成源于顶部电极中的金属原子迁移进入MoS₂层；此外，金（gold）与镍（nickel）两种金属电极的选择显著影响开关行为，其差异归因于二者的吸附能（adsorption energy）和扩散能（diffusion energy）不同。

Conclusion: 该工作阐明了导电细丝的形成机制，提出了一种可重复的原位工作状态表征（in-operando characterization）方法，推动了基于二维材料的忆阻器的理解与优化。

Abstract: Two-dimensional (2D) transition metal dichalcogenides (TMDs), such as molybdenum disulfide (MoS$_2$), are emerging as promising materials for next-generation electronic devices. They have proved to be serious candidates for integration with memristors in non-volatile memory and radio frequency (RF) applications. However, the physical mechanisms behind their resistive switching, particularly the formation and resorption of conducting filaments, remain unclear. In this study, we present a novel mechanical exfoliation technique that selectively removes the top metallic electrode from MoS$_2$-based memristors by exploiting the weak van der Waals interaction between MoS$_2$ and the top electrode. This method enables direct and multi-scale characterization of the MoS$_2$ surface in different states (initial, ON and OFF) using Kelvin Probe Force Microscopy (KPFM) and Raman spectroscopy mapping. To complete this study, cross-sectional Transmission Electron Microscopy (TEM) was also performed in different conductive states. Our results reveal that the conducting filament is formed by metallic atom migration from the top electrode into the MoS$_2$ layer. Additionally, we demonstrate that the choice of metallic electrodes (gold vs. nickel) significantly impacts the switching behavior due to differences in adsorption and diffusion energies. This work not only clarifies the filament formation mechanism and introduces a reproducible approach for in-operando characterization but also represents a real progress in the understanding and optimization of 2D material-based memristors.

</details>


### [85] [Pulsed thermal annealing enables switching of chiral antiferromagnetic order with a sub-millitesla field in Mn$_3$Sn](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23205)
*Xiaokang Li,Jing Zhang,Xiaodong Guo,Zengwei Zhu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过热脉冲结合低至 0.1 mT 的极小磁场，在 Weyl 反铁磁体 Mn₃Sn 中实现了手性反铁磁态（chiral AFM state）的可靠翻转，揭示了热软化（thermal softening）效应在降低能量势垒、实现低场翻转中的关键作用，并指出热效应应与自旋轨道矩（spin–orbit torque）协同考虑。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 反铁磁（antiferromagnetic, AFM）序的操控是现代自旋电子学（spintronics）的核心课题。现有方法通常需要较大磁场或复杂结构，探索在极小外场下实现可靠翻转的机制具有重要理论与应用价值。

Method: 在高品质 Mn₃Sn 单晶中系统测量反常霍尔效应（anomalous Hall effect, AHE），利用脉冲热退火（pulsed thermal annealing）将样品加热至 Néel 温度（Néel temperature）T_N 以上，随后在极小的外磁场（低至 0.1 mT）下冷却，实现磁八极序（magnetic octupole order）的完全且可重复翻转。同时建立了一个简单模型，用以估算纳米尺度器件中电流脉冲引起的温升。

Result: 翻转所需磁场随温度趋近 T_N 而降低，并在 T_N 处消失。热软化——即加热至 T_N 以上以暂时移除磁各向异性（magnetic anisotropy）——将能量势垒降至接近零，使得极弱的方向性场（如薄膜器件中自旋轨道矩产生的有效场）即可在冷却过程中设定最终的磁态。

Conclusion: 热效应并非自旋轨道矩的附属问题，而是与之协同的重要因素。未来器件设计应同时考虑热效应与自旋矩的贡献。

Abstract: The manipulation of antiferromagnetic (AFM) order is a central theme in modern spintronics. In this work, we achieve reliable switching of the chiral AFM state in the Weyl antiferromagnet Mn$_3$Sn using a heat pulse combined with a very small magnetic field as small as 0.1 mT. By systematically measuring the anomalous Hall effect (AHE) in high-quality single crystals, we show that the field needed for switching decreases as the temperature approaches the Néel temperature $T_N$, and vanishes at $T_N$. Pulsed thermal annealing above $T_N$ followed by cooling in a tiny external field enables full and reproducible switching of the magnetic octupole order. Our results show that thermal softening (heating above $T_N$ to temporarily remove the magnetic anisotropy) is a key step that lowers the energy barrier to nearly zero. This allows an extremely weak directional field (like the effective field from spin-orbit torque in thin-film devices) to set the final magnetic state during cooling. We also provide a simple model to estimate the temperature rise in nanoscale devices under current pulses, giving practical guidance for device design. This work highlights that thermal effects are not a side issue but an important partner to spin torques, and suggests that future work should take both into account.

### [86] [Non-adiabatic phonon renormalization in metallic versus insulating rutile oxides](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23227)
*Reshma Kumawat,Shubham Farswan,Simranjeet Kaur,Kaushik Sen*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 通过对金属性金红石氧化物（RuO₂、IrO₂）和绝缘性金红石氧化物（TiO₂、SnO₂）的变温拉曼散射对比研究，发现金属性化合物中声子频率硬化（Δω≈6–10 cm⁻¹）显著强于绝缘体（Δω≈1–3 cm⁻¹），而线宽变化无系统性区分。传统Klemens非简谐衰减模型无法一致描述金属性体系的参数，引入电子贡献的T²修正项后，该框架能定量解释金属体系中增强的重整化，证实了非绝热电子-声子耦合的存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究金属性与绝缘性金红石氧化物中声子重整化（phonon renormalization）的差异，旨在揭示电子贡献对声子自能（phonon self-energy）的影响，并验证非绝热电子-声子耦合（non-adiabatic electron-phonon coupling）在金属性体系中的作用。

Method: 采用变温拉曼散射（temperature-dependent Raman scattering）对比研究金属性（RuO₂、IrO₂）与绝缘性（TiO₂、SnO₂）金红石氧化物；使用传统Klemens非简谐衰减模型（Klemens anharmonic decay model）拟合温度依赖数据，并引入含电子贡献的频率T²修正项构建修正框架。

Result: 金属性化合物声子频率硬化（Δω≈6–10 cm⁻¹）显著大于绝缘体（Δω≈1–3 cm⁻¹）；线宽变化（ΔΓ≈1–7 cm⁻¹）未呈现金属-绝缘系统性分类；传统Klemens模型拟合金属性体系时产生不一致的非简谐参数，而加入电子贡献T²修正项后能定量解释实验观察。

Conclusion: 金属性金红石中存在有限非绝热电子-声子耦合，且即使在声子线形（phonon line shape）未观测到Fano不对称性（Fano asymmetry）的情况下，仍可通过声子重整化识别该耦合效应。

Abstract: We present a comparative Raman scattering study of metallic rutile oxides (RuO$_2$ and IrO$_2$) and insulating rutiles (TiO$_2$ and SnO$_2$). Temperature-dependent Raman spectra reveal that the metallic compounds exhibit pronounced phonon frequency hardening, $ω(11~\mathrm{K})-ω(300~\mathrm{K})=Δω\approx 6$-$10~\mathrm{cm}^{-1}$, whereas the insulating rutiles show only modest hardening, $Δω\approx 1$-$3~\mathrm{cm}^{-1}$. In contrast, the linewidth changes, $ΔΓ\approx 1$--$7~\mathrm{cm}^{-1}$, do not display a systematic metallic-insulating classification. Fits with the conventional Klemens anharmonic decay model reproduce the overall temperature trends but yield inconsistent anharmonic parameters for the metallic compounds when benchmarked against insulating rutile analogues. A modified Klemens framework, incorporating an additional $T^{2}$ correction to the phonon frequency arising from the electronic contribution to the phonon self-energy, quantitatively accounts for the enhanced renormalization observed in metallic systems. These results establish finite non-adiabatic electron-phonon coupling in metallic rutiles and demonstrate that phonon renormalization can be identified even in the absence of observable Fano asymmetry in the phonon line shapes.

### [87] [In situ estimation of local acoustic pressure amplitude by force balancing with a ferrofluid droplet probe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23279)

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 声镊（acoustic tweezers）虽能实现微尺度物体的非接触操控，但在受限器件中对峰值局部声压幅值进行定量原位评估十分困难，传统基于水听器（hydrophone）的测量方法在微尺度受限于探头尺寸和安装条件。

Method: 采用力平衡法：将捕获的铁磁流体液滴作为驻波声场（standing-wave acoustic field）中的局部探针，通过调节外加磁场梯度，使磁力（magnetic force）与液滴上的最大初级声辐射力（primary acoustic radiation force）达到平衡，进而依据平衡点的磁力估算峰值局部声压幅值。

Result: 在 7.2 MHz 工作频率、10 Vpp 驱动电压下，估算得到的峰值局部声压幅值为 $2.6\times10^{5}$ Pa。

Conclusion: 该方法为微尺度声场的定量原位表征（quantitative in situ characterization）以及紧凑型声流控器件（acoustofluidic devices）工作条件的设定提供了一条实用路径。

Abstract: Acoustic tweezers enable non-contact manipulation of microscale objects, but quantitative in situ evaluation of the peak local pressure amplitude remains difficult in confined devices. Conventional hydrophone-based measurements are often limited at the microscale by probe size and installation constraints. Here, we present a force-balance method in which a trapped ferrofluid droplet serves as a local probe in a standing-wave acoustic field and an externally applied magnetic-field gradient is tuned so that the magnetic force balances the maximum primary acoustic radiation force on the droplet. From the magnetic force on the ferrofluid droplet, determined at the balance point, we estimate a peak local pressure amplitude of $2.6\times10^{5}$~Pa for 7.2~MHz operation at 10~V$_{\mathrm{pp}}$. This approach provides a practical route for quantitative in situ characterization of microscale acoustic fields and for setting operating conditions in compact acoustofluidic devices.

In exploring concomitant optimized growth temperature and Ag/Cr composition ratio of supply, we find the critical growth temperature ($T\mathrm{_{sub}}$) for obtaining single 60$^{\circ}$ domain in c-axis oriented AgCrSe$_{2}$ thin film on a lattice-matched (111) plane of the yttria-stabilized zirconia substrate. At temperatures below and above the critical $T\mathrm{_{sub}}$, metastable 0$^{\circ}$ domain in addition to the 60$^{\circ}$ domain emerges, indicating delicate energy balance of thermodynamic stability for obtaining the single-domain structure. In the present work, a crystal plasticity finite element (CPFE) framework is used to study the creep-fatigue response of a single-crystal nickel superalloy under a range of practically relevant thermo-mechanical loading conditions. In particular, the effects of strain amplitude, R-ratio, hold duration, and temperature on cyclic deformation, stress relaxation, damage evolution, and creep-fatigue life are examined. Particular attention is given to separate the roles of fatigue and creep damage, understanding their interaction, and identify the creep-dominated and fatigue-dominated regimes as a function of strain amplitude and hold time. ### [90] [Cathodoluminescence Analysis of Defects and Grain Boundaries in Zn3P2 Thin Films Grown on Graphene by MOVPE and MBE](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23357)

Result: CL观测表明，晶界（grain boundaries）作为非辐射复合中心（non-radiative sinks），其影响可延伸至晶粒内部数微米；与MBE相比，MOVPE生长的材料中与应变相关的亚带隙发射（sub-bandgap emission）受到抑制；MOVPE生长的Zn3P2晶粒更大，材料质量更优。

Here, we demonstrate the quasi-van der Waals epitaxy of Zn3P2 on graphene by metal-organic vapour phase epitaxy (MOVPE) and directly link the density of antiphase boundaries to optical emission modulation using correlative electron microscopy and cathodoluminescence (CL). Moreover, it is observed through CL that grain boundaries act as non-radiative sinks for excited charge carriers. The effect extends several micrometres into the grains, making grain boundaries detrimental to the applicability of Zn3P2 in read devices. Further comparison with molecular beam epitaxy grown films reveals the suppression of strain-related sub-bandgap emission in MOVPE-grown material. Overall, quasi-van der Waals epitaxy of Zn3P2 by MOVPE resulted in larger grains and improved material quality. In addition, these results directly link extended defects to recombination pathways in Zn3P2 and highlight grain-size control as a key strategy for improving earth-abundant photovoltaic absorbers.

### [91] [A Metadynamics-Based Framework for Free Energy Surface Mapping of Multiparticle Diffusion in Crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23360)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于元动力学(metadynamics, MetaD)提出两种方法：副本状态交换元动力学(replica state exchange MetaD)和平行偏置元动力学(parallel bias MetaD)，两者均将高维集体变量(CV)分解为多个低维变量。

Result: 以LixTiS2中锂(Li)的二维扩散为基准，获得的自由能面(FES)估算出的Li跳跃频率展现出与动力学蒙特卡洛(kinetic Monte Carlo)模拟及核磁共振(nuclear magnetic resonance, NMR)测量一致的浓度与温度依赖性趋势。

Conclusion: 所提出的方法为捕捉传统分子动力学(molecular dynamics, MD)模拟通常难以触及的扩散载流子慢动力学行为提供了一个有前景的框架。

Abstract: We propose two metadynamics (MetaD)-based methodologies for efficiently mapping free energy surfaces (FESs) of multiple interacting carriers diffusing in crystalline solids. Our approaches circumvent the challenges of high-dimensional collective variables (CVs) by employing replica state exchange MetaD and parallel bias MetaD, both of which decompose the high-dimensional CVs into multiple lower-dimensional ones. As a benchmark, we investigate two-dimensional lithium (Li) diffusion in LixTiS2 across a wide range of Li concentrations. The Li jump frequencies estimated from the obtained FESs exhibit concentration- and temperature-dependent trends consistent with previous kinetic Monte Carlo simulations and nuclear magnetic resonance measurements. Our approaches provide a promising framework for capturing the slow dynamics of diffusive carriers that are typically inaccessible to conventional molecular dynamics simulations.

### [92] [Symmetry-protected nodal planes and accidental nodal surfaces in mixed odd-even wave spin-momentum locking of relativistic altermagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23438)
*Xujia Gong,Amar Fakhredine,Sahar Izadi Vishkayi,Carmine Autieri*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文研究了相对论性交变磁体（altermagnet）中自旋-动量锁定（spin–momentum locking）的波对称性演化，发现主导自旋分量在 Néel 矢量沿 z 轴时保持 g 波（g-wave）对称性，而次主导分量可呈现 d 波（d-wave）或 p 波（p-wave）对称性；在铁电交变磁体中还可出现 p 波磁性及对称性保护的节面（nodal plane）与意外节面（accidental nodal surface）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非相对论性交变磁体存在偶数个节面（nodal planes），但在相对论极限下，由于 Néel 矢量与自旋-轨道耦合（spin–orbit coupling）导致的对称性降低，节面数量可能减少，因此需要系统分析相对论性交变磁体中节面的演化行为。

Method: 以中心对称的 CrSb 和非中心对称的纤锌矿（wurtzite）MnTe 为研究对象，分析其在相对论框架下的自旋-动量锁定特征，并考察 Néel 矢量取向与电场（反演对称性破缺）对波对称性的影响。

Result: 在两种体系中，主导自旋分量仅在 Néel 矢量沿 z 轴时于相对论情形下保持 g 波特征，次主导分量在 CrSb 中表现为 d 波对称性，在铁电纤锌矿 MnTe 中表现为 p 波对称性。铁电交变磁体的相对论性自旋-动量锁定可产生一个对称性保护的节面与一个不受保护的意外节面，或两个意外节面；当 Néel 矢量沿 x 轴时，MnTe 的部分能带呈现 p 波磁性。

Conclusion: 交变磁体可在相对论极限下容纳不同自旋分量实现混合的角动量波对称性（angular-momentum wave symmetries），从而拓展了对交变磁体中自旋-动量锁定与节面行为的理解。

Abstract: Non-relativistic spin--momentum locking in altermagnets exhibits an even number of nodal planes. In the relativistic limit, the number of nodal planes can be lowered by symmetry reduction due to the Néel vector and spin--orbit coupling in noncentrosymmetric systems. Therefore, an analysis of the evolution of the nodal planes in relativistic altermagnets is required. While $g$-wave spin--momentum locking is straightforward to realize in non-relativistic altermagnets, this $g$-wave does not necessarily survive in the relativistic case. In this work, we investigate the relativistic spin--momentum locking of the centrosymmetric CrSb and the noncentrosymmetric wurtzite MnTe. As a first result, we show that in both systems the dominant spin component retains its $g$-wave character in the relativistic regime only when the Néel vector is oriented along the $z$-axis, while the subdominant components exhibit $d$-wave symmetry in CrSb and $p$-wave symmetry in ferroelectric wurtzite MnTe. More generally, the $g$-wave character is preserved in the relativistic limit only when both the Néel vector and the electric field associated with inversion-symmetry breaking are oriented along the $z$-axis. As a second result, we show that relativistic spin--momentum locking of ferroelectric altermagnets can exhibit $p$-wave magnetism with one symmetry-protected nodal plane and an accidental nodal surface not protected by symmetry, or can have two accidental nodal surfaces. With the Néel vector aligned along the $x$-axis, selected bands of ferroelectric altermagnet wurtzite MnTe exhibit $p$-wave magnetism. Our results establish that altermagnets can host distinct spin components that realize a mixture of angular-momentum wave symmetries in momentum space in the relativistic limit.

### [93] [Self-organized formation of step-terrace structure in SrRuO3 thin films grown on mixed-terminated SrTiO3 (100) substrates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23450)
*Ryotaro Arakawa,Sachio Komori,Kotaro Tomita,Shunsei Komori,Masaaki A. Tanaka,Tomoyasu Taniyama*

TL;DR: 本文报道了在未处理表面的混合终端SrTiO₃(100)衬底上，通过脉冲激光沉积自组织形成SrRuO₃薄膜台阶-平台（step-terrace）结构的过程。薄膜从三维岛状生长模式转变为台阶流（step-flow）生长模式，形成与SRO单胞参数一致的台阶形态；通过改变衬底温度和靶-衬底距离可系统调控平均平台宽度。该自组织结构可显著改善后续BiFeO₃薄膜的表面平整度和结晶质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 氧化物薄膜的外延生长中，衬底及底层薄膜的表面形貌起着关键作用。本文旨在探索在不经过任何预处理、具有混合终端（mixed-terminated）的SrTiO₃(100)衬底上，通过自组织方式形成SrRuO₃薄膜的台阶-平台结构，并阐明其生长模式转变机制与调控方法。

Method: 采用脉冲激光沉积（pulsed laser deposition, PLD）技术在未处理的混合终端SrTiO₃(100)衬底上生长SrRuO₃薄膜；利用原子力显微镜（atomic force microscopy, AFM）观测薄膜表面形貌演变；通过改变衬底温度和靶-衬底距离调节台阶平台宽度；并在自组织SRO薄膜上沉积BiFeO₃以验证其应用效果。

Result: SRO薄膜初始以三维岛状模式生长，随厚度增加通过岛合并（island coalescence）转变为台阶流生长模式，最终形成具有明确台阶-平台结构且台阶高度与SRO单胞参数一致的形貌。平均平台宽度可通过衬底温度和靶-衬底距离系统性调控，这归因于临界岛半径（critical island radius）的变化。在具有该自组织结构的SRO薄膜上生长的BiFeO₃薄膜，其表面平整度和结晶质量均优于直接在裸SrTiO₃衬底上生长的样品。

Conclusion: 本工作揭示了钙钛矿氧化物薄膜在不同生长条件下厚度驱动的生长模式转变机制，提供了一种无需衬底预处理即可自组织获得高质量台阶-平台形貌的途径，并为后续功能氧化物薄膜的异质外延生长提供了改进的底层模板。

Abstract: Surface morphology of the substrate and bottom layers plays a critical role in the epitaxial growth of oxide thin films. Here, we report on the self-organized formation of a step-terrace structure in SrRuO3 (SRO) thin films grown using pulsed laser deposition on mixed-terminated SrTiO3 (100) substrates without any prior surface treatment. Atomic force microscopy observations reveal that SRO films initially grow in a three-dimensional island mode and subsequently undergo a transition to a step-flow growth mode through island coalescence as the film thickness increases, resulting in a well-defined step-terrace morphology with a step height consistent with the SRO unit-cell parameter. The average terrace width of the self-organized structure can be systematically tuned by varying the substrate temperature and the target-substrate distance, which we attribute to changes in the critical island radius that governs the nucleation behavior. To demonstrate the utility of this self-organized morphology, we show that BiFeO3 thin films grown on SRO films with such a step-terrace structure exhibit improved surface flatness and crystalline quality compared to those grown directly on bare SrTiO3 substrates. These findings provide a clear understanding of the mechanism of thickness-driven growth-mode transitions in perovskite oxide thin films under various growth conditions.

### [94] [Intrinsic Point Defects and Frenkel Pair Formation in Photovoltaic Absorber Zn$_3$P$_2$: Regulating $p$-type Conductivity through Growth and Annealing Conditions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23479)
*Nico Kawashima,Silvana Botti*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究利用基于密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）的第一性原理（ab initio）计算，结合广泛的势能面搜索，揭示了Zn₃P₂中本征点缺陷的基态能量学和热力学特性，指出锌空位（V_Zn）主导p型导电性，而磷间隙（P_i）浓度极低；n型掺杂受热力学限制，建议通过富磷生长和高温退火优化空穴浓度，并转向界面工程策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解Zn₃P₂中本征点缺陷的基态能量学与热力学行为，以解释其本征p型导电性的来源，并评估实现n型掺杂的可能性，从而为光伏应用提供材料优化方向的指导。

Method: 采用基于密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）的第一性原理（ab initio）计算，并结合广泛的势能面（potential energy landscape）搜索，对Zn₃P₂中的本征点缺陷进行系统分析。

Result: 缺陷化学由锌空位（V_Zn）和锌间隙（Zn_i）主导，其平衡浓度显著高于其他本征缺陷；磷间隙（P_i）形成能高，浓度可忽略；V_Zn作为浅受主（shallow acceptor）拉低费米能级（Fermi level），导致p型导电；V_Zn与Zn_i之间存在正结合能，形成电中性的弗仑克尔对（Frenkel pair），部分补偿本征p型导电性。

Conclusion: 实现n型导电受到热力学限制；可通过富磷生长条件和高温退火优化空穴浓度；未来光伏策略应优先考虑界面工程（interface engineering），而非体相n型掺杂（bulk n-type doping）。

Abstract: This study investigates the ground-state energetics and thermodynamics of intrinsic point defects in zinc phosphide Zn$_3$P$_2$ using \emph{ab initio} density functional theory combined with an extensive potential energy landscape search. Our analysis reveals that the defect chemistry is dominated by zinc vacancies $V_\mathrm{Zn}$ and zinc interstitials Zn$_i$, with equilibrium concentrations significantly surpassing those of other intrinsic species. Notably, we find that phosphorus interstitials P$_i$, previously suggested to be significant, possess high formation energies and likely exist only in negligible quantities. The characteristic $p$-type conductivity of undoped Zn$_3$P$_2$ is shown to be a direct consequence of zinc vacancies, which act as shallow acceptors and pull the Fermi level toward the valence band. Furthermore, we identify a positive binding energy between $V_\mathrm{Zn}$ and Zn$_i$, leading to the formation of electrically benign Frenkel pairs that partially compensate the intrinsic p-type conductivity. Our results suggest that achieving $n$-type conductivity is fundamentally limited by these thermodynamic constraints. We conclude that hole densities can be optimized through phosphorus-rich growth conditions and high-temperature annealing, and suggest that future photovoltaic strategies should prioritize interface engineering over bulk $n$-type doping.

Abstract: High-energy optical transitions in monolayer transition-metal dichalcogenides exhibit characteristics that are markedly distinct from those of lower-lying band-edge excitons. In this work, we investigate the ultrafast dynamics of these high-energy excitations by employing broadband ultrafast transient absorption spectroscopy spanning the visible to ultraviolet spectral range. We observe that the formation and relaxation dynamics of one of the high energy transitions display a distinct behavior compared to the lower-energy excitonic resonances, developing on a significantly slower timescale. First-principles calculations of the excitonic landscape allow us to account for this delayed response and attribute it to the phonon-mediated formation of momentum-dark excitons.

### [96] [Ambiguity in B-Site cation ordering: A Case study of the double perovskite Ca$_2$CoNbO$_6$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23558)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: The ordering of cations in the B sublattice remains a challenging issue in double perovskites. In this work, a combined experimental and theoretical approach was employed to investigate the Co/Nb distribution in Ca$_2$CoNbO$_6$ and its influence on magnetic and transport properties. The density functional theory, supported by magnetic susceptibility measurements, indicates that Co adopts a high-spin Co$^{3+}$ state. No long-range magnetic ordering was observed down to low temperatures; however, the presence of short-range correlations points to the partial disorder in the Co/Nb sublattice. This interpretation is further supported by electron paramagnetic resonance, which also reveals slight oxygen nonstoichiometry. Electrical transport follows a small-polaron hopping mechanism with an activation energy of 0.25 eV. The Seebeck coefficient reaches 0.4 mV/K at 600 K.

### [97] [First-principles transition-state tensorial cluster expansion of vacancy diffusion in Ta-W beyond the kinetically-resolved activation approximation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23612)
*Jacob Jeffries,Brianna Sebastian-Olazabal,Enrique Martinez*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出一个基于第一性原理（first-principles）的框架，通过张量团簇展开（tensorial cluster expansion）直接学习依赖于局域原子环境的迁移势垒（migration barriers），并将其嵌入到晶格动力学蒙特卡洛（kinetic Monte Carlo）模拟中。该方法无需简化动力学近似（如KRA模型），能够预测化学复杂合金（如Ta-W体系）中因溶质捕获与渗流低势垒输运路径竞争所导致的非平凡扩散行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 化学复杂合金（chemically complex alloys）中的扩散预测面临重大挑战，因为迁移势垒（migration barriers）对局域原子环境（local atomic environments）具有强烈的依赖性。现有的简化动力学近似（如kinetically resolved activation, KRA模型）无法准确捕捉这种环境依赖性，因此需要发展一种不依赖此类近似、直接基于第一性原理（first-principles）的计算框架。

Method: 开发了一个基于第一性原理的框架：首先通过密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）和微动弹性带（nudged elastic band, NEB）方法计算迁移势垒；然后利用张量团簇展开（tensorial cluster expansion）方法表示包含过渡态（transition states）的势垒能量；最后将这些信息部署到晶格动力学蒙特卡洛（on-lattice kinetic Monte Carlo, kMC）模拟中。

Result: 将该框架应用于Ta-W体系，成功捕捉了由溶质捕获（solute trapping）与渗流低势垒输运路径（percolated low-barrier transport pathways）之间的竞争（crossover）所导致的非平凡成分依赖扩散行为，并在中间成分附近观测到表观活化能（apparent activation energy）出现最大值。

Conclusion: 该方法为将第一性原理过渡态能量学（transition-state energetics）整合到介观动力学模拟（mesoscale kinetic simulations）中提供了一条通用且可扩展的路径，能够实现对化学复杂材料中扩散行为的多尺度预测建模（predictive multiscale modeling），并为揭示新兴输运现象（emergent transport phenomena）提供了途径。

Abstract: Predicting diffusion in chemically complex alloys remains challenging due to the strong dependence of migration barriers on local atomic environments. Here, we develop a first-principles-informed framework that directly learns environment-dependent migration barriers without relying on reduced kinetic approximations such as the kinetically resolved activation (KRA) model. Migration barriers computed using density functional theory and nudged elastic band calculations are represented via a tensorial cluster expansion including transition states and deployed in on-lattice kinetic Monte Carlo simulations. Applied to the Ta-W system, the framework captures nontrivial composition-dependent diffusion behavior arising from a crossover between solute trapping and percolated low-barrier transport pathways, yielding a maximum in the apparent activation energy near intermediate compositions. This approach establishes a general and scalable route for integrating first-principles transition-state energetics into mesoscale kinetic simulations, enabling predictive multiscale modeling of diffusion in chemically complex materials and providing a pathway for uncovering emergent transport phenomena.

</details>


### [98] [Close correlation between giant magnetostriction and the microstructure in Fe-Ga melt-spun ribbons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23624)
*Likun Chen,Mitsutaka Sato,Jiahao Han,Rie Y. Umetsu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究通过稀土（RE）掺杂和冷却速率调控，在熔体快淬法制备的Fe-Ga（Galfenol）薄带中实现了可控的<100>织构和磁弹性各向异性，最终在1 at.% Ce掺杂、转速1000 rpm条件下获得了高达688 ppm的磁致伸缩值，为设计高磁致伸缩合金提供了加工-织构-性能的指导方针。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 单晶Fe-Ga（Galfenol）制备工艺复杂、技术难度大，而多晶Fe-Ga磁致伸缩性能较低，亟需探索一种兼具高磁致伸缩和可加工性的替代方案。

Method: 采用熔体快淬（melt-spun）法制备了Fe₈₁Ga₁₉二元薄带以及不同稀土（RE）掺杂（0.2 at.% Pr、1 at.% Pr和1 at.% Ce）的薄带，并在不同冷却速率下进行制备；通过微观结构分析和磁致伸缩性能测试评估织构与各向异性行为。

Result: 稀土元素优先固溶于基体，较高冷却速率抑制了第二相形成；稀土掺杂通过增强磁晶畸变能（magnetocrystalline distortion energy）提高了磁致伸缩，冷却速率则有效调控<100>织构的优劣程度。1 at.%稀土掺杂导致熔点降低，使最佳织构对应的冷却速率低于二元合金及0.2 at.%掺杂样品。在1000 rpm转速下制备的1 at.% Ce掺杂薄带获得了高达688 ppm的磁致伸缩值。

Conclusion: 稀土掺杂熔体快淬薄带是获得巨磁致伸缩（giant magnetostriction）的 promising 候选材料，本研究建立了一套实用的加工-织构-性能（processing-texture-property）指导准则，可用于设计高磁致伸缩合金。

Abstract: Magnetoelastic anisotropy and <100> texture are crucial for promoting magnetostriction in Galfenol (Fe-Ga). Given that single-crystal Fe-Ga remains technically demanding and low magnetostriction of polycrystal, we explore melt-spun as an alternative, where rare-earth (RE) doping and cooling rates optimizing enable controllable <100> textured with required magnetoelastic anisotropy. Fe81Ga19 binary ribbons and RE-doped ribbons (0.2 at.% Pr, 1 at.% Pr and 1 at.% Ce) were fabricated at various cooling rates. Microstructural analyses reveal that RE elements preferentially dissolve into the matrix, while second-phase formation is suppressed at higher cooling rates. RE substitution increases the magnetostriction by enhancing magnetocrystalline distortion energy, while cooling rates act as an effective tuning knob to maximize the <100> texture. Notably, the decreased melting temperature associated with 1 at.% RE doping shifts the optimum texture to lower cooling rate compared with the binary alloy and 0.2 at.% RE doping sample. The magnetostriction as high as 688 ppm is achieved for the 1 at.% Ce doped ribbon fabricated at the speed of 1000 rotation per minute. These results demonstrate that RE-doped melt-spun ribbons are promising candidates for giant magnetostriction and establish a practical processing-texture-property guideline for designing highly magnetostrictive alloys.

</details>


### [99] [Evidence of a Hybridized Topological State in Weyl Semimetal/Topological Insulator Mn$_{3+x}$Sn$_{1-x}$/Bi$_{0.85}$Sb$_{0.15}$ Heterostructures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23765)
*Ryan T. Van Haren,Gillian P Boyce,Gregory M. Stephen,Vinay Sharma,Don Heiman,Aubrey T. Hanbicki,Adam L. Friedman*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过磁输运实验证据，报道了在铁磁性Mn₃₊ₓSn₁₋ₓ/Bi₀.₈₅Sb₀.₁₅异质结界面形成了一种杂化的外尔半金属（Weyl semimetal, WSM）费米弧/拓扑绝缘体（topological insulator, TI）表面态。研究发现，当Bi₀.₈₅Sb₀.₁₅覆盖层生长在铁磁相Mn₃₊ₓSn₁₋ₓ上时，外尔节点拓扑输运信号被恢复，这归因于WSM/TI界面杂化拓扑态的形成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索铁磁性外尔半金属与拓扑绝缘体界面处可能形成的杂化拓扑态，并验证其对外尔节点拓扑输运信号的恢复作用，以理解异质结界面拓扑物理的调控机制。

Method: 采用高靶材利用率溅射（HiTUS）技术在热氧化Si/SiO₂(100)衬底上生长多晶Mn₃₊ₓSn₁₋ₓ薄膜及Mn₃₊ₓSn₁₋ₓ/Bi₀.₈₅Sb₀.₁₅异质结；通过引入缺陷和杂质诱导铁磁相（FM）并观察其对输运性质的影响；通过对比Bi₀.₈₅Sb₀.₁₅覆盖层与重金属覆盖层的效果，验证拓扑绝缘体界面的特异性。

Result: 多晶Mn₃₊ₓSn₁₋ₓ薄膜表现出源于拓扑外尔节点输运的负系数反常霍尔效应（AHE）；引入缺陷后产生的铁磁相几乎消除了拓扑外尔节点导电性，并在T<200 K下展现出大的交换偏置效应；在铁磁相Mn₃₊ₓSn₁₋ₓ上生长Bi₀.₈₅Sb₀.₁₅覆盖层后，外尔节点拓扑输运信号得到恢复，而重金属覆盖层无此效果。

Conclusion: 外尔节点拓扑输运信号的恢复归因于WSM/TI界面处形成了杂化的拓扑态，该态是外尔半金属费米弧与拓扑绝缘体表面态的杂化产物，并揭示了拓扑绝缘体在恢复拓扑输运中的关键作用。

Abstract: We report magnetotransport evidence of a hybridized Weyl semimetal (WSM) Fermi arc/topological insulator (TI) surface state at the interface of a ferromagnetic Mn$_{3+x}$Sn$_{1-x}$/Bi$_{0.85}$Sb$_{0.15}$ heterostructure. High target utilization sputtering (HiTUS) was used to grow polycrystalline Mn$_{3+x}$Sn$_{1-x}$ films and Mn$_{3+x}$Sn$_{1-x}$/Bi$_{0.85}$Sb$_{0.15}$ heterostructures on thermally oxidized Si/SiO$_2$ (100) substrates that exhibit the negative coefficient anomalous Hall effect (AHE) resulting from topological Weyl node transport. When various defects and impurities are introduced into these Mn$_{3+x}$Sn$_{1-x}$ films, a ferromagnetic (FM) phase develops that practically eliminates the topological Weyl node conduction. These FM Mn$_{3+x}$Sn$_{1-x}$ films exhibit large exchange bias effects below T=200 K that we attribute to the coexistence of a FM phase and the triangular antiferromagnetic (AFM) WSM phase. When Bi$_{0.85}$Sb$_{0.15}$ overlayers are grown on the FM Mn$_{3+x}$Sn$_{1-x}$, the magnetotransport signal of Weyl node topological transport is restored, an effect we do not observe when replacing the Bi$_{0.85}$Sb$_{0.15}$ TI with heavy metal overlayers. We attribute the restoration of the Weyl node topological transport to the formation of a hybridized topological state at the WSM/TI interface.

</details>


### [100] [Phase-dependent electronic structure of two-dimensional Ag layers at the graphene/SiC interface](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23855)
*Sawani Datta,Boyang Zheng,Arpit Jain,Kathrin Küster,Joshua A. Robinson,Vincent H. Crespi,Ulrich Starke*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文报道了一种在超高真空条件下原位制备石墨烯/SiC界面第二相插层银（Ag$_{(2)}$）的方法。通过低能电子衍射、角分辨光电子能谱和密度泛函理论计算，系统表征了Ag$_{(2)}$的晶体结构、电子能带特性及其对上层石墨烯电荷载流子密度和等离激元相互作用的调控作用，发现Ag$_{(2)}$相比第一相Ag$_{(1)}$具有更丰富的能带结构和更强的电荷掺杂效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 石墨烯/SiC界面插层（intercalation）方法可稳定原子级薄层材料，但所获插层相的结构与稳定性高度依赖于衬底缺陷分布。在石墨烯/SiC界面插层二维银中，已观察到两种相：与SiC晶格外延的相Ag$_{(1)}$已被广泛研究，而更致密的相Ag$_{(2)}$仍缺乏系统探索。因此，本研究旨在开发Ag$_{(2)}$的原位制备方法并揭示其结构与电子性质。

Method: 采用原位超高真空（ultra-high-vacuum, UHV）制备方法在石墨烯/SiC界面实现Ag$_{(2)}$插层相的生长，此前该相仅能通过高压限制异质外延（high-pressure confinement heteroepitaxy）制备。利用低能电子衍射（low-energy electron diffraction, LEED）表征晶体结构，高分辨角分辨光电子能谱（angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy, ARPES）测量电子能带，并结合密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）计算，通过定义展开熵（unfolding entropy）量化评估能带展开的适宜性。

Result: LEED显示Ag$_{(2)}$相对SiC晶格旋转30度并形成超胞，与Ag$_{(1)}$的$(1\times 1)$外延关系不同。ARPES表明Ag$_{(2)}$能带色散比Ag$_{(1)}$更丰富。DFT计算定义的展开熵定量表明Ag$_{(2)}$的能带结构更适宜展开至SiC原胞，展开后的能带色散与实验数据高度吻合。此外，Ag$_{(2)}$使上层准自由石墨烯的电荷载流子密度比Ag$_{(1)}$提高约1.75倍，并改变了石墨烯层的电荷-等离激元相互作用，表明界面有效屏蔽效应发生变化。

Conclusion: 成功开发了Ag$_{(2)}$插层相的原位UHV制备方法，系统表征了其晶体和电子结构。不同银插层相可差异化调控石墨烯层的电子性质，为通过界面工程（interface engineering）调控二维材料性质提供了新途径。

Abstract: Intercalation at the graphene/SiC interface provides a controlled route to stabilize atomically thin layers with properties distinct from their bulk counterparts. In this platform, the structure and stability of the intercalated phase depend sensitively on the defect landscape of the starting substrate. For intercalated two-dimensional silver at the graphene/SiC interface, two phases have been observed: a phase epitaxial to the SiC lattice, Ag$_{(1)}$, readily obtained following the conventional intercalation method under ultra-high-vacuum conditions and extensively characterized, and a more densely packed phase, called Ag$_{(2)}$, which has remained largely unexplored. Here we report an in situ ultra-high-vacuum preparation method of the second phase intercalated at the graphene/SiC interface; this phase previously was prepared via high-pressure confinement heteroepitaxy. Low-energy electron diffraction shows that Ag$_{(2)}$ is rotated by 30 degree relative to the SiC lattice and forms supercells, in contrast to the $(1\times 1)$ epitaxial relation of Ag$_{(1)}$ with SiC. High-resolution angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy reveals a more rich Ag$_{(2)}$ band dispersion compared to the Ag$_{(1)}$. In density functional theory calculations, by defining the unfolding entropy which, in a quantified way, finds that the band structure of Ag$_{(2)}$ is more suitable to be unfolded to the SiC primitive cell, and the resulting unfolded band dispersion is in great agreement with the experimental data. We further show that the different intercalated Ag phases tune the electronic properties of the overlying quasi-free-standing graphene layer differently: compared with Ag$_{(1)}$, Ag$_{(2)}$ yields an $\sim$1.75 times higher charge carrier density and modifies the charge-plasmon interaction of the graphene layer, indicating a change in effective screening at the interface.

</details>


### [101] [Photoluminescent Tetragonal Tb-doped Pb2P2O7](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23876)
*Yong Liu,Wenhua Bi,Alla Arakcheeva,Arnaud Magrez*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究报道了一种新型四方相（tetragonal polymorph）Tb掺杂Pb2P2O7的合成与表征，通过单晶X射线衍射确认了室温下P41和P43对映体的稳定化。光学研究显示Tb3+的特征绿色光致发光（photoluminescence），其强度随温度先增至125°C后发生热猝灭（thermal quenching），且材料在约800°C熔化前无相变，表明其作为新型光致发光材料的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索新型稀土掺杂无机发光材料，具体通过Tb3+离子掺杂稳定Pb2P2O7的四方多晶型，并系统研究其结构、光学性质与热稳定性。

Method: 采用单晶X射线衍射（single-crystal XRD）确定晶体结构；通过光致发光（PL）光谱研究Tb3+的5D4 → 7Fj特征跃迁；利用功率依赖和温度依赖PL测量分析激发过程与发光行为；使用高温X射线衍射（high-temperature XRD）评估高温结构稳定性。

Result: Tb3+掺杂稳定了室温下P41和P43对映体；观察到Tb3+的绿色光致发光，由于晶场效应（crystal field effect）各发射峰发生分裂，表明Tb3+处于多种配位环境；PL强度呈线性功率律行为，对应单光子激发（one-photon excitation）过程；温度依赖PL显示强度在125°C前上升（源于结构缺陷的能量转移），随后发生热猝灭；材料在约800°C熔化前无相变。

Conclusion: 四方相Tb掺杂Pb2P2O7具有优异的结构稳定性和特征绿色发光性能，是一种具有潜力的新型光致发光材料。

Abstract: In this study, we report the synthesis and characterization of a novel tetragonal polymorph of Tb-doped Pb2P2O7. Single-crystal X-ray diffraction confirms the stabilization of the P41 and P43 enantiomorphs at room temperature due to the incorporation of Tb3+ ions. Optical investigations reveal green photoluminescence from the characteristic 5D4 -> 7Fj (J = 1-5) transitions of Tb3+, with each emission split due to the crystal field effect, indicating the presence of Tb3+ in multiple coordination environments. The power dependence of the PL intensity follows a linear power-law behavior, suggesting a one-photon excitation process. Temperature-dependent PL measurements show an initial increase in intensity up to 125C, attributed to energy transfer from structural defects, followed by thermal quenching above this temperature. Structural stability at elevated temperatures is confirmed via high-temperature X-ray diffraction (XRD), showing no phase transitions before melting at approximately 800C. These findings highlight the potential of tetragonal Tb-doped Pb2P2O7 as a new class of photoluminescent material.

### [102] [Propagation Maps, Maradona Exceptional Points, and Pele Singularities in Anisotropic, Tellegen, Chiral, Moving-Medium, Omega and Other Isotropy-Broken Materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22839)
*Maxim Durach*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文通过将Fresnel波面转化为传播映射（propagation map），系统描述了各向异性（anisotropic）、非互易（non-reciprocal）及双曲（hyperbolic）等对称性破缺光子材料中正负相速度传播、衰减与放大的组织方式，揭示了Hermitian体系中的Michelangelo轮廓分界线（Michelangelo silhouette separatrix）与非Hermitian体系中的Caravaggio明暗分界线（Caravaggio chiaroscuro separatrix），并定义了与之对应的Maradona奇异点（Maradona exceptional points）和Pele奇异点（Pele singularities），其中后者由非Hermitian线宽坍塌（linewidth collapse）产生，表现为动量分辨态密度（momentum-resolved density of states, DOS）的尖锐峰值与符号反转。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 各向异性、Tellegen、手性（chiral）、运动介质型、omega、回旋（gyrotropic）、双曲及多双曲材料等对称性破缺光子介质中，波动传播无法仅由Fresnel波面（Fresnel wave surface）描述，需要更系统的几何语言来组织正负相速度、衰减与放大等传播行为。

Method: 将Fresnel波面转化为传播映射（propagation map），在Hermitian介质中识别向前与向后传播之间的Michelangelo轮廓分界线（也是Maradona奇异点的连续轨迹），在非Hermitian介质中识别衰减-放大边界形成的Caravaggio明暗分界线（关联Pele奇异点），并借助动量分辨态密度的Lorentzian线宽分析揭示奇异点的物理意义。

Result: 在Hermitian体系中，Michelangelo轮廓分界线是折射率算符（index-of-refraction operator）退化的连续轨迹（Maradona奇异点）；在非Hermitian体系中，Caravaggio分界线处的Pele奇异点保持手征性连续而增益-损耗特性改变符号，其动量分辨态密度的Lorentzian线宽坍塌，产生尖锐DOS峰值且符号跨分界线反转。

Conclusion: Pele奇异点是Fresnel波面传播映射中由非Hermitian线宽坍塌产生的阈值型增益-损耗奇异点（threshold-like gain-loss singularity），其结果为对称性破缺电磁材料中手征性（handedness）、简并性（degeneracy）、损耗、增益与动量分辨态密度的组织提供了一种紧凑的几何描述语言。

Abstract: Anisotropic, Tellegen, chiral, moving-medium-type, omega, gyrotropic, hyperbolic, and multi-hyperbolic materials form an important class of isotropy-broken photonic media in which wave propagation can no longer be characterized by the Fresnel wave surface alone. Here we show that Fresnel wave surfaces can be converted into propagation maps that organize positive- and negative-phase-velocity propagation together with attenuation and amplification. In Hermitian media, the boundary between forward and backward propagation forms the Michelangelo silhouette separatrix. This separatrix is also a continuous locus of Maradona exceptional points, where the index-of-refraction operator becomes defective even though the material medium remains Hermitian. In non-Hermitian media, the attenuation-amplification boundary forms the Caravaggio chiaroscuro separatrix. The associated Pele singularities occur where the handedness remains continuous while the gain-loss character changes sign. Their physical importance is revealed by the momentum-resolved density of states: at these points, the Lorentzian linewidth of the non-Hermitian momentum-resolved density of states (DOS) collapses, producing sharp DOS peaks whose sign reverses across the separatrix. Thus, Pele singularities are threshold-like gain-loss singularities of the Fresnel wave-surface propagation map, generated by non-Hermitian linewidth collapse. The result is a compact geometric language for describing how handedness, degeneracy, loss, gain, and momentum-resolved DOS are organized in isotropy-broken electromagnetic materials.

</details>


### [103] [Real time monitoring of pressure-induced deformation of PDMS to evaluate pressure distribution in microfluidic channels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23729)
*Kiran Acharya,Serge Monneret,Martin Brandenbourger,Thomas Chaigne*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于定量相位成像（quantitative phase imaging）的微流控通道压力测量方法，通过监测通道形变实现高灵敏度、实时、大视场的压力传感，无需嵌入额外元件或改造芯片。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 微米级通道中的精确压力测量对多种微流控应用至关重要，但现有方法通常需要在芯片制造期间或之后集成额外探头或传感元件，增加了系统复杂性和制造难度。

Method: 采用定量相位成像技术，测量柔性微流控通道在压力作用下的形变，从而反推通道内压力。该方法利用光学相位信息获取形变量，无需嵌入组件或修改微流控器件本身。

Result: 实验证明该方法能在无需嵌入式组件或器件改造的前提下，实现大视场（large field of view）下通道形变的实时（real-time）测量，且具有高灵敏度。

Conclusion: 所提出的基于定量相位成像的压力传感方法为微流控系统提供了一种非侵入式、免集成元件的压力测量途径，兼具高灵敏度和实时性，有望简化微流控实验中的压力监测流程。

Abstract: Accurate pressure measurements in micrometric channels are essential for a wide range of microfluidic applications. Existing approaches rely on a variety of sensing mechanisms, but generally require the integration of additional probes or sensing elements during or after chip fabrication. Here, we introduce a pressure sensing approach based on quantitative phase imaging of the deformation of compliant microfluidic channels. We demonstrate real-time measurements of channel deformation over a large field of view with high sensitivity, without the need for embedded components or modifications of the microfluidic device.

</details>

### [104] [Phase diagram of the vortex state in an amorphous Re6Zr thin film exhibiting inverse melting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23567)
*Pritam Das,Subhamita Sengupta,Anjan Jana,Rishabh Duhan,Sulagna Dutta,Arghya Dutta,John Jesudasan,Vivas Bagwe,Pratap Raychaudhuri*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在第二类超导体（Type II superconductor）中，涡旋晶格（vortex lattice）可以表现出"反熔融"（inverse melting）现象，即随温度升高从液态转变为晶态。该现象近期在20 nm厚的非晶Re6Zr薄膜中通过扫描隧道显微镜（scanning tunneling microscopy, STM）被观测到，但其对应的宏观输运和磁响应特征尚不清楚，需要进一步刻画。

Method: 采用直流（d.c.）输运测量和低频磁屏蔽（low-frequency magnetic screening）响应实验，结合扫描隧道谱（scanning tunneling spectroscopy, STS）成像技术，系统研究非晶Re6Zr薄膜中涡旋态随温度和磁场变化的演化行为，并比较不同厚度（5 nm、20 nm和50 nm）样品的差异。

Result: 成功识别出反熔融相变在输运和磁响应中的特征信号，构建了磁场-温度（magnetic field-temperature）参数空间下的完整涡旋态相图（vortex-state phase diagram）。发现反熔融存在厚度依赖性：5 nm薄膜维持非均匀液态（inhomogeneous liquid state），50 nm薄膜除上临界场（upper critical field）附近外保持晶态（crystalline solid structure）。

Conclusion: 反熔融现象在非晶Re6Zr薄膜中具有明确的输运和磁响应特征，且其行为强烈依赖于薄膜厚度，表明维度效应对涡旋晶格相变起着关键调控作用。

Abstract: In Type II superconductors, the vortex lattice can exhibit "inverse melting," transitioning from a liquid to a crystalline solid as temperature increases. While recently observed via scanning tunneling microscopy in a 20 nm thick amorphous Re6Zr thin film, this work investigates the corresponding d.c. transport and low-frequency magnetic screening responses. By identifying distinct signatures of these transitions and integrating scanning tunneling spectroscopy imaging, we construct a comprehensive vortex-state phase diagram in the magnetic field-temperature parameter space. Furthermore, we demonstrate that inverse melting is thickness-dependent: a 5 nm film retains an inhomogeneous liquid state, while a 50 nm film maintains a crystalline solid structure except near the upper critical field.

### [105] [Disorder-Induced Phase Transitions in Altermagnetic Josephson Junctions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23607)
*Chang-An Li*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该论文研究了d波交错磁约瑟夫森结（altermagnetic Josephson junction, AMJJ）中无序对非常规相的影响，发现无序可以诱导π相与0相之间的相变并强烈抑制临界电流，且异常φ相在无序中高度脆弱，可被非互易地驱动为π相或0相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实验和理论已发现交错磁约瑟夫森结（AMJJ）尽管宏观净磁化强度为零，却可支持非常规的π相和φ相。但这些相在真实材料中存在的无序下是否稳定，仍是一个未解决的问题。

Method: 本文对二维d波AMJJ中的无序效应进行理论分析，研究其对非常规约瑟夫森相位的影响。通过分析隧穿库珀对相移（tunneling Cooper-pair phase shift）和超导退相干（superconducting decoherence）的修正来阐释无序的作用机制。

Result: 无序能够诱导非常规π相与常规0相之间的相变，并强烈抑制临界电流。异常φ相在无序存在时高度脆弱，可被非互易地（nonreciprocally）驱动为π相或0相。在这些相变过程中，电流-相位关系（current-phase relation）的第一谐波改变符号，而高阶谐波被迅速抑制。

Conclusion: 该发现揭示了无序在调控AMJJ不同相中的关键作用，为理解AMJJ的潜在功能提供了新的视角。

Abstract: Altermagnetic Josephson junctions (AMJJs) can host unconventional $π$ phase and $\varphi$ phase despite vanishing net magnetizations. Whether these phases are stable against disorder existing in real materials remains an open question. Here, we investigate impact of disorder on exotic phases in two-dimensional d-wave AMJJs. We show that disorder is able to induce phase transitions between the exotic $π$ and conventional 0 phases, accompanied by a strong suppression of critical current. This behavior is attributed to modifications of the tunneling Cooper-pair phase shift and superconducting decoherence. Remarkably, the anomalous $\varphi$ phase is highly fragile in presence of disorder and can be driven to either a $π$ phase or 0 phase in a nonreciprocal manner. Across such transitions, the first harmonic of current-phase relation changes sign, while the higher-order harmonics are rapidly suppressed. Our findings reveal the crucial role of disorder in tailoring distinct phases of AMJJs and shed new light on their potential functionalities.

### [106] [Quantum critical collapse of a pinned vortex glass](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23838)
*David Perconte,Thibault Charpentier,Nikolaos Koutsopoulos,Kalpajit Roy,Nadjib Benchabane,Xiaoli Peng,Florent Blondelle,Frédéric Gay,Mikhail Feigel'man,Viktor Kabanov,Benjamin Sacépé*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究通过等离子体微波光谱学测量非晶氧化铟薄膜中超导谐振器的超流密度，发现其在磁场中仅呈对数缓慢衰减，并在临界场线性消失。这一反常行为归因于涡旋-涡旋相互作用增强的集体钉扎机制，揭示了涡旋玻璃态是磁场驱动超导体-绝缘体相变的关键中间态，并展现出显著的正Kerr非线性光学效应，具有量子传感潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强无序超导体中，无序与涡旋-涡旋相互作用可稳定涡旋玻璃态（vortex-glass state），其特征为强钉扎和缺乏位置有序。然而，该态在磁场驱动的超导体-绝缘体相变（superconductor–insulator transition）中如何破坏超导电性，此前尚未得到解决。

Method: 研究采用等离子体微波光谱学（plasmonic microwave spectroscopy），对非晶氧化铟（amorphous indium oxide）薄膜制成的超导谐振器进行测量，直接追踪超流密度（superfluid density）直至临界场 $B_c$。

Result: 超流密度在近三个数量级的磁场范围内仅呈对数缓慢衰减，与涡旋晶格（vortex lattices）预期的快速幂律抑制（power-law suppression）形成鲜明对比。超流密度在 $B_c$ 处线性消失，伴随磁阻测量识别出的连续量子临界点（quantum critical point）。此外，涡旋玻璃态表现出异常大的非线性电磁响应，即显著的正Kerr效应（positive-Kerr effect）。

Conclusion: 这些结果表明，无序控制着临界磁场，涡旋玻璃态是磁感应超导体-绝缘体相变的关键中间态。涡旋-涡旋相互作用反直觉地增强了集体钉扎机制（collective vortex-pinning mechanism），从而导致了超流密度的反常缓慢衰减，并揭示了涡旋玻璃态在量子传感中的潜在应用价值。

Abstract: The interplay between disorder and vortex--vortex interactions in strongly disordered superconductors in a magnetic field can stabilize a vortex-glass state, characterized by strong pinning and the absence of positional order. Yet its role in the destruction of superconductivity at the field-driven superconductor--insulator transition has remained unresolved. Here we use plasmonic microwave spectroscopy of superconducting resonators patterned from amorphous indium oxide thin films to directly track the superfluid density up to the critical field $B_c$. We find an unexpected resilience of the superfluid density, which decreases only logarithmically over nearly three orders of magnitude in field, in stark contrast to the rapid power-law suppression expected for vortex lattices. We attribute this anomalously slow decay to a collective vortex-pinning mechanism counterintuitively enhanced by vortex--vortex interactions. The superfluid density then vanishes linearly at $B_c$, where independent magnetoresistance measurements identify a continuous quantum critical point, unlike the abrupt transition observed at zero field. We further uncover an exceptionally large nonlinear electromagnetic response of the vortex glass, manifested as a pronounced positive-Kerr effect with potential for quantum sensing. These results show how disorder controls the critical magnetic field and identify the vortex glass as the key intermediate state governing the magnetic-field-induced superconductor--insulator transition.

</details>

Method: 利用基于CUDA的高性能并行计算，数值研究存在弦云（string clouds）和暗能量（dark energy）成分的非对易旋转带电黑洞的事件视界结构、阴影性质及能量发射率；基于数值数据构建训练集，使用全连接神经网络（fully connected neural network）判断参数集是否与事件视界望远镜（Event Horizon Telescope）观测数据匹配。

Abstract: Motivated by string theory, we constrain non-commutative black hole parameters through shadow behaviors using machine learning techniques combined by CUDA computations. To do so, we first investigate the structure of the event horizon of non-commutative black holes in the presence of string clouds and dark energy sectors by exploiting CUDA-based methods. We numerically approach the shadow properties and the energy emission rate of rotating and charged black holes in non-commutative geometry via such high-performance parallel computings. To bridge these findings with observational data, we implement a CUDA-based framework in order to constrain the involved black hole parameters including the non-commutative one. Using the resulting numerical data, we build a robust training datasets for a fully connected neural network to determine whether a given set of parameters matches with the observational data provided by Event Horizon Telescope collaborations. As a result, we find that the non-commutative model under study is consistent with the observations of $SgrA^*_{\mathrm{Keck}}$ black holes.

### [108] [Gravitational Field of a Rotating Mass on an Expanding Universe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22895)
*Antonio Peña Peña*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出爱因斯坦场方程的一个新精确解，将克尔黑洞（Kerr black hole）与弗里德曼-勒梅特-罗伯逊-沃克宇宙学（FLRW cosmology）统一起来；该解在适当极限下退化为克尔-德西特度规（Kerr-de Sitter metric），并同时描述了黑洞内外宇宙膨胀的动力学。结果正确推广了麦维蒂度规（McVittie metric）至旋转质量情形，或克尔-德西特度规至任意尺度因子 $a(t)$，并发现能层（ergosphere）随宇宙膨胀趋于消失。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有经典解分别描述了旋转黑洞（克尔解）和膨胀宇宙（FLRW宇宙学），但缺乏一个同时考虑旋转黑洞嵌入动态膨胀宇宙的精确解。本文旨在填补这一空白，将克尔度规与FLRW宇宙学统一为单一精确解。

Method: 通过构造爱因斯坦场方程的一个新精确解来实现统一；该度规在适当极限下可还原为克尔-德西特度规，并包含任意的宇宙尺度因子 $a(t)$，从而推广了麦维蒂度规和克尔-德西特度规。

Result: 新解预测黑洞具有静止质量（stationary mass），且能层和事件视界（event horizon）相对于膨胀的宇宙静止参考系（cosmic rest frame）呈现收缩行为。此外，能层随宇宙膨胀趋于消失，暗能量（dark energy）与黑洞旋转之间无进一步相互作用。

Conclusion: 该解正确推广了麦维蒂度规（原适用于非旋转质量）至旋转质量情形，或克尔-德西特度规（原适用于恒定宇宙常数）至任意尺度因子 $a(t)$，从而为研究旋转黑洞在动态膨胀宇宙中的行为提供了统一的精确框架。

Abstract: We present a new exact solution to Einstein's field equations that unifies the Kerr black hole with Friedmann-Lemaître-Robertson-Walker cosmology. This metric reduces to Kerr-de Sitter in the appropriate limit and accounts for cosmological expansion dynamics both inside and outside the black hole. The model predicts a stationary mass, as well as a contracting ergosphere and event horizon with respect to the expanding cosmic rest frame. This result correctly generalises the McVittie metric to rotating masses or Kerr-de Sitter to arbitrary scale factors $a(t)$. Additionally, we find that the ergosphere tends to fade away with respect to the universe's expansion and no further interactions of dark energy with respect to the black hole's rotation.

</details>


### [109] [Horizon structure and extremal configurations of Kerr-Newman-anti-de Sitter black holes in f(R) gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23090)
*Alikram N. Aliev*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文基于广义相对论中Kerr-Newman-(A)dS黑洞解与f(R)引力中常曲率对应解之间的对应关系，采用统一框架研究其视界结构与极端构型，重点分析反de Sitter情形。通过求解关于旋转参数a²和反弯曲率标度l⁻²的极端性条件，得到了封闭的解析关系，给出了极端分支在参数空间中的透明参数化描述，并确定了物理允许的极端区域及电荷上限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 建立广义相对论中Kerr-Newman-(A)dS黑洞解与f(R)引力中常曲率对应解之间的统一描述框架，系统分析其视界结构（horizon structure）与极端构型（extremal configurations）的物理性质，尤其是反de Sitter情形下的极端分支行为。

Method: 利用两类黑洞解之间的对应关系（correspondence），构建统一分析框架；通过求解关于旋转参数a²和反弯曲率标度l⁻²的极端性条件（extremality conditions），导出封闭解析关系；对比反de Sitter与de Sitter情形下的极端分支结构差异。

Result: 得到了物理允许的极端区域，推导出电荷上限q_max=M/2；在无电荷情形下旋转参数沿极端分支单调递减且有下界，最小旋转a_min=3√3M/8；极端分支存在内外标度匹配点（scale-matching point）；引入电荷后最小旋转降至a_min=M/4；AdS情形受几何端点（geometric endpoint）约束，dS分支则呈现超极端极大值（ultra-extremal maximum）等更丰富结构；四阶视界方程（quartic horizon equation）的代数质量约束完全消除实根结构，产生一类无物理视界的解。

Conclusion: AdS与dS两种极端分支具有截然不同的结构特性：AdS极端性受到几何端点的严格约束，而dS分支展现出更复杂的超极端现象；电荷的引入会拓展极端分支并降低最小旋转值；某些情形下代数约束可导致黑洞完全失去物理视界。

Abstract: Exploiting the correspondence between Kerr-Newman-(A)dS black hole solutions in general relativity and their constant-curvature counterparts in $f(R)$ gravity, we employ a unified framework to investigate the horizon structure and extremal configurations of these black holes, focusing primarily on the anti-de Sitter case. By solving the extremality conditions with respect to the squared rotation parameter $a^2$ and the inverse curvature scale $l^{-2}$, we obtain closed analytic relations that provide a transparent parametrization of the extremal branch in the $(a^2,\, l^{-2})$ parameter space. We determine the physically admissible extremal domain and derive an upper bound on the electric charge, $q_{\max}=M/2$, corresponding to the point at which the metric becomes singular and the extremal branch terminates. For vanishing electric charge, the rotation parameter decreases monotonically along the extremal branch and remains bounded from below, implying the existence of a minimal rotation, $a_{\min}=3\sqrt{3}M/8$. The extremal branch also exhibits a distinguished internal scale-matching point at which the rotation parameter and the AdS curvature scale become comparable. The inclusion of electric charge introduces an additional competing scale, extending the extremal branch while lowering the minimal rotation to $a_{\min}=M/4$ at the maximal allowed charge $q_{\max}=M/2$. Comparing these results with the corresponding de Sitter case, we show that extremality in AdS is constrained by a geometric endpoint, whereas the dS branch exhibits a considerably richer structure characterized by an ultra-extremal maximum and a subsequent decay toward the non-rotating limit. Finally, we demonstrate that the algebraic mass constraint associated with the quartic horizon equation completely removes the real-root structure, yielding a class of solutions without physical horizons.

</details>


### [110] [General Expressions for Measurable Parameters in Curved Spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23337)
*Dmitri Lebedev,Kayll Lake*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在广义协变框架下，系统建立了用于测量角度、距离、速度和加速度的通用表达式，并发展了费米坐标系（Fermi frames）与费米-沃克导数（Fermi-Walker derivative）等数学工具，讨论了曲率效应、相对静止条件、光学距离及推广的测地偏离方程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为在任意实验设置下提供关于可测量角度、距离、速度和加速度的广义协变（general covariant）表达式，使曲率效应以清晰的张量形式体现，弥补现有理论在处理观测者与近距物体间物理距离时缺乏统一协变描述的不足。

Method: 通过建立几何指数映射（geometrical exponential map）的展开式，并借助费米坐标系与费米-沃克导数等工具，推导出适用于任意方向观测者与光线的相对论光行差（relativistic aberration）关系，以及针对任意秩张量的广义泰勒展开（Taylor expansion）。进一步给出角直径距离（angular diameter distance）与光度距离（luminosity distance）的广义表达式，并验证了互易定理（reciprocity theorem）。

Result: 得到了包含曲率效应的、以一般张量形式表示的可测量距离、速度和加速度公式；从第一性原理出发推导了费米-沃克导数并赋予其物理含义；给出了适用于极端相对运动（extreme relative motion）的推广测地偏离方程（geodesic deviation equation）。

Conclusion: 本文构建了一套完整的广义协变测量理论框架，为相对论性观测几何中各类可测量量提供了统一的数学表述，并对费米-沃克导数等核心概念给出了从物理原理出发的严格推导。

Abstract: General covariant expressions for measurable angles, distances, velocities, and accelerations are provided in terms of fundamental parameters that can be applied in any setup. The relativistic aberration of light relationship is presented in full generality, which is applicable to any orientation of observers and light rays. An expansion for the geometrical exponential map is established and used to form an expression for the physical distance between an observer and a nearby object within its extended local frame. Curvature effects on measurable distances, velocities, and accelerations are made explicit and appear in general tensorial form. The concepts of Fermi frames on timelike worldlines and the Fermi-Walker derivative are discussed in detail and used throughout; and in examining the meaning of relative stationarity between timelike observers, the Fermi-Walker derivative is established from first principles through physically meaningful consideration. A generalized type of Taylor expansion is provided for tensors of any rank in a covariant form. Expressions for the optically based angular diameter distance and luminosity distance are provided in general forms, and the reciprocity theorem is discussed and verified. A generalized version of the geodesic deviation equation, applicable to extreme relative motion, is provided as well.

</details>


### [111] [The field-theoretical formalism for TEGR](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23376)
*E. D. Emtsova,A. N. Petrov*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 论文将广义相对论的teleparallel等价形式（TEGR）表述为场论形式，在该形式中，tetrad与物质扰动在TEGR背景解上传播，并基于该形式推导了守恒流、超势和荷，成功计算了Schwarzschild和Kerr黑洞的质量以及Kerr解的角动量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在为TEGR（teleparallel equivalent of general relativity）建立一个基于拉格朗日量（Lagrangian）的场论表述，使扰动（perturbations）作为动力学场来处理，从而统一描述背景与扰动，并为后续的守恒量构造和黑洞物理分析提供系统框架。

Method: 采用拉格朗日场论方法，将tetrad与物质扰动视为动力学场，在满足背景Einstein场方程的TEGR背景解上进行传播。通过变分原理推导扰动方程，定义规范（gauge）变换并论证拉格朗日量与场方程的规范不变性（gauge invariance）。应用Noether定理（Noether theorem）构造守恒流、超势（superpotential）及相关荷（charge）。作为应用，在Ricci平坦背景上研究线性引力方程，导出TT规范（TT-gauge）下的引力波方程与tetrad扰动。

Result: 成功构建了TEGR的场论化扰动形式，该形式与原TEGR等价且允许有限（非无穷小）扰动。通过新电荷公式，计算了Schwarzschild黑洞和Kerr黑洞的质量，以及Kerr解的角动量，结果均符合预期。

Conclusion: 该新形式具有强大功能，可用于TEGR的进一步推广，展现出良好的未来发展潜力。

Abstract: The teleparallel equivalent of general relativity (TEGR) is represented in a field-theoretical form, where tetrad and matter perturbations are propagated on a background solution of TEGR. Thus, the background tetrad and metric satisfy the background Einstein field equations. This presentation, where perturbations can be finite (not infinitesimal or approximate), is equivalent to the original form of TEGR. The background can be arbitrary, usually corresponding to the solution of TEGR under consideration. Such a formalism is Lagrangian based, where perturbations are classified as dynamic fields, and varying the Lagrangian with respect to dynamic variables leads to the equations for perturbations. Gauge (inner) transformations are defined, and the gauge invariance of the Lagrangian and the field equations are stated. Applying the Noether theorem to the Lagrangian we construct conserved currents, related superpotentials and charges. As an application, we have considered linear gravitational equations on the Ricci-flat background and analyzed their properties, finally deriving gravitational wave equations and the tetrad perturbations in TT-gauge. By new formulae for charges, we have calculated the mass for the Schwarzschild and Kerr black holes and the angular momentum for the Kerr solution. The results are quite acceptable, which signals that the new formalism is powerful, can be used further, and has a potential for future development that can be applied to generalizations of TEGR.

</details>


### [112] [On the Gravitational Angular Momentum of Axial Perturbations of a Regular Black Hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23711)
*S. C. Ulhoa,F. L. Carneiro,B. C. C. Carneiro*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在广义相对论的遥平行等价理论（TEGR）框架下，推导了Bardeen正则黑洞轴性（奇宇称）微扰所携带的引力角动量δJ表达式，发现δJ在奇多极指数ℓ时为零、偶ℓ时非零的多极选择定则，并利用轴性准正则模展示了δJ的径向与时间行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在TEGR框架下研究Bardeen正则黑洞轴性微扰所携带的引力角动量，旨在揭示引力角动量的多极选择定则，并检验该角动量在奇偶宇称微扰模式下的不同行为。

Method: 采用TEGR中的哈密顿定义（Hamiltonian definition of conserved quantities）计算守恒量；针对Bardeen正则黑洞的轴性（odd-parity）微扰，导出微扰角动量δJ关于轴性微扰函数h0(r,t)的闭式表达式。

Result: δJ表现出尖锐的多极选择定则（multipolar selection rule）：对于多极指数ℓ为奇数值的模式，δJ为零；而对于ℓ为偶数值的模式，δJ贡献非零。利用已知的Bardeen时空轴性准正则模（axial quasinormal modes）展示了δJ的径向和时间依赖行为。

Conclusion: 在TEGR框架下，Bardeen正则黑洞的轴性微扰角动量仅由偶ℓ模式贡献，奇ℓ模式完全消失，这为理解正则黑洞微扰的角动量输运提供了新的约束条件。

Abstract: This Letter deals with the gravitational angular momentum carried by axial (odd-parity) perturbations of the Bardeen regular black hole within the teleparallel equivalent of general relativity (TEGR). Using the Hamiltonian definition of conserved quantities in TEGR, we derive a closed expression for the perturbative angular momentum $δJ$ in terms of the axial perturbation function $h_0(r,t)$. The result exhibits a sharp multipolar selection rule: $δJ$ vanishes for odd values of the multipole index $\ell$, while even-$\ell$ modes yield a nonzero contribution. The radial and temporal behavior of $δJ$ is illustrated using the known axial quasinormal modes of the Bardeen spacetime.

</details>


### [113] [The imprints of the instantaneous appearance of a conformal Killing vector field on the evolution of self-gravitating fluid spheres](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23732)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自引力流体球（self-gravitating fluid spheres）在演化过程中，共形 Killing 矢量（conformal Killing vector, CKV）的瞬时出现可能对系统动力学产生重要影响，但该瞬时效应尚未被系统研究。本文旨在通过引入适当的张量变量，刻画 CKV 在特定时间瞬间出现时的物理后果，并寻找可用于探测这一事件的可观测信号（smoking gun signature）。

Method: 作者引入了一个张量变量（tensor variable），其时间依赖性（time dependence）决定了在给定类时坐标（time-like coordinate）取值下 CKV 是否存在。研究分别考虑了绝热流体（adiabatic fluid）和耗散流体（dissipative fluid）两种情形，通过分析相关物理变量在 CKV 出现前后的变化，识别该事件的特征信号。

Result: 分析表明，自引力流体球演化过程中 CKV 的瞬时出现会在某些相关物理变量上留下明确的可观测特征，即所谓的“冒烟枪信号”（smoking gun signature），可作为该事件发生的判据。

Conclusion: 本文为识别自引力系统演化中共形对称性的瞬时出现提供了理论框架与信号判据；文中还讨论了该结果在未来研究中的潜在应用前景以及尚待解决的开放问题。

Abstract: We study the influence of the instantaneous appearance of a conformal Killing vector (CKV) in self-gravitating fluid spheres during their evolution. For doing that we introduce a tensor variable whose time dependence allows the existence of a CKV for a given value of the time-like coordinate. We consider adiabatic and dissipative fluids. The analysis of different relevant physical variables in this process provides a smoking gun signature from the emergence of CKV at some point of the evolution. Prospective applications of these results, as well as open questions and pending issues related to this problem, are discussed.

### [114] [Entropy and stability of an extremally charged Einstein-Born-Infeld thin shell](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23767)
*Ernesto Eiroa,Griselda Figueroa-Aguirre,Miguel Peñafiel*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在爱因斯坦引力与玻恩-因费尔德电动力学（Born-Infeld electrodynamics）耦合框架下，研究了球对称薄壳（spherical thin shell）的动力学稳定性与热力学稳定性。采用极值带电解，推导了径向扰动下的动力学稳定条件，并建立了完整的平衡热力学。研究发现，尽管壳上存在非零压力，其熵仅由引力半径决定；热力学稳定性条件归结为与壳上电荷交换相关的一个单一不等式，确定了动力学与热力学稳定构型共存的参数区域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 提供一个能够同时自洽研究薄壳物质动力学稳定性与热力学稳定性的理论框架，并将其应用于爱因斯坦引力与玻恩-因费尔德电动力学耦合的极值带电薄壳系统。

Method: 采用极值带电（extremally charged）解析解以获得视界位置的闭合解析形式，通过有效势（effective potential）方法分析径向扰动下的动力学稳定性；建立完整的平衡热力学（equilibrium thermodynamics），并引入物理合理的状态方程（equations of state）假设以求得壳的熵密度封闭表达式。

Result: 动力学稳定性条件通过有效势形式给出；与极值赖斯纳-诺德斯特罗姆（Reissner-Nordström）情形不同，该壳上存在非零压力；壳的熵唯一地表示为引力半径的函数；热力学稳定性条件简化为一个与壳上电荷交换相关的单一不等式，确定了动力学与热力学稳定构型共存区域。

Conclusion: 在爱因斯坦-玻恩-因费尔德理论框架下，极值带电薄壳的动力学与热力学稳定性可由简洁条件刻画，两者的兼容性决定了稳定构型的可行域。

Abstract: Spacetimes with a thin shell offer a framework where both the dynamical stability and the thermodynamical stability of the matter comprising the shell can be consistently studied. In the present work, we consider the dynamical and thermodynamical stability of a spherical thin shell in Einstein gravity coupled to Born-Infeld electrodynamics. For our construction, we adopt the extremally charged solution of the theory, which offers a closed analytic form for the horizon location that allows for a clear derivation of the corresponding physical quantities of interest. Under this scenario, the dynamical stability conditions under radial perturbations are readily obtained in terms of an effective potential. The complete equilibrium thermodynamics for such a shell is presented. We find that, despite a non-zero pressure at the shell (unlike the extremally charged Reissner-Nordström counterpart), its entropy is solely characterized as a function of the gravitational radius. We propose a physically suitable \emph{ansätze} for the relevant equations of state in order to obtain a closed expression for the entropy density of the shell. We find that the thermodynamical stability conditions reduce to a single inequality related to exchanges of the charge at the shell, which determines the domain where both dynamical and thermodynamical stable configurations exist.

### [115] [Natural Metric-Affine Inflation: Reloaded](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23827)
*D. Kraiko,A. Racioppi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文在度规-仿射引力（metric-affine gravity）框架下重新审视自然暴胀（natural inflation），通过引入暴胀子（inflaton）与Nieh-Yan项（Nieh-Yan term）的周期非最小耦合（periodic non-minimal coupling），并结合与Ricci标量的类似耦合，成功使得模型在亚普朗克周期尺度（sub-Planckian periodicity scale）和较小耦合常数下仍与观测数据相符。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准的自然暴胀（natural inflation）模型在与观测数据比较时面临困境，特别是在强耦合极限下仅能给出线性暴胀（linear inflation）预测，无法有效解救自然暴胀场景。因此，作者旨在通过引入度规-仿射引力（metric-affine gravity）中的新耦合机制来拓展模型空间，使自然暴胀在更宽泛的参数范围内与数据兼容。

Method: 作者在度规-仿射引力框架下引入暴胀子与Nieh-Yan项之间的周期非最小耦合，同时额外加入与Ricci标量（Ricci scalar）的类似非最小耦合，并分析这些耦合对暴胀动力学和可观测量（如标量谱指数和张量-标量比）的影响。

Result: 仅引入Nieh-Yan项的非最小耦合在强耦合极限下导致线性暴胀预测，无法挽救自然暴胀场景。但一旦加入与Ricci标量的非最小耦合，模型能够轻松实现与观测数据的一致性。更重要的是，即便周期尺度低于普朗克尺度（sub-Planckian）且非最小耦合参数仅为量级1（order of one），该场景仍然有效。

Conclusion: 在度规-仿射引力框架下，通过同时引入暴胀子与Nieh-Yan项和Ricci标量的周期非最小耦合，自然暴胀模型可以在亚普朗克周期尺度和较小耦合常数下与观测数据良好吻合，显著扩展了该模型的理论可行性空间。

Abstract: We revisit natural inflation within the framework of metric-affine gravity, considering the impact of a periodic non-minimal coupling between the inflaton and the Nieh-Yan term. Such a term, alone, leads to linear inflation predictions in the strong coupling limit and cannot help to rescue the natural inflation scenario. However, once an analogous non-minimal coupling with the Ricci scalar is added, agreement with data can be easily achieved. Remarkably, the scenario remains viable even with a sub-Planckian periodicity scale and relatively small (order of one) non-minimal couplings.

### [116] [Sharpening the Supersymmetric Axion Weak Gravity Conjecture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22912)
*Muldrow Etheredge,Matthew Reece,Tom Rudelius,Christopher Tudball*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过三种互补方法验证了弦景观（string landscape）中不同轴子扇区（axion sectors）的轴子弱引力猜想（Axion Weak Gravity Conjecture）的具体序一系数边界，并推导出更严格的瞬时子（instanton）边界，例如四维超对称瞬时子满足 $\frac{fS}{|n|}\leq \frac 1{κ_4}\sqrt{\frac{7}{2}}$。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 轴子弱引力猜想（Axion Weak Gravity Conjecture）是约束粒子物理和宇宙学的重要量子引力工具，但其系数长期被视为模糊的序一量级。近期关于轴子虫洞（axion wormholes）的研究提出了一个具体的序一系数，本文旨在通过弦景观中的多种轴子扇区验证该边界。

Method: 采用三种互补的研究方法，对弦景观中不同轴子扇区的边界条件进行系统验证，并在验证过程中进一步推导出更严格的瞬时子边界。

Result: 成功验证了近期提出的具体序一系数边界 $\frac{fS}{|n|} \leq \frac{π}{2 κ_d} \sqrt{\frac{d-1}{d-2}}$，并得到了更严格的约束。例如，四维（4d）超对称瞬时子满足 $\frac{fS}{|n|}\leq \frac 1{κ_4}\sqrt{\frac{7}{2}}$。

Conclusion: 轴子弱引力猜想的序一系数可以精确化为具体数值边界，且超对称扇区中存在更严格的约束。

Abstract: The Axion Weak Gravity Conjecture provides one of the most effective quantum gravity tools for constraining particle physics and cosmology, but it has long been thought of as a slightly fuzzy statement: given an axion with decay constant $f$ there should exist an instanton of charge $n$ and action $S$ with $fS/|n|$ at most an order-one number in Planck units. Recent work related to axion wormholes motivated a specific order-one coefficient, $\frac{fS}{|n|} \leq \fracπ{2 κ_d} \sqrt{\frac{d-1}{d-2}}$. In this work, we verify this bound in various axion sectors across the string landscape using three complementary approaches. In the process, we derive even tighter bounds on instantons in such sectors. For example, we argue that supersymmetric instantons in 4d satisfy the stronger bound of $\frac{fS}{|n|}\leq \frac 1{κ_4}\sqrt{\frac{7}{2}}$.

### [117] [Cuspidal Singularities in Collapsing Domain Walls](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22974)
*Jose J. Blanco-Pillado,Matthew Elley,Francesc Ferrer,Alberto García Martín-Caro,Daniel Jiménez-Aguilar,Oriol Pujolàs,Juan S. Valbuena-Bermúdez*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过解析方法和自适应网格细化场论模拟，研究了封闭畴壁（domain walls）在坍缩过程中形成的两类世界体积奇点（worldvolume singularities），即尖棱奇点（cuspidal edge singularities）和尖点顶点奇点（cuspidal vertex singularities），并证明这些结构是薄壁近似（thin wall approximation）之外的场论模拟中的鲁棒特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 准确描述畴壁网络（domain wall networks）坍缩动力学具有挑战性，通常需要大规模数值模拟。本文旨在通过研究单个封闭畴壁的坍缩，提供一种互补性的解析理解，并与场论模拟结果进行对比验证。

Method: 采用解析方法扩展了先前的薄壁近似分析，并与自适应网格细化（adaptive mesh refinement）场论模拟进行比较。利用Nambu-Goto方程和相对论区域有效的类程函近似（eikonal-like approximation）描述奇点结构，并在全场论模拟中验证其鲁棒性。

Result: 发现坍缩畴壁会普遍形成两类世界体积奇点：一维的尖棱奇点（沿壁面以光速传播有限时间）和瞬时性的尖点顶点奇点（壁面瞬间以光速运动）。两种奇点均能从光滑初始条件产生，遵循奇点理论（singularity theory）的普适模式。这些结构在Nambu-Goto方程、类程函近似及全场论模拟中均得到复现。

Conclusion: 场论模拟中的奇点结构并非薄壁近似的人为产物，而是真实畴壁动力学的鲁棒特征。这些聚焦效应会导致局部高能量密度区域，可能具有重要的唯象学含义。

Abstract: Domain wall networks have attracted renewed interest, particularly in relation to the dynamics of network collapse. Accurately describing this process is challenging and typically requires large scale numerical simulations. Here we adopt a complementary approach by studying the collapse of individual closed domain walls, extending previous thin wall analyses and comparing them with adaptive mesh refinement field theory simulations. Firstly, we show that collapsing domain walls generically develop worldvolume singularities of two types: cuspidal edge singularities, consisting of one dimensional singular edges that propagate along the wall surface at the speed of light for a finite time, and cuspidal vertex singularities, which are spike like and instantaneous events where the wall moves momentarily at the speed of light. Both types of features arise generically from smooth initial conditions, and their formation and evolution follow the universal patterns of singularity theory. We show that these structures are captured both by the Nambu-Goto equations and by an eikonal like approximation valid in the relativistic regime. Furthermore, we demonstrate that the same singular structures are reproduced qualitatively in full field theory simulations, establishing that they are not artifacts of the thin wall approximation but robust features of realistic domain wall dynamics. Naturally, such focusing effects in the field theory simulations result in localized regions of high energy density. We briefly discuss possible phenomenological implications.

</details>

*Vasileios Basiouris*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了理解弦论中有限温度效应如何影响膜紧致化场景的真空结构与稳定性，特别是在大体积场景（LVS）框架下，热力学效应对Kähler模动力学及宇宙学演化的作用尚待系统分析。

Method: 采用微扰方法分析LVS中的有限温度效应，研究热化Kähler模的动力学；利用对Kähler势（Kähler potential）的微扰对数圈修正实现模稳定（moduli stabilization），并通过高阶导数$F^4$项检验真空的鲁棒性。

Result: 确定了最大退紧致温度$T_{\max}$依赖于有效理论中的卷绕圈修正（winding-loop corrections）；模型倾向于高标度暴胀场景，其中重模（heavy modulus）在主导宇宙能量密度之前衰变；$T=0$真空的恢复高度依赖于暴胀后热历史，可能产生反德西特（AdS）真空、亚稳态或稳定的德西特（dS）构型。

Conclusion: 有限温度效应对熵辅助隧穿（entropy-assisted tunneling）及弦景致（string landscape）具有重要影响，热历史决定了真空恢复的最终归宿。

Abstract: We analyze finite-temperature effects in the perturbative Large Volume Scenario (LVS), examining the dynamics of thermalized Kähler moduli and the stability of thermally induced vacua. We determine the maximum decompactification temperature $T_{\max}$, showing its dependence on winding-loop corrections in the effective theory. Moduli stabilization arises from perturbative logarithmic loop corrections to the Kähler potential, with higher-derivative $F^4$ terms used to test vacuum robustness. We derive cosmological implications, including bounds on reheating, and show that the model favors high scale inflationary scenarios with the heavy modulus decaying before dominating the energy density of the universe. We also analyze thermal metastability, demonstrating that the recovery of the $T=0$ vacuum is sensitive to the post-inflationary thermal history, potentially yielding either an AdS vacuum, a metastable phase, or a stable dS configuration. We conclude by briefly discussing the relevance of finite-temperature effects for entropy-assisted tunneling and the broader string landscape.

### [119] [On Thermodynamics of Charged Black Holes, Swampland, and Dark Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23047)
*Saad Eddine Baddis,Adil Belhaj,Hajar Belmahi,Salah Eddine Ennadif*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文受宇宙学常数（cosmological constant）可被视为动力学量的启发，从黑洞热力学（black hole thermodynamics）的新视角出发，建立了特定沼泽地猜想（swampland conjectures）之间的桥梁。通过将视界处的径向度规函数视为状态方程，讨论了结构转变与共存曲线；并借助准静态标量场（quasi-static scalar field）的有效势，连接了弦论（string theory）中的沼泽地猜想。最后，通过卡拉比-丘（Kaluza-Klein）对标量场的诠释，以带电黑洞的热力学途径探讨了暗维度（dark dimension）与暗物质（dark matter）。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将宇宙学常数视为动力学量，并试图从黑洞热力学的新视角出发，将不同的沼泽地猜想联系起来，以探索更深层的理论结构。

Conclusion: 该工作展示了通过黑洞热力学的新视角，可以桥接弦论中的沼泽地猜想，并为暗维度和暗物质的研究提供热力学途径。

Abstract: Inspired by the idea that the cosmological constant can be considered as a dynamical quantity, we present a scenario bridging certain swampland conjectures from a new look at thermodynamics of black holes. Dealing with the radial metric function at the horizon as an equation of state, we discuss structural transitions and coexistence curves. By considering an effective potential with a quasi-static scalar field that could find a place in string theory, we then establish a connection between certain swampland conjectures. Relying on Kaluza Klein interpretations of scalar fields, we approach the dark dimension and dark matter through such a thermodynamic approach to charged black holes.

Abstract: We show that spacetime symmetries on any background give rise to stealth vector fields obeying Proca-type equations supplemented by curvature terms. In particular, this allows one to construct exact Proca hair charged and magnetized rotating black holes in all dimensions. In fact, such a construction is not limited to Killing vector fields and equally works for conformal Killing vectors and hidden symmetries encoded in Killing-Yano tensors.
