### [121] [Counting Degrees of Freedom in Open Effective Theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23375)
*Enrica Lausdei,Enrico Pajer*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出一种从运动方程直接计数自由度数（degrees of freedom）的算法，用于处理非哈密顿（non-Hamiltonian）的开放有效场论（open effective field theories）系统，适用于经典线性化动力学与均匀各向同性背景，并通过引入对偶“超前”方程（advanced equations）或等效的Martin-Siggia-Rose泛函，识别约束（constraints）、规范冗余（gauge redundancies）及随机源的一致性条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开放有效场论中动力学通常是耗散（dissipative）且非哈密顿的，标准哈密顿量与拉格朗日量算法无法直接应用，因此需要发展一种不依赖哈密顿形式、直接从运动方程出发的自由度数计数方法。

Method: 限制在经典线性化动力学与均匀各向同性背景（homogeneous and isotropic backgrounds）下，从运动方程出发，引入一组对偶的“超前”方程（advanced equations）或等价的Martin-Siggia-Rose泛函，以此处理场与方程数目不等的非拉格朗日系统（non-Lagrangian systems），包括含约束和规范冗余的系统。

Result: 算法能够识别约束、规范恒等式（gauge identities）、规范冗余及随机源的一致性条件（consistency conditions）；并证明原场的规范冗余对应于对偶超前方程的规范恒等式，反之亦然。在耦合标量系统、介质中的电磁学及宇宙学相关引力有效理论等例子中进行了验证。

Conclusion: 该算法为研究随机动力学（stochastic dynamics）、非平衡统计系统以及Schwinger-Keldysh路径积分中开放量子系统的半经典极限提供了有用的工具。

Abstract: Open effective field theories provide a systematic framework for describing physical systems interacting with an environment whose microscopic details are unknown, unobservable, or uncalculable. A basic step in constructing any effective field theory is the identification of the relevant degrees of freedom. For open effective theories, however, this step is subtle: their dynamics is generically dissipative and non-Hamiltonian, so the standard Hamiltonian and Lagrangian algorithms are not directly applicable.
  To overcome this limitation, we develop an algorithm to count degrees of freedom directly from the equations of motion. Restricting to classical, linearised dynamics on homogeneous and isotropic backgrounds, our method applies to non-Lagrangian systems with unequal numbers of fields and equations, including systems with constraints and gauge redundancies. As a by-product, our algorithm identifies constraints, gauge identities, gauge redundancies, and consistency conditions on stochastic sources. The central ingredient is the introduction of a dual set of ``advanced'' equations, or equivalently an auxiliary Martin-Siggia-Rose functional. We show that gauge redundancies of the original fields are associated with gauge identities of the dual advanced equations, and vice versa. We illustrate our procedure in examples ranging from coupled scalar systems to electromagnetism in a medium and gravitational effective theories relevant for cosmology. Our results will prove useful in the study of stochastic dynamics, non-equilibrium statistical systems and the semi-classical limit of open quantum systems on the Schwinger-Keldysh path integral.

</details>

We also investigate the behavior of the energy density and linear stability of the solutions. We show that compact vacuumless kinks cannot be obtained in impurity-free canonical models. By considering two distinct impurities, we study the conditions needed to induce compactification. In this scenario, stable half-compact or compact solutions are shown to emerge from the systems.

### [124] [Twirled Perfect Tensor Networks: Computationally covariant holographic tensor networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23670)
*Gurbir Arora,Matthew Headrick,Albion Lawrence,Martin Sasieta,Brian Swingle,Connor Wolfe*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本论文受黑洞内部局部张量网络模型中的"Python's Lunch猜想"（PLC）启发，定义了一类新型张量网络。研究发现PLC对建模引力的张量网络细结构做出隐含假设，使其不具有一般性；随机张量网络缺乏"计算协变性"（computational covariance），而基于"扭曲完美张量"（twirled perfect tensors）构建的网络满足该性质并受PLC值约束，同时兼具完美张量网络与随机张量网络的理想全息特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Python's Lunch猜想（PLC）在短程关联的扩展黑膜态中预测的复杂度低于一般短程关联态的上界，这暗示PLC对张量网络的细结构有特殊假设，需澄清其有效性。

Method: 通过构建随机张量网络（random tensor networks）模型分析python's lunch的复杂度行为，并与PLC预测对照；提出基于"扭曲完美张量"（twirled perfect tensors）的新型张量网络类，系统检验其计算协变性与复杂度特性。

Result: 随机张量网络中指数复杂度通常不受PLC指数控制，差异源于缺乏"计算协变性"（computational covariance）；扭曲完美张量网络满足计算协变性，复杂度受PLC值约束，但仍存在局部后选择（local postselection）带来的离散限制，该限制在引力中似乎不存在。此类网络同时满足完美张量网络和随机张量网络的理想全息性质，例如对任意边界子区域服从格点Ryu-Takayanagi公式。

Conclusion: 扭曲完美张量网络为一类兼具全息特征与可控复杂度的张量网络模型提供了灵活框架，其应用潜力可能超越量子引力范畴。

Abstract: We define a novel class of tensor networks motivated by the Python's Lunch Conjecture (PLC) in local tensor network models of the black hole interior. We start from the observation that, for extended black brane states with short-range correlations, the PLC predicts a complexity that is smaller than the upper bound for generic short-range correlated states. We argue that the PLC makes implicit assumptions about the fine structure of the relevant tensor networks modeling gravity that render them non-generic. We demonstrate this explicitly in random tensor network models of the python's lunch, where the exponential complexity is not generally controlled by the PLC exponent. We trace the difference with the PLC to a lack of "computational covariance" in random tensor networks: while the PLC is motivated by an ability to arbitrarily decompose space into low-complexity units provided certain basic rules are followed, we show that random tensor networks do not generically have this property. We propose another class of tensor networks built from what we call "twirled perfect tensors" that do satisfy the computational covariance property and have a complexity bounded by the PLC value. We still find a discrete limitation from local postselection that appears to be absent in gravity. Moreover, we show that this class of tensor networks combines desirable holographic features of perfect tensor networks and random tensor networks, for example, it obeys a lattice Ryu-Takayanagi formula for arbitrary boundary subregions. Though motivated by holography, these tensor networks provide a flexible framework with potential applications beyond quantum gravity.

Employing Gaussian state methods, we analytically compute the logarithmic negativity and construct closed-form solutions for the localized modes carrying it, called negativity cores. These results deepen our understanding of quantum fields and suggest extensions to higher dimensions and fermionic fields.

### [126] [Thermodynamics and transport in holographic QCD with Gauss-Bonnet corrections](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23834)
*ChenWei Tong,Jie Zhou,YuanXu Wang,Rong-Gen Cai,Song He,Li Li*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在一个包含高斯-博内（Gauss-Bonnet）修正的全息QCD模型中，研究了热力学与输运性质。通过固定模型参数以匹配格点QCD热力学数据，分析了状态方程、相图以及剪切粘度与熵比（η/s）和体粘度与熵比（ζ/s）。发现常耦合下η/s呈单调行为，不满足唯象预期；而引入依赖于膨胀子的耦合后，得到了非单调的η/s和有峰值的ζ/s，同时相图中包含关键端点（critical end point）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在爱因斯-坦麦克斯韦-膨胀子（Einstein–Maxwell–Dilaton）框架中加入高斯-博内（Gauss-Bonnet）修正，构建全息QCD模型；利用最新的格点QCD热力学数据固定模型参数；通过相应的涨落方程分析剪切和体粘度与熵比（η/s和ζ/s）。

Result: 在常高斯-博内耦合下，模型能较好描述状态方程，但η/s在穿越区呈单调行为，不满足唯象预期。当高斯-博内耦合依赖膨胀子（dilaton）时，η/s呈现非单调性，ζ/s出现峰值，同时保持与热力学约束一致；所得相图包含位于唯象相关区域的关键端点（critical end point）。

Conclusion: 引入依赖于膨胀子的高斯-博内耦合能使全息QCD模型同时合理描述热力学与输运性质，并定性地捕捉强相互作用物质在穿越区附近的非单调输运行为。

Abstract: Thermodynamics and transport are investigated in a holographic QCD model that extends the Einstein--Maxwell--Dilaton framework by incorporating Gauss--Bonnet corrections. Model parameters are fixed using state-of-the-art lattice QCD thermodynamics. The analysis then examines the equation of state at zero and finite baryon chemical potential, the phase structure in the temperature and chemical potential plane, as well as the shear and bulk viscosity to entropy ratios, $η/s$ and $ζ/s$, via the corresponding fluctuation equations. For a constant Gauss--Bonnet coupling, the model preserves a reasonable description of the equation of state and generates a temperature-dependent $η/s$, although the resulting profile remains monotonic near the crossover region, which does not satisfy the phenomenological expectation. When the Gauss--Bonnet coupling is allowed to depend on the dilaton, a non-monotonic $η/s$ and a peaked $ζ/s$ are obtained while maintaining agreement with thermodynamic constraints. The resulting phase diagram contains a critical end point in a phenomenologically relevant region.

The off-diagonal components of the higher-dimensional stress tensor become non-Abelian color currents, while the higher-dimensional shear tensor induces shear, bulk-like and vector-dissipative structures in the reduced theory. We derive the map for the equation of state, sound speed, color current, entropy current and first-order transport coefficients. In particular, \[
  η=\ee^{α\varphi}\coshξ\,\heta,\qquad
  τ=η\,\frac{n}{(D-1)(d-1)},\qquad
  κ=η\sinh^2ξ. \] We also spell out the hydrodynamic-frame issue induced by dimensional reduction, discuss the status of the internal rapidity field $ξ$, and give a detailed account of how the second law descends from the parent theory, including the roles of temperature-dependent viscosity, non-unimodular groups and possible choices for $ξ$. The construction should be regarded as a toy model for non-Abelian dissipative hydrodynamics with the potential of paving the way to direct phenomenological model of, for example, quark--gluon plasma.

Motivation: 探索处于不同普适类（universality class）的临界自旋链之间的界面行为，寻找新型共形界面结构，并考察其在里德伯原子阵列（Rydberg atom arrays）中实现的可能性。

Method: 采用缺陷/界面共形场论（defect/interface conformal field theory, DCFT/ICFT）框架，利用非可逆对称性（non-invertible symmetries）和模变换（modular transformations）一致性进行分析，结合缺陷耦合（defect couplings）与缺陷谱（defect spectrum）包括混合边界条件情形，推导可观测量结构。

Result: 发现三重临界伊辛模型（Tricritical Ising model, TIM）与伊辛共形场论（Ising CFT）之间的一种新共形界面（conformal interface）；揭示该界面上出现一种新的涌现W₃手征对称性（emergent W₃ chiral symmetry）模式。

Conclusion: 该发现不仅在理论上拓展了不同普适类临界自旋链间界面的理解，也为里德伯原子阵列中的实验实现提供了明确的、可供检验的预言。

Abstract: We consider interfaces between critical spin-chains in different universality classes, described in the continuum limit by defect/interface conformal field theory (DCFT/ICFT). We find a new conformal interface between the Tricritical Ising (TIM) and the Ising CFT. We also explore the possibility of its experimental realizations in the context of Rydberg atom arrays. Our analysis emphasizes non-invertible symmetries and consistency under modular transformations, and uses defect couplings and the defect spectrum -- including in the case of mixed boundary conditions -- to make sharp experimental predictions. The structure of the observables hinges on a newly discovered pattern of emergent ${W}_3$ chiral symmetry for the Tricritical-Ising/Ising interface.

</details>


### [129] [Not all black holes decohere quantum superpositions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23880)
*Anna Biggs,Stefano Trezzi*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究近极端带电黑洞外部量子系统的退相干现象，发现当黑洞足够接近极端值时，量子引力效应会导致退相干率在晚期消失，且在任何情况下都比半经典理论预期更小，从而增强量子叠加的相干性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨近极端黑洞（near-extremal black holes）在低温下其近视界几何中巨大的量子度规涨落（quantum metric fluctuations）如何影响外部量子系统的退相干行为，以检验量子引力效应对量子相干性的作用机制。

Method: 基于文献中近期讨论的思想实验（thought experiment），该实验中的量子系统为一个制备于空间叠加态（spatial superposition）的带电粒子，通过分析该粒子在近极端黑洞外部的退相干过程进行研究。

Result: 在足够接近极端值的黑洞中，晚期退相干率趋于零；该现象源自量子黑洞谱中的自旋诱导能隙（spin-induced energy gap）。能量高于该能隙时退相干率虽非零，但仍低于半经典预期，因此量子引力效应始终增强叠加态的相干性。

Conclusion: 近极端黑洞的量子引力效应可抑制甚至消除外部带电量子系统的退相干，表现为对量子相干性的保护而非破坏作用，这与半经典图像形成鲜明对比。

Abstract: We study the decoherence induced by near-extremal charged black holes on quantum systems in their exterior. Specifically, we analyze a thought experiment recently discussed in the literature, where the quantum system is a charged particle prepared in a spatial superposition. Near-extremal black holes are known to exhibit large quantum metric fluctuations of the near-horizon geometry at low temperatures. We show that, at late times, if the black hole is sufficiently close to extremality, these quantum gravity effects make the decoherence rate vanish. This phenomenon is due to a spin-induced energy gap in the quantum black hole spectrum. For energies above the gap, the decoherence rate becomes nonzero, but is still suppressed relative to semiclassical expectations, so these quantum gravity effects always enhance the coherence of the superposition.

</details>


### [130] [Heterotic Strings on Enriques Surfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23886)
*Arata Ishige,Elisa Iris Marieni*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了杂弦（heterotic strings）在恩里克斯曲面（Enriques surfaces）上的轨形紧化（orbifold compactifications），分类了E8×E8与Spin(32)/Z2格点上的不等价平移向量（shift vectors），分析了模型的光谱，并指出这些模型可解释为十维非超对称杂弦在恩里克斯曲面上的紧化。特定平移类中，继承自父理论（parent theories）的与模无关的快子（moduli-independent tachyons）会被投影掉。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索杂弦在恩里克斯曲面上的轨形紧化模型结构，并理解其与非超对称杂弦紧化之间的深层联系。

Method: 采用轨形紧化方法，对E8×E8和Spin(32)/Z2两种格点的不等价平移向量进行分类，并计算模型的光谱（light spectrum）。

Result: 证明了这类模型等价于十维非超对称杂弦在恩里克斯曲面上的紧化；在特定平移类中，源自父理论的与模无关的快子被投影移除。

Conclusion: 恩里克斯曲面上的轨形紧化提供了一种从非超对称杂弦出发构造一致性模型的有效途径，并通过平移向量的选择实现了快子（tachyon）的消除。

Abstract: We study orbifold compactifications of heterotic strings on Enriques surfaces. We classify the inequivalent shift vectors for both the E8\times E8 and Spin(32)/Z2 lattices, and analyse the light spectrum of the resulting models. We show that these models can be interpreted as compactifications of ten-dimensional non-supersymmetric heterotic strings on Enriques surfaces. For certain classes of shifts, the moduli-independent tachyons inherited from the parent theories are projected out.

</details>


### [131] [What to do with a Ricci-flat Calabi--Yau metric?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23900)
*Per Berglund,Tristan Hübsch,Vishnu Jejjala*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出利用里奇平坦卡拉比-丘度量的数值近似，将弦论紧致化研究从拓扑与全纯数据拓展至度量和埃尔米特-杨-米尔斯丛数据，并系统阐述这一方向在物理和数学领域带来的新机遇，作为未来研究的路线图。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的弦论紧致化研究长期局限于拓扑和全纯不变量，而度量和与之关联的埃尔米特-杨-米尔斯（Hermitian Yang–Mills）丛数据因计算困难被忽略；然而这些非全纯数据对于确定物质Kähler度量、规范化的Yukawa耦合、Kaluza–Klein谱、阈值效应、软项等四维有效作用的非全纯成分至关重要，因此需要发展数值方法填补这一空白。

Method: 通过数值近似方法计算里奇平坦（Ricci-flat）的卡拉比-丘（Calabi–Yau）度量，并进一步扩展到相关的埃尔米特-杨-米尔斯丛数据，从而为异质紧致化（heterotic compactifications）和更广泛的几何物理问题提供定量输入。

Result: 该数值方法使得模稳定化、α'修正背景、de Sitter模型构建、轴子物理、沼泽地距离检验（swampland distance tests）以及内蕴几何随时空变化的紧致化等课题获得定量分析手段；同时为特殊拉格朗日子流形、SYZ纤维化、镜像对称、校准几何、度量退化、里奇平坦度量在纤维上的限制等长期数学问题提供了计算途径。

Conclusion: 数值卡拉比-丘几何提供了一条将物理与数学中此前难以触及的非全holomorphic问题纳入可计算框架的路线，作者将其作为未来工作的路线图呈现。

Abstract: Numerical approximations to Ricci-flat Calabi--Yau metrics make it possible to move beyond the topological and holomorphic data that have traditionally dominated explicit string compactifications. This article explains what new physics and mathematics become accessible once the metric, and eventually the associated Hermitian Yang--Mills bundle data, can be computed. In heterotic compactifications, such data are needed to determine matter Kähler metrics, canonically normalized Yukawa couplings, Kaluza--Klein spectra, threshold effects, soft terms, and other non-holomorphic ingredients of the four-dimensional effective action. More broadly, numerical Calabi--Yau geometry provides quantitative input for moduli stabilization, $α'$-corrected backgrounds, de~Sitter model building, axion physics, swampland distance tests, and compactifications in which the internal geometry varies over spacetime. Geometric data permit a computational approach to long-standing mathematical questions involving special Lagrangian submanifolds, SYZ fibrations, mirror symmetry, calibrated geometry, metric degeneration, restrictions of Ricci-flat metrics to fibers, and the search for analytic or semi-analytic structures. We present these directions as a roadmap for future work.

</details>

### [132] [Approximate controllability in small times of bilinear Schr{ö}dinger equations with magnetic drift](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23665)
*Eugenio Pozzoli*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究了双线性薛定谔方程（bilinear Schrödinger equations）的小时间近似可控性（small-time approximate controllability），其中漂移项为磁薛定谔算子（magnetic Schrödinger operator），控制项为电势（electric potential）。在两种情形下证明了该性质：一是$\mathbb{R}^d$中，控制项含二次型和额外有界电势，漂移项含均匀磁场；二是在$\mathbb{R}^d$或$\mathbb{T}^d$中，控制电势支撑在有限个埃尔米特或傅里叶本征函数上，漂移项含任意可微磁势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双线性薛定谔方程的可控性问题是量子控制理论中的核心课题，小时间近似可控性决定了系统能否在任意短时间内在状态空间中近似达到任意目标态。本文旨在拓展已有结果，覆盖更一般的磁势和更灵活的控制函数形式。

Method: 采用分析框架，分别处理两种场景：场景(i)利用均匀磁场下二次型加上有界电势的控制结构；场景(ii)利用有限个埃尔米特或傅里叶本征函数支撑的电势控制，并结合可微磁势的漂移项。证明基于小时间近似可控性的理论工具。

Result: 证明了在两种设定下双线性薛定谔方程均具有小时间近似可控性：第一种设定在$\mathbb{R}^d$中，控制电势包含二次型和额外的有界电势，漂移项含均匀磁场；第二种设定在$\mathbb{R}^d$或环面（torus）$\mathbb{T}^d$上，控制电势支撑在有限个本征函数上，漂移项含任意可微磁势。

Conclusion: 本文表明，对于具有磁薛定谔算子的双线性系统，在适当的控制电势条件下，小时间近似可控性在多种空间结构和磁场配置下均可实现，为量子系统的快速操控提供了理论依据。

Abstract: We study the small-time approximate controllability of bilinear Schr{ö}dinger equations, where the drift is a magnetic Schr{ö}dinger operator and the control is an electric potential. We prove this property in two circumstances: (i) in $\mathbb{R}^d$, with a quadratic and an additional generic bounded electric potential in the control, and with a uniform magnetic field in the drift; (ii) in $\mathbb{R}^d$ or $\mathbb{T}^d$, with control electric potentials supported on a finite number of Hermite or Fourier eigenfunctions, and with any differentiable magnetic potential in the drift.

</details>

### [133] [Full-Scattering-Matrix Deterministic Phonon Boltzmann Transport Simulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23005)
*Y. Sungtaek Ju*

Main category: physics.comp-ph

TL;DR: 本文发现声子玻尔兹曼输运方程（BTE）在弛豫时间近似（RTA）下忽略了散射矩阵的非对角元，而实际的非平衡声子分布仅占据模式空间的一个低维子空间，且散射算子的主导奇异模与该子空间对齐，从而可以在保持输运精度的前提下对散射矩阵进行截断。基于此，作者开发了一个计算高效的3D BTE求解器，并在纳米鳍式场效应晶体管（FinFET）结构中揭示了RTA温度预测的几何无关乘性修正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 弛豫时间近似（relaxation-time approximation, RTA）下的声子玻尔兹曼输运方程（Boltzmann transport equation, BTE）忽略了散射矩阵的非对角元（off-diagonal elements），这些非对角元编码了模间能量再分布（intermode energy redistribution）。本文旨在克服这一根本限制，在包含完整散射矩阵的前提下开发高效的三维BTE求解器，以支持弹道与准弹道声子输运区间的精确研究。

Method: 作者发现了两个关键结构特性：1) 非平衡声子分布在模式空间中仅占据一个极低维子空间（low-dimensional subspace），不受模式总数影响；2) 散射算子的主导奇异模（leading singular modes）与该输运活性子空间（transport-active subspace）选择性对齐。基于此，即使截断引入较大的范数误差（norm error），输运误差仍可忽略不计。进一步结合声子流算子（streaming operator）的模式对角特性，构建了混合架构（hybrid architecture）以实现高效求解。

Result: 声子入散射矩阵（in-scattering matrix）在全局上不可压缩（incompressible），需要接近满秩才能获得有用的Frobenius精度，且不可压缩性随布里渊区（Brillouin zone）细化而加剧。然而，基于上述子空间结构进行的截断在输运精度上几乎无损。将该求解器应用于模拟鳍式场效应晶体管（fin field-effect transistor, FinFET）的纳米结构时，可量化RTA预测温升的一个几何无关乘性修正（geometry-independent multiplicative correction）。

Conclusion: 本文的理论工作与所开发的BTE求解器有助于在弹道及准弹道声子输运区（ballistic and quasi-ballistic phonon transport regime）开展严谨的声子输运研究，并支持对相关器件与结构的系统化设计。

Abstract: Solutions to the phonon Boltzmann transport equation under the relaxation-time approximation (RTA) are fundamentally limited in that they do not account for the off-diagonal elements of the scattering matrix, which encode intermode energy redistribution. We find that the phonon in-scattering matrix is globally incompressible, requiring nearly its full rank for any useful Frobenius accuracy. The incompressibility worsens as the Brillouin zone is refined. We show that, despite this difficulty, one can develop a computationally efficient 3D BTE solver incorporating the complete scattering matrix by leveraging our two structural discoveries: the non-equilibrium phonon distribution inhabits a remarkably low-dimensional subspace of mode space regardless of how many phonon modes exist, and the leading singular modes of the scattering operator align selectively with this transport-active subspace. Consequently, truncation incurs negligible transport error even under large norm error. The phonon streaming operator's mode-diagonal character further motivates a hybrid architecture that exploits these two properties. When applied to nanoscale structures emulating a fin field-effect transistor, our BTE solver quantifies a geometry-independent multiplicative correction to the temperature rise predicted under RTA. Our theoretical work and resulting BTE solver help enable rigorous study of phonon transport and systematic design of devices and structures in the ballistic and quasi-ballistic phonon transport regime.

</details>
